prathamadvitīyadhyānayo sukhasaumanasyopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate / tṛtīyadhyāne sukhopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate
# bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa la ni bde ba dang yid bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no / / gsum pa la ni bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
tadūrdhvamupekṣayaiva saṃprayujyate
# de yan chad du ni btang snyoms kho na dang mtshungs par ldan no /
yathā mānastathā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ antagrāhadṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca
# nga rgyal ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang lta ba mchog tu 'dzin par lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa yang de bzhin no /
mithyādṛṣṭiḥ kāmadhātau daurmanasyasaumanasyopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate
# log par lta ba ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no; /
rūpadhātāvārupyadhātau ca yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate
# gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
vicikitsā kāmadhātau dauramanasyopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate
# the tshom ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
rūpadhātāvārūpyadhātau ca yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate / avidyā dvividhā
# gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
saṃprayuktā asāmānyā ca / sarvakleśasaṃprayogataḥ saṃprayuktā avidyā yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate
# ma rig pa ni nyon mongs pa thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan pa yin pas gang na tshor ba gang yod pa de dang der mtshungs par ldan pa can zhes bya'o /
āsāmānyā avidyā kāmadhātau daurmanasyopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate
# ma rig pa ma 'dres pa gang yin pa de ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
tadūrdhvadhātau yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate
# de yan chad du ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
kathaṃ sarvakleśā upekṣayā saṃprayujyante
# ci'i phyir nyon mongs pa thams cad btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan zhe na /
sarvakleśānāmaudāsīnyamāgamyāstagamanatāmupādāya
# tha mal par 'dug pa la brten nas nub par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
api khalu rāgaḥ kāmadhātau ṣaḍvijñānakāyikaḥ / yathā rāgastathā pratigho 'vidyā ca
# 'dod chags ni 'dod pa'i khams na rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug dang mtshungs par ldan no / / 'dod chags ji lta bar khong khro ba dang ma rig pa yang de bzhin no /
rāgo rūpadhātau caturvijñānakāyikāḥ
# gzugs kyi khams na ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs bzhin dang mtshungs par ldan no /
ārūpyadhātau manovijñānakāyikaḥ / yathā rāgastathā avidyā / māno dṛṣṭirvicikitsā ca sarvatra manovijñānakāyikāḥ / api khalu rāgaḥ pratigho mānaśca kāmadhātau vastvekadeśapravṛttikāḥ
# gzugs med pa'i khams na ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang mtshungs par ldan no / / 'dod chags ji lta bar ma rig pa yang de bzhin no / / nga rgyal dang lta ba dang the tshom ni thams cad du yang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang mtshungs par ldan no / / 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal ni 'dod pa'i khams na dngos po'i phyogs gcig la 'jug go /
kāmadhātuvad rūpadhātāvārūpyadhātāvapi śiṣṭāḥ kleśāḥ sarvatra sarvavastu pravṛttikāḥ
# 'dod pa'i khams na ji ltar bar gzugs kyi khams dang gzugs med pa'i khams na yang de bzhin no / / lhag ma rnams ni thams cad du yang dngos po mtha' dag la 'jug go /
nikāyaḥ katamaḥ / dvau kleśanikāyau / darśanaprahātavyanikāyo bhāvanāprahātavyanikāyaśca
# ris kyis ji lta bu zhe na / / nyon mongs pa'i ris gnyis te / / mthong bas spang bar bya ba dang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'o /
darśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ punaścaturvidhaḥ / duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ samudayadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ / nirodhadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ mārgadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaśca / kāmadhātau duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyā daśa kleśāḥ / duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyavat samudayadarśanaprahātavyāḥ nirodhadarśanaprahātavyā mārgadarśanaprahātavyāśca
# 'dod pa'i khams na sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni bcu'o / / sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba ji lta bar kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams kyang de bzhin no / / gzugs kyi khams na sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni dgu'o / / sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams ji lta bar kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams kyang de bzhin no /
rūpadhātau duḥkhādicaturvidhadarśanaprahātavyāḥ pratyekaṃ navakleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham / rūpadhātuvadārūpyadhātāvapi / evaṃ ca darśanaprahātavyakleśanikāyā dvādaśādhikaṃ śataṃ kleśāḥ / kāmadhātau bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ ṣaṭkleśāḥ / sahajā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ antaprāhadṛṣṭiḥ rāgaḥ pratigho māno 'vidyā ca / rūpadhātau bhāvanāprahātavyāḥ pañca kleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham
# gzugs kyi khams na ji lta bar gzugs med pa'i khams na'ang de bzhin te / / de dag mdor bsdu na nyon mongs pa brgya rtsa bcu gnyis ni mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i ris so / / 'dod pa'i khams na bsgom pas spang bar bya ba drug ste / / 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba lhan cig skyes pa dang 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa'o / / gzugs kyi khams na khong khro ba ma gtogs par lnga'o /
rūpadhātuvadārūpyadhātāvapi / evaṃ ca bhāvanāprahātavyanikāyāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ kleśāḥ
# gzugs kyi khams na ji lta bar gzugs med pa'i khams na'ang de bzhin te / / de dag mdor bsdu na bcu drug ni bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i ris so /
prahāṇaṃ katamat
# spong bas ji ltar bu zhe na /
tathā paryāyaprahāṇaṃ tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam / tasmāt pratilambhāt prahāṇam
# ji ltar spong ba dang yid la byed pa ci 'dra ba dang gang zhig gang las spong ba'o /
tathā paryāyaprahāṇaṃ katamat / parijñānataḥ parivarjanataḥ pratipakṣalābhataśca
# ji ltar spong zhe na / / yongs su shes pa dang yongs su spong ba dang gnyen po rnyed pas so /
parijñānaṃ katamat / tannidānavastuparijñānam svabhāvaparijñānam ādīnavaparijñānaṃ ca
# yongs su shes pa gang zhe na / / de'i gzhi'i dngos po yongs su shes pa dang ngo bo nyid yongs su shes pa dang nyes dmigs yongs su shes pa'o /
parivarjanaṃ katamat
# yongs su spong ba gang zhe na /
tatkālotpannasyānādānam
# 'byung bar gyur pa dang du mi len pa'o /
pratipakṣalābhaḥ katamaḥ
# gnyen po rnyed pa gang zhe na /
anutpannasyānutpādata utpannasya varjanato vā pratipakṣa lābhamārgaḥ / tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam
# ma skyes pa spang ba'i phyir lam rnyed pa gang yin pa'o / / yid la byed pa ci 'dra bas spong zhe na /
kīdṛśena manaskāreṇa kiṃ prajahāti
# 'dres pa la dmigs pas spong ste /
asaṃbhinnālambanena manaskāreṇa sarvadharmā anātmāna iti paśyati / anityākārā iti kleśān prajahāti / anityākāra parikarmataḥ
# chos thams cad bdag med pa'o zhes bya ba'o / / mi rtag pa'i rnam pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa gang yin pa de dag ni bdag med pa'i rnam pa'i yongs su sbyong bar byed pa'o /
tasmāt pratilambhāt prahāṇam
# gang zhig gang las spong zhe na /
kasmāt pratilambhāt prajahāti
# 'das pa ni 'gags pa'i phyir ma yin no /
nātītāt niruddhataḥ / nānāgatāt anutpannataḥ / na pratyutpannāt asahabhāvataḥ
# ma 'ongs pa ni ma byung ba'i phyir ma yin no / / de ltar byung ba ni lam dang mnyam du mi 'jug pa'i phyir ma yin no /
kevalaṃ kleśadauṣṭhulyapratilambhāt prajahātīti prahāṇam
# 'on kyang nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len gang la yod pa de las spong ngo /
yathā yathā dauṣṭhulyamutpadyate tathā tathā pratipakṣa utpadyate yathā yathā pratipakṣa utpadyate tathā tathā dauṣṭhulyanirodhaḥ / samaṃ samam
# gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa gang gi gnyen po gang byung ba gnyen po'i rnam pa de 'byung ba dang gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa de 'gog pa ni mnyam pas mnyam ste /
yathā  loke jyotirutpadyate tamaśca nirudhyate / tadvisaṃyogato yadānāgatakleśo 'nutpannadhamaṣu avatiṣṭhate tat prahāṇamucyate
# snang ba dang mun pa 'byung ba dang 'gog pa bzhin no / / gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa dang bral bas ma 'ongs pa na nyon mongs pa mi skye ba'i chos can du gnas pa de ni spong ba'o /
kleśādhipateyaṃ karma katamat / cetanā karma cetayitvā karma ca / sarvaṃ karmalakṣaṇaṃ nāma / punaḥ karma pañcavidham / upalabdhikarma kāritrakarma vyavasāyakarma pariṇatikarma prāptikarma ca
# las gang zhe na / / sems pa'i las dang bsams pa'i las te / / las kyi mtshan nyid mdor bsdus pa'o / / yang las rnam pa lnga ste / / dmigs pa'i las dang byed pa'i las dang rtsol ba'i las dang bsgyur ba'i las dang 'thob pa'i las so /
asmiṃstvarthe yad bhūyasā vyavasāyakarmābhipretam / cetanākarma katamat
# skabs 'dir phal cher rtsol ba'i las su 'dod do / / sems pa'i las gang zhe na /
puṇyakarma apuṇyakarma āniṃjyakarma ca / cetayitvā karma katamat
# sems mngon par 'du byed pa yid kyi las te / / bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'o / / bsams pa'i las gang zhe na /
kāyakarma vākkarma manaskarma ca
# lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las so /
tāni trīṇi kāyavāṅmanaskarmāṇi akuśalāni kuśalāni ca
# lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las de yang dge ba dang mi dge ba'o /
akuśalāni katamāni daśākuśalakarmapathāḥ / prāṇātipātaḥ adattādānam kāmamithyācāraḥ mṛṣāvādaḥ piśunavāk paruṣavāk saṃbhinnapralāpaḥ abhidyā vyāpādaḥ mithyādṛṣṭiśca
# mi dge ba ni mi dge ba'i las kyi lam bcu ste / / 'di lta ste / / srog gcod pa dang ma byin par len pa dang 'dod pa la log par g yem pa dang brdzun du smra ba dang phra ma dang tshig rtsub po dang tshig kyal ba dang brnab sems dang gnod sems dang log par lta ba'o /
kuśalāni katamāni / daśa kuśalakarmāpathāḥ
# dge ba ni dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams te /
prāṇātipātād viratiḥ adattādānādviratiḥ kāmamithyācārādviratiḥ mṛṣāvādādviratiḥ piśunavāco viratiḥ paruṣavāco viratiḥ saṃbhinnapralāpādviratiḥ anabhidhyā avyāpādaḥ samyagdṛṣṭiśca / apica prāṇātipātādīnāṃ yathāyogaṃ pañca lakṣaṇaprabhedāḥ / vastutaḥ āśayataḥ prayogataḥ kleśataḥ niṣṭhāgamanataśca / yaduktaṃ sūtre cetanākarma
# 'di lta ste / / srog gcod pa spong ba nas tshig kyal ba'i bar du spong ba dang brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa dang yang dag par lta ba'o / / srog gcod pa la sogs pa rnams kyi mtshan nyid ni gzhi dang bsam pa dang sbyor ba dang nyon mongs pa dang zin par byas pas kyang rig par bya'o / / sems pa las gyur pa'i las zhes gang 'byung ba la sems pa las gyur ba gang zhe na /
katamāni cetanākarmāṇi parājñaptisaṃcetanīyatākarma paramasaṃjñaptisaṃcetatīyatākarma avijñāyasaṃcetanīyatākarma mūlābhiniveśasacetanīyatākarma viparyāsasaṃcetanīyatākarma ca / teṣu mūlābhiniveśasaṃcetanīyatākarma viparyāsaṃcetana yatā karma ca / teṣu mūlābhiniveśasaṃcetanīyatā karmaviparyāsasaṃcetanīyatākarmabhyāṃ yadi kṛtaṃ bhavatyupacitaṃ ca na nāsya vipākaḥ pratisaṃvedyate
# gzhan gyis bsgo ba sems pa las gyur pa dang gzhan gyis gsol ba btab pa sems pa las gyur pa dang mi shes pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang rtsa ba la mngon par zhen pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang phyin ci log gi sems pa las gyur ba'o / / de la rtsa ba las mngon par zhen pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang phyin ci log gi sems pa las gyur pa'i las byas shing bsags pa'i rnam par smin pa ni myong bar mi 'gyur ba ma yin no /
kṛtaṃ samudācārasamutthāpitam
# las kyi byed pa ni kun tu spyod pa'o /
upacitaṃ ca vāsanā samupacitam
# bsags pa ni bag chags 'phel ba'o /
yadūktaṃ sūtre niyatavedanīyaṃ karma iti / katame niyaptāḥ karmakiyāniyamaḥ vipākapatisaṃvedanāniyamaḥ avasthāniyamaśca
# myong bar nges pa'i las zhes gang 'byung ba las nges pa gang zhe na / / las byed par nges pa dang rnam par smin pa myong bar nges pa dang dus nges pa'o /
tanna daśānāmakuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalaṃ triṣu apāyeṣu
# de la mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni ngan song rnams su'o /
mṛdūmadhyādhimātrāṇāṃ tiryakpretanarakeṣu vipākaḥ
# rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni so so dang mthun par mi'i lus dang yongs su gzungs ba mi 'byor ba'o /
nipyandaphalaṃ pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇa manuṣyeṣūpanannānā mātmabhāvaparigrahayorvipattiḥ / adhipatiphalaṃ pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇaiva vāhyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ vipattiḥ / yathoktaṃ sūtre
# bdag po'i 'bras bu ni so so dang mthun pa nyid du phyi'i dngos po mi 'byor ba'o / / de yang mdo las ji skad du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du'o /
daśānāṃ kuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalaṃ devamanuṣyamatiṣūpapadyamānānāṃ deveṣu manuṣyeṣu vā vipākaḥ
# rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni de dag nyid du so so dang mthun par lus dang yongs su gzung ba phun sum tshogs pa'o /
niṣyandaphalaṃ tadāyataneṣu pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇa ātmābhāvaparigrahayoḥ saṃpattirabhinirvarttate / adhipattiphalaṃ tadāyataneṣu pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇaiva vāhyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ saṃpattirabhinirvarttate / kuśalānāmakuśalānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ sugatau durgatau ca vipāko 'bhinirvarttate
# bdag po'i 'bras bu ni de dag nyid du so so dang mthun pa'i phyi'i dngos po phun sum tshogs pa'o / / dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyis ni bde 'gro dang ngan 'gror skye ba 'phen pa dang yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i las su rig par bya'o / / 'phen pa ni gang gis rnam par smin pa 'phen pa'o /
taccākṣepakeṇa karmaṇā paripūrakeṇa ca karmaṇā
# yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ni gang gis skyes pa na 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa myong ba'o /
ākṣepakaṃ karma katamat / yena phala vipāko 'bhinirvarttate
# las gcig gis lus gcig 'phen par byed pa'i las kyang yod / / las gcig gis lus du ma 'phen par byed pa'i las kyang yod /
paripūrakaṃ karma katamat
# las du mas lus gcig 'phen pa'i las kyang yod /
yenopapanna iṣṭāniṣṭaphalaṃ vedayate
# las du mas lus du ma 'phen pa'i las kyang yod do /
yena ekena karmaṇā ekamātmabhavanākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā ekamātmabhāvamākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā anekamātmabhāvamākṣipati vā / ekaḥ sattvo 'nekena karmaṇā samanvāgataḥ
# las mang po dang po dang ldan pa'i sems can ji ltar rim gyis rnam par smin pa myong bar 'gyur zhe na / / de la gang shin tu lci bar gyur pa de thog mar rnam par smin par 'gyur ro /
tatra vipākaphalavedanāyāḥ kaḥ kramaḥ
# yang na 'chi ba'i dus na gang mngon du gyur pa'o /
kāye yad audārikaṃ pūrvaṃ pacyate cyutikāle pratyupasthitaṃ vā pūrvaṃ bahulīkāratāṃ gataṃ vā atrasamācaritaṃ vā / tadvipākaḥ pūrvaṃ pacyate / yaduktaṃ sūtre trividhaṃ karma puṇyakarma apuṇya karma āniṃjyakarma ca / puṇyakarma katamat
# yang na gang goms par gyur pa'o / / yang na gang thog mar spyad pa de thog ma nyid du rnam par smin par 'gyur ro / / bsod nams kyi las dang bsod nams ma yin pa'i las dang mi g yo ba'i las zhes gang 'byung ba la / / bsod nams gang zhe na /
kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ kuśalaṃ karma
# gang 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'o /
apuṇyakarma katamat / akuśalaṃ karma
# bsod nams ma yin pa gang zhe na / / gang mi dge ba'o /
āniṃjyakarma katamat
# mi g yo ba'i las gang zhe na /
rūpārūpyapratisaṃyuktaṃ kuśalaṃ karma
# gang gzugs dang gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'o /
yaduktaṃ sūtre avidyālambanāḥ saṃskārāḥ puṇyāniṃjyā apuṇyāniṃjyāśceti
# ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'i 'du byed rnams so zhes gang gsungs pa de la /
katame  puṇyāniṃjyā avidyālambanāḥ saṃskārā utpadyante / dvividhaḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ
# ji ltar na bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'i 'du byed rnams ma rig pa'i rkyen las byung ba yin zhe na / / rmongs pa ni gnyis te /
phalavipākasaṃmūḍhaḥ tattvārthasaṃmūḍhaśca
# 'bras bu rnams par smin pa la rmongs pa dang de kho na'i don la rmongs pa'o /
phalavipākasaṃmūḍhasyāpuṇyāḥ saṃskārāḥ
# 'bras bu rnams par smin pa la rmongs pa'i ni mi dge ba'i 'du byed rnams 'byung ngo /
tattvārthasaṃmūḍhasya puṇyāniṃjyāḥ saṃskārāḥ
# de kho na'i don la rmongs pa'i ni bsod nams dang mi g yo ba rnams so /
prāṇātipātasya karmapathasya lobhadveṣamohaiḥ prayogaḥ
# srog gcod pa la ni chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gis sbyor te /
dveṣeṇaiva niṣṭhā / prāṇātipātavat paruṣavāgavyāpādayorapi karmapathayoḥ
# zhes sdang gis mthar phyin par byed do / / srog gcod pa la ji ltar bar ngag rtsub po dang gnod sems la yang de bzhin no /
adattādānasya karmapathasya lobhadveṣamohaiḥ prayogaḥ
# ma byin par len pa la ni 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gis sbyor te /
lobhenaiva niṣṭhā
# chags pas mthar phyin par byed do /
adattādānavat kāmamithyācārābhidhyayoḥ karmapathayoḥ
# ma byin par len pa la ji lta bar 'dod pa la log par g yem pa dang brnab sems la yang de bzhin no /
mṛṣāvādasya karmapathasya lobhadveṣamohaiḥ prayogaḥ
# brdzun du smra ba la ni chags pa dang zhes sdang dang gti mug gis sbyor te /
trayāṇāmanyatamena niṣṭhā / mṛṣāvādavat saṃbhinnapralāpapiśunavācoḥ karmapathayoḥ
# gsum po dag las gang yang rung bas mthar phyin par byed do / / brdzun du smra ba la ji lta bar phra ma dang tshig kyal pa la yang de bzhin no /
mithyādṛṣṭeḥ karmapathasya rāgadveṣamohaiḥ prayogaḥ
# log par lta ba la ni chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gis sbyor te /
mohenaiva niṣṭhā / yaduktaṃ sūtre sādhāraṇaṃ karma asādhāraṇaṃ karma valavatkarma durvalaṃ karma ca
# gti mug gis mthar phyin par byed do / / las thun mong pa zhes kyang 'byung / / las thun mong ma yin pa zhes kyang 'byung /
sādhāraṇaṃ karma katamat
# stobs dang ldan pa zhes kyang 'byung /
yatkarma bhājanaloke nānāvidhaṃ vikalpaṃ karoti / asādhāraṇaṃ karma katamat / yatkarma sattvaloke nānavidhaṃ vikalpaṃ karoti
# mthu chung ba zhes kyang 'byung ba la / / thun mong pa gang zhe na / / gang snod kyi 'jig rten rnams par 'byed pa'o / / thun mong ma yin pa gang zhe na /
api ca sattvānāmanyonyādhipateyaṃ karmāpi
# gang sems can gyi 'jig rten rnam par 'byed pa'o /
yena karmabalena sattvānāmanyonyādhipatipratyayaḥ proktaḥ / teṣāmanyonyādhipatibalatastadapyucyate sādhāraṇaṃ karma
# yang gang gis sems can rnams kyi phan tshun gyi dbang gis byung ba zhes brjod pa sems can rnams kyi phan tshun gyi dbang gis 'byung ba'i las kyang yod de /
yataḥ sūtre uktam / yathā sattvānāmānyaiḥ sattvaiḥ saha anyonyaṃ darśanādikaṃ nopabhogo nopalabdhiḥ / balavatkarma katamat / pratipakṣabalavatpugdalasya saṃcetanīyamakuśalaṃ karma / pratipakṣavalaviskāmbhaṇena vedanīyanarakakarmapravṛtteḥ dṛṣṭadharmavedanāyāḥ pariniṣpādanaṃ dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyanarakakarmapravṛtteranutpādaḥ
# 'di ltar gang sems can gzhan rnams dang phan tshun du lta ba la sogs pas nye bar spyod par mi 'gyur ba'i sems can de ni mong pa ma yin no / / stobs dang ldan pa'i las gang zhe na / / gnyen po'i stobs can gyi gang zag gi sems pa las gyur pa'i las mi dge ba gang yin pa de ni gnyen po'i stobs bskyed pas / / gang sems can dmyal ba myong bar 'gyur ba de mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba'am /
yena tatkarma balavadityucyate / prātipakṣikakarmabalavataḥ sarvaṃ saṃcetanīyaṃ kuśalaṃ karma balavadityucyate
# gang mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba de myong bar mi 'gyur ba ste / / de ltar na gnyen po las byung ba'i las dang sems pa las gyur ba'i dge ba'i las thams cad kyang stobs dang ldan pa'o /
tatkarma niśrityoktaṃ bhagavatā mamāryaśrāvakā apramāṇavaipulyakarmaṇi cittaṃ kuśalaṃ paribhāvayanti abhisaṃskṛte sapramāṇe karmaṇi nākṣipanti nāvasthāpayanti na parihāpayanti tatsaṃkhyāte / yadapi pratipakṣadurbalapugdalasya saṃcetanīyamakuśalaṃ karma tadapi kuśalātkarmaṇo  balavadityucyate / yat punaḥ saṃcetanīyaṃ karma niyatavipākamaprahīṇamaparijñātaṃ tad balavat karma ityucyate / tanmanasi nidhāyoktaṃ sarvaṃ ca kuśalākuśalaṃ karma niyatavipākamāryamārgeṇa prahīṇaṃ balavat karma ityucyate / yadapi kāmapratisaṃyuktamakuśalaṃ karma yadapi pūrvamabhyastaṃ yadapi padasthaṃ yadapyasādhyamabhisaṃskṛtaṃ karma aparinirvāṇadharmataḥ tadapi prakṛtyā balavat karma ityucyate / kṣetrato 'pi cittābhisaṃskārato 'pi balavat karma veditavyam / punarnavabhirākārairbalavat karma veditavyam
# 'di las dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis 'phags pa nyan thos sems shin tu bsgoms pa tshad med pas rgya che ba la / / gang tshad du byas pa'i las nges de khrid par mi byed do / / de la de dag gnas par mi bya'o / / des de bgrang bar mi 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so / / gnyen po'i mthu chung ba'i gang zag gi sems pa las gyur pa'i las mi dge ba gang yin pa de dang gang yang sems pa las gyur pa'i las rnam par smin par nges pa de ma spangs ba dang yongs su ma shes pa de ni stobs dang ldan pa yin te / / 'di ni 'dir dgongs pa'o / / yang 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i mi dge ba gang yin pa dang gang sngon goms par byas pa dang gnas la gnas pa dang yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can rnams kyi bsgrub tu med pa gang yin pa da ni rang bzhin gyis stobs dang ldan pa yin no / / zhing dang sems kyi mngon par 'du byed pas kyang stobs dang ldan pa'i las su rig par bya'o / / yang rnam pa dgus stobs dang ldan pa'i las su rig par bya ste /
tadyathā kṣetrataḥ vastutaḥ svabhāvataḥ āśrayataḥ manasikārataḥ āśayataḥ sahāyataḥ bahulīkārataḥ bāhujanyataśca
# zhing dang dngos po dang ngo bo nyid dang gzhi bo dang yid la byed pa dang bsam pa dang grogs dang lan mang du byed pa dang skye bo mang pos kyang stobs dang ldan pa ste /
tadviparyeṇa durbalaṃ karma / bhagavatoktaṃ ya evaṃ vadedyathāyaṃ puruṣapugdalaḥ karma karotyupacinoti tathā tathā vipākaṃ pratisaṃvedayata ityevaṃ sati brahmacaryabhāso na bhavatyavakāśaśca na prajñāyate samyag duḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai / yastvevaṃ vadedyathāyaṃ puruṣapugdalo yathāvedanīyaṃ karma karotyupacinoti tathā tathā yathāvedanīyaṃ vipākaṃ pratisaṃvedayata ityevaṃ sati brahmacaryabhāso bhavatyavakāśaśca prajñāyate samyag duḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai
# 'di las bzlog pa ni stobs dang mi ldan pa'i las so / / bcom ldan 'das kyis su zhig 'di skad du skyes bu gang zag 'di ji lta ji ltar las byed cing sogs pa de lta de ltar rnam par smin pa myong bar 'gyur na / / de lta na tshangs par spyod par gnas par mi 'gyur zhing yang dag par sdug bsngal zad pa dang sdug bsngal mthar dbyung ba'i skabs kyang mi snang ngo zhes zer ba dang yang su zhig 'di skad du skyes bu gang zag 'di ji lta ji ltar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las byed cing sogs pa de lta de ltar rnam par smin pa myong bar 'gyur na /
iti yaduktaṃ sūtre tatra ko 'bhisaṃdhiḥ / tatra buddhā manasyevaṃ mithyāvacanaṃ pratiṣeddhuṃ kāmayante / yat sukhasahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukhasahagata eva vipāko 'bhinirvarttate duḥkhasahagatasya karmaṇo duḥkhasahagata eva vipāko 'bhinirvarttate aduḥkhāsukhasahagatasya karmaṇastatsahagata eva vipāko 'bhinirvarttate / ityevamuktam
# de lta na ni tshangs par spyod pas gnas par 'gyur zhing yang dag par sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur pa dang sdug bsngal mthar dbyung ba'i skabs kyang snang ngo / / zhes zer zhes / / bcom ldan 'das kyis gang gsungs pa de la dgongs pa gang zhe na / / 'dir ni bcom ldan 'das kyis bde ba dang ldan pa'i las kyi rnam par smin pa bde ba dang ldan pa bkag go / / sdug bsngal dang ldan pa'i sdug bsngal dang ldan pa dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang ldan pa'i sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang ldan pa yang de bzhin no /
samyagvacanaṃ tvevamanumanyate / sukhasahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukhavedanīyasya sukhavipāko 'nujñāyate duḥkhavedanīyasya duḥkhavipāko 'nujñāyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanīyasyāduḥkhāsukhavipāko 'nujñāyate
# yang bde ba dang ldan zhing bde ba myong ba bar 'gyur ba'i rnams par smin pa bde ba ni gnang ngo / / sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa bde ba yang ma yin pa dang sdug bsngal dang ldan la bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i rnam par smin pa bde ba ni gnang ngo /
duḥkhasahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukhavedanīyasya sukhavipāko 'nujñāyate duḥkhavedanīyasya duḥkhavipāko 'nujñāyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanīyasyāduḥkhāsukhavipāko 'nujñāyate / aduḥkhāsukhasahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukhavedanīyasya  sukhavipāko 'nujñāyate duḥkhavedanīyasya duḥkhavipāko 'nujñāyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanīyasyāduḥkhāsukhavipāko 'nujñāyate / eṣo 'bhisandhiḥ tatra sūtre / api khalu karmaprabhedastrividhaḥ / saṃvarakarma asaṃvarakarma naivasaṃvaranāsaṃvarakarma ca / saṃvarakarma katamat / prātimokṣasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma dhyānasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma anāsravasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma ca / prātimokṣasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma katamat / sapta saṃghopapannānāṃ saṃvarāḥ / bhikṣusaṃvaraḥ bhikṣuṇīsaṃvaraḥ śikṣamāṇavasaṃvaraḥ śrāmaṇerasaṃvaraḥ śrāmaṇerī saṃvaraḥ upāsakasaṃvaraḥ upāsikāsaṃvaraḥ upavāsasaṃvaraśca
# sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa bde ba yang ma yin pa dang ldan la bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i rnam par smin pa bde ba ni gnang ngo / / sdug bsngal la myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'o zhes bya ba 'di ni 'dir dgongs pa'o / / las kyi rab tu dbye ba ni / / sdom pa'i las dang sdom pa ma yin pa'i las dang sdom pa yang ma yin sdom pa ma yin pa yang ma yin pa'i las so / / sdom pa'i las gang zhe na / / so sor thar pa'i sdom pas bsdus pa dang bsam gtan gyi sdom pas bsdus pa dang zag pa med pa'i sdom pas bsdus pa'o / / so sor thar pa'i sdom bas bsdus pa'i las gang zhe na / / ris brgyad de / / dge slong gi sdom pa dang dge slong ma'i sdom pa dang dge slong ma'i sdom pa dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa dang dge tshul ma'i sdom pa dang dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang dge bsnyen ma'i sdom pa dang bsnyen gnas pa'i sdom pa'o /
katamaṃ pugdalamadhikṛtya pravrajitasaṃvaro vyavasthāpitaḥ
# rab tu byung ba'i sdom pa gang zag ji lta bu'i dbang du byas te rnam par gzhag ce na /
duścaritavivekacaritaṃ kāmavivekacaritaṃ pugdalamadhikṛtya
# nyes par spyod pa las bden par spyod pa dang 'dod pa las bden par spyod pa'o /
kaṃ pugdalamadhikṛtya upāsakopāsikāsaṃvaro vyavasthāpitaḥ
# dge bsnyen dang dge bsnyen ma'i sdom pa gang zag ji lta bu'i dbang du byas te rnam par gzhag ce na /
duścaritavivekacaritamadhikṛtya no tu kāmavivekacaritaṃ pugdalam
# nyes par spyod pa las bden par spyod pa yin gyi 'dod pa las bden par spyod pa ni ma yin no /
kaṃ pugdalamadhikṛtyopavāsasaṃvaro vyavasthāpitaḥ
# bsnyen gnas pa'i sdom pa gang zag ji lta bu'i dbang du byas te rnam par gzhag ce na /
naiva duścaritavivekacaritaṃ na kāmavivekacaritaṃ pugdalamadhikṛtya
# nyes par spyod pa las bden par spyod pa yang ma yin / / 'dod pa las bden par spyod pa yang ma yin pa'o /
upāsakānāmekatyānāṃ śikṣāsyānīyānāṃ śikṣasamavāgama ityucyate
# dge bsnyen bslab pa'i gzhi'i phyogs gcig la slob na dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang ldan pa zhes bya'am /
upāsakasaṃvaro 'samanvāgama ityucyate / uktaḥ samanvāgamaḥ śīlavipattirapyucyate / yathā ṣaṇḍapaṇḍakānām
# ldan pa ma yin pa zhes bya zhe na / / ldan pa zhes kyang bya / / tshul khrims 'chal pa zhes kyang bya'o /
teṣā mupāsakasaṃvaraḥ pratiṣidhyate na vā / teṣāmupāsakasaṃvaro na pratiṣidhyate
# za ma dang ma ning rnams las dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa bkag gam / / dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa ma bkag ce na /
kevalaṃ teṣāmupāsakatvaṃ pratiṣidhyate / bhikṣubhikṣuṇīnāmubhayapravrajitānāṃ saṃghasya pakṣasya saṃsevopāsanāyogyatvāt
# dge bsnyen nyid ni bkag ste / / dge slong dang dge slong ma'i phyogs gnyis la bsnyen bkur bya ba'i 'os ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
paṇḍakaḥ punaḥ pañcavidhaḥ / jātipaṇḍakaḥ īrṣyāpaṇḍakaḥ pakṣapaṇḍakaḥ āsecanakapaṇḍakaḥ āpatpaṇḍakaśca / dhyānasaṃvarasaṃgṛhitaṃ karma katamat
# ma ning ni lnga ste / / skyes nas ma ning du gyur pa dang ma ning phrag dog can dang ma ning zla phyed pa dang rlugs pa'i ma ning dang nyams pa'i ma ning ngo / / bsam gtan gyi sdom pa gang zhe na /
dauḥśīlyasamutthāpakānāṃ kleśānāṃ vījopaghāte sati kāmebhyo vītarāgasya yā viratiḥ / prathamadhyānavītarāgasya yā viratiḥ / dvitīyadhyanavītarāgasya yā viratiḥ
# 'chal ba'i tshul khrims kun nas slong ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi sa bon 'joms pa'i dus na 'dod pa la 'dod chags dang bral bas spong ba gang yin pa dang bsam gtan dang po la 'dod chags dang bral ba dang bsam gtan gnyis pa la 'dod chags dang bral ba dang bsam gtan gsum pa la 'dod chags dang bral bas spong ba gang yin pa'o / / zag pa med pa'i sdom pa gang zhe na /
tṛtīyadhyānavītarāgasya yā viratiḥ / socyate dhyānasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ kāyavākkarma / anāsravasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma katamat / satyadarśanena anāsravamanaskārabalena pratilabdhā anāsravā viratiḥ / socyate anāsravasaṃvarasaṃgṛhītaṃ karma
# bden pa mthong ba'i zag pa med pa'i yid la byed pas spangs pa gang yin pa'o / / sdom pa ma yin pa gang zhe na / / sdom pa ma yin pa shan pa dang bya gag gsod pa dang phag gis 'tsho ba dang; nya pa dang ri dags kyi rngon pa dang bya pa dang bong rgyas 'tshor ba dang tshom rkun pa dang gshed ma dang glang po che 'dzin pa dang sbrul gyis 'tsho ba dang btson srung dang nyan rna byed pa dang gnod pa byed pa pa rnams kyi gang yin pa'o /
asaṃvarakarma katamat
# de dag gi rigs las skyes pas sam /
abhijanmato vā tatkarmasamādānato vā tatkarmādhyācāraniścayaḥ asaṃvara ityucyate / te punarasaṃvarāḥ katame / aurabhrikāḥ kaukkṛṭikāḥ śaukarikāḥ śākunikāḥ mātsyikāḥ lubdhakāḥ vāgurikāḥ corāḥ ghātakāḥ govaṃdhakāḥ nāgavaṃdhakāḥ māṇḍalikāḥ nāgamaṇḍalikāḥ kārāgārikāḥ sūcakāḥ upaghātakāḥ prabhṛtayaḥ / naivasaṃvaranāsaṃvara saṃgṛhītaṃ karma katamat / naivasaṃvaranāsaṃvaravihāraḥ kuśalākuśalaṃ karma / punaḥ karmaprabhedastrividhaḥ / sukhavedanīyaṃ karma duḥkhavedanīyaṃ karma aduḥkhāsukhavedanīyaṃ karma ca / sukhavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / kāmāvacarāt tṛtīyadhyānaṃ yāvad yat kuśalaṃ karma / duḥkhavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / akuśalaṃ karma / aduḥkhāsukhavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / tṛtīyadhyānādūrdhvaṃ yat kuśalaṃ karma / karmaprabhedaḥ punastrividhaḥ / dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyaṃ karma upapadyavedanīyaṃ karma aparaparyāyavedanīyaṃ karma ca / dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / tatkarma dṛṣṭe dharme yasya vipāko vipacyate / tacca maitrīsamāpatteruccalitasyaṃ parihāṇiṃ vṛddhiṃ vā kurvataḥ dṛṣṭe dharme vipāko labhyate / yathā maitrīsamāpatteruccalitasya tathā araṇasamāpatteruccalitasya niurodhasamāpatteruccalitasya strotāpattiphalāduccalitasya arhattvaphalāduccalitasya ca / buddhapramukhe saṃghe kuśalamakuśalaṃ ca kurvataḥ dṛṣṭe dharme vipāko labhyate / anyeṣāṃ tīvrāśayaprayogeṇa kuśalākuśalakarmapratipannānāmapi dṛṣṭe dharme vipāko labhyate / upapadyavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / tatkarma anantare janmani yasya vipāko vipacyate / tadyathā paṃcanāntaryakarmāṇi / api ca yānyanyāni kuśalākuśalāni karmāṇi yeṣāmanantare janmani vipāko vipacyate tatsarvamucyate upapadyavedanīyaṃ karma / aparaparyāyavedanīyaṃ karma katamat / tatkarma yasyānantarajanmano 'paraparyāyeṣu vipāko vipacyate / taducyate 'paraparyāyavedanīyaṃ karma / punaḥ karmaprabhedaścaturvidhaḥ / kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇavipākaṃ karma śuklaṃ śuklavipākaṃ karma kṛṣṇaśuklaṃ kṛṣṇaśuklavipākaṃ karma akṛṣṇaśuklāvipākaṃ vyāmiśraṃ karma / kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇavipākaṃ karma katamat / akuśalaṃ karma / śuklaṃ śuklavipākaṃ karma katamat / traidhātukaṃ kuśalaṃ karma / kṛṣṇaśuklaṃ kṛṣṇaśuklavipākaṃ karma katamat / kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ karma yat karma vā āśayataḥ prayogato vā śuklaṃ yat karma vā prayogataḥ kṛṣṇamāśayataḥ śuklam / akṛṣṇaśuklāvipākaṃ vyāmiśraṃ karma katamat / prayogānantaryamārge 'nāsravaṃ karma aviśeṣeṇa ca sarvasyānāsravakarmaṇaḥ paripanthamānukūlyasvabhāvamadhikṛtya vaṃkadoṣakaṣāyāṇāṃ śauceyānāṃ mauneyānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ yathākramaṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / tathā ca dānāni śauceyāni karmāṇi / dānakarma katamat / nidānataḥ utthānataḥ pradeśataḥ svabhāvataśca dānakarma vikalpyate / nidānam alobho 'dveṣo 'mohaśca kuśalamūlāni / utthānaṃ tānyeva cetanāsahagatāni / pradeśo deyāni vastūni / svabhāvo dānasaṃpattikāle kāyavāṅmanaskarmāṇi / dānasaṃpat katamā / abhīkṣṇadānataḥ apakṣapātadānataḥ icchāparipūraṇadānataśca dānasaṃpad veditavyā / api ca aniśritadānataḥ mahāśucidānataḥ parama prahṛṣṭadānataḥ abhikṣṇadānataḥ kṣetrabhājanadānataḥ navapurāṇasaṃvibhāgadānataśca dānasaṃpad veditavyā / deyasaṃpat katamā / anabhidutadeyavastutaḥ aparāpakṛtadeyavastutaḥ akuthitavimaladeyavastutaḥ śucideyavastutaḥ dharmārjitadeyavastutaśca deyasaṃpad veditavyā / tathācoktaṃ sūtre śīlasamanvāgataḥ prātimokṣasaṃvarasaṃvṛta ācāragocarasaṃpanno 'ṇumātreṣvavadyeṣu mahābhayadarśī śikṣate śikṣāpadeṣu iti / kathaṃ śīlasamanvāgato bhavati / viśuddhaśīlanupkṣaṇopapannataḥ / kathaṃ prātimokṣasaṃvarasaṃvṛto bhavati / nairyāṇikaśīlasaṃdhāraṇataḥ / kathamācāragocarasaṃpanno bhavati / viśuddhaśīlasahabhāvato 'garhitānām
# yang dag par blangs pa ste / / de dag gi las spyad par nges par byas pa'o / / sdom pa yang ma yin sdom pa ma yin pa yang ma yin pa gang zhe na / / sdom pa yang ma yin sdom pa ma yin pa yang ma yin pa'i las dge ba'am / / mi dge ba gang yin pa'o / / bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / 'dod pa'i khams dang bsam gtan gsum po dag gi dge ba gang yin pa'o / / sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / gang mi dge ba'o / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / bsam gtan gsum pa las gong ma'i dge ba'o / / mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / gang mthong ba'i chos la rnams par smin pa rnam par smin par 'gyur ba ste / / 'di lta ste / / byams pa'i ting nge 'dzin las langs pa la phan 'dogs pa dang gnod par byed pa las byung ba dang byams pa'i ting nge 'dzin la ji lta bar nyon mongs pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang 'gog pa la snyoms par 'jug pa dang rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu las langs pa dang sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun la yang de bzhin no / / yang na gang bsam pa shin tu drag pos sbyor bas dge ba'am mi dge ba spyod pa'o / / skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / gang tshe phyi ma'i nyid la rnam par smin pa rnams par smin par 'gyur ba ste / / 'di lta ste / / mtshams med pa lnga'i las rnams so / / yang na dge ba dang mi dge ba gzhan yang yin no / / lan grangs gzhan la myong bar 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / gang de phan chad du rnam par smin pa rnam par smin par 'gyur ba'o / / gnag la rnam par smin pa gnag pa'i las gang zhe na / / gang mi dge ba'o / / dkar la rnam par smin pa dkar ba'i las gang zhe na / / khams gsum pa'i dge ba'o / / dkar gnag tu gyur la rnam par smin pa dkar gnag tu 'gyur ba gang zhe na / / 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i 'dren ma ste / / bsam pas gnag la sbyor bas dkar ba'am / / sbyor bas gnag la bsam pas dkar ba'o / / mi gnag cing dkar la rnam par smin par mi 'gyur zhing las zad par 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na / / sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa'i lam rnams la zag pa med pa'i las so / / sbyin pa'i las gang zhe na / / de'i gzhi dang kun nas slong ba dang dngos po dang ngo bo nyid kyis kyang rig par bya ste / / gzhi ni ma chags pa dang zhe sdang med pa dang gti mug med pa'o / / kun nas slong ba ni de dag dang ldan pa'i sems pa'o / / dngos po ni dngos po'o / / ngo bo nyid ni gtong ba na lus kyi las dang ngag gi las so / / ji ltar na sbyin pa phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na / / phyir zhing sbyin pa dang phyogs mi 'byed par sbyin pa dang 'dod pa yongs su rdzogs par sbyin pa'i phyir ro / / yang mi gnas par sbyin pa dang rgya cher sbyin pa dang dga' bas sbyin pa dang phyir zhing sbyin pa dang snod la sbyin pa dang 'khor dang glo bur du 'ongs pa la legs par bgos te sbyin pas sbyin pa phun sum tshogs par rig par bya'o / / ji ltar na sbyin par bya ba phun sum tshogs par rig par ba zhe na / / sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po gnod pas grub pa ma yin pa dang sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po gzhan las phrogs pa ma yin pa dang sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po ma rul zhing dri ma med pa dang sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po rung ba dang sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po chos kyis bsgrubs pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na / / yang dag par blangs pa'i tshul khrims rjes su srung ba'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na so sor thar pa'i sdom pas bsdoms pa yin zhe na / / nges par 'byin pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na cho ga dang spyod yul phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na / / ma smad pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir ro /
kathamaṇumātreṣvavadyeṣu mahābhayadarśī bhavati
# ji ltar na kha na ma tho ba chung ngu tsam rnams la yang 'jigs par lta ba yin zhe na /
tīvreṇa gauraveṇa śīlaśikṣaṇataḥ
# shin tu gus par slob pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ śikṣate śikṣāpadeṣu
# ji ltar na yang dag par blangs pa la slob ce na /
śikṣāśīlānāṃ śikṣaṇataḥ / ataḥ paraṃ śīlamārabhya yad buddhena sūtreṣu nirdṛṣṭaṃ kāyena saṃvṛto bhavatītyevamādi / kathamucyate kāyena vācā saṃvṛto bhavati
# bslab pa'i gzhi'i gnas rnams la bslab pa yongs su rdzogs par slob pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gis bsdams pa yin zhe na /
saṃprajanyaparigṛhītataḥ
# shes bzhin gyis yongs su zin pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ kāyavāksaṃpattyā saṃpanno bhavati
# ji ltar na lus dang ngag phun sum tshogs pas phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na /
āpattyanāpattidānataḥ / kathaṃ pariśuddhakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati / avipratisārādīnāṃ krameṇa saṃpratipattyā yāvat samādhilābhasanniśraya taḥ / kathaṃ kuśalakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# ltung ba mi byed pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa yongs su dag pa yin zhe na / / 'gyod pa med pa la sogs pa'i rim gyis ting nge 'dzin gyi bar la gnas pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa dge ba yin zhe na /
kliṣṭavitarkavyavatīrṇataḥ
# nyon mongs pa can gyi rtog pa dang ma 'dres pa'i phyir ro /
kathamanavadyakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa kha na ma tho ba med pa yin zhe na /
mithyāpraṇidhiparivarjanena brahmacaryabhāvanātaḥ / kathamavyāvadhyakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# smon nas tshangs par spyod pa la gnas pa rnam par spangs pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa gnod pa med pa yin zhe na /
pareṣāmanavajñayā sukhasaṃvāsataḥ
# gzhan la brnyas thabs mi byed cing 'grogs na bde ba'i phyir ro /
kathamānulomikāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa rjes su mthun pa yin zhe na /
nirvāṇaprāptyanukūlataḥ / katha manucchavikakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# mya ngan las 'das pa thob par byed pa dang mthun pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa rjes su 'byor ba yin zhe na /
kuśalasya cchādanato 'kuśalasya prakāśanataśca / kathamaupayikakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# dge ba mi spyoms pa dang sdig pa mi 'chab pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa thabs dang ldan pa yin zhe na /
sabrahmacaryagrahaṇaśīlataḥ / kathaṃ pratirūpakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa nye bar sdud pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa 'tsham pa yin zhe na /
guruṣu gurusthānīyeṣu cānihitamānataḥ / kathaṃ pradakṣiṇakāyāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# bla ma rnams dang bla ma dang 'dra ba rnams la nga rgyal bcag pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa mthun pa yin zhe na /
avavāde pradakṣiṇaprāhitataḥ / kathamataptakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# gdams ngag la mthun par 'dzin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa gdung ba med pa yin zhe na /
kaṣṭapohīnādhimukti vivarjitataḥ / kathamatanutāpyakāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# dka' thub drag po dang ngan don la mos pa rnam par spangs pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa phyis 'gyod pa med pa yin zhe na /
samutsṛṣṭabhogakarmāntāvipratisāritaḥ / kathamavipratisārikāyavāksamudācāro bhavati
# longs spyod dang las kyi mtha' spangs pa la 'gyod pa med pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa yid la gcags pa med pa yin zhe na /
alpamātreṇāsaṃtuṣṭāvipratisāritayā
# cung zad tsam gyis chog par mi 'dzin pas yid la gcags pa med pa'i phyir ro /
yaduktaṃ bhagavatā yathā sattvāḥ / karmasvakā karmadāyādāḥ karmayonīyāḥ karmapratisaraṇāḥ karma sarvān sattvān vibhajati uccanīcatayā hīnapraṇītatayā  iti
# bcom ldan 'das kyis sems can 'di dag las bdag gir bya ba las kyi bgo skal la spyod pa las kyi skye gnas pa la brten par bya ba dag ste / / las ni sems can mthon po dang dma' ba dang ngan pa dang gya nom pa rnam par 'byed pa'o zhes gang gsungs pa la /
kathaṃ sattvāḥ karmasvakā bhavanti
# las bdag gir bya ba ji lta bu zhe na /
svayaṃkṛtakarmanipākapratisaṃvedanātāmupādaya
# rang gis byas pa'i las kyi rnam par smin pa myong ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ karmadāyādā bhavanti
# ji ltar na las kyi bgo skal la spyod pa yin zhe na /
svayaṃ kṛtakarmavipākapratisaṃvedanatāyāṃ kuśalākuśalānāṃ karmaṇāmanyonyadāyādatāmupādāya
# rang gis byas pa'i rnam par smin pa myong ba de la dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las so so'i bgo skal la spyod pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ karmayonīyā bhavanti
# ji ltar na las kyi skye gnas pa yin zhe na /
sattvānāṃ mahetuviṣamahetuvivarjitayonitāmupādāya / kathaṃ karmapratisaraṇā bhavanti / pratipakṣakarmaviśiṣṭakarmabandhanāśrayatāmupādāya
# rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa'i rgyu rnam par spangs pa'i las kyi skye gnas las sems can byung ba'i phyir ro / / ji ltar na las brten par bya ba yin zhe na / / las kyis bcings pa las rnam par thar par byed pa'i gnyen po'i las brten pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ karmaṇā sattvo uccanīcā bhavanti
# sems can mthon po dang dma' ba gang zhe na /
yat karmaṇā sugatau durgatau vātmabhāvaprabhedaṃ labhante / kathaṃ hīnapraṇītā bhavanti / yat sattvā guṇadoṣaprabhedena samanvāgatā bhavanti
# bde 'gro dang ngan 'gror lus thob pa'o / / ngan pa dang gya non pa gang zhe na / / de dag nyid skyon dang ldan pa dang yon tan dang ldan pa'o /
yaduktaṃ bhagavatā sattvānāṃ karmavipāko 'cintya iti / tatra kathaṃ karmavipākaścintyaḥ kathaṃ karmavipāko 'cintyaḥ
# sems can rnams kyi las kyi rnam par smin pa bsam gyis mi khyab po zhes gang gsungs pa de la / / las kyi rnam par smin pa bsam gyis khyab pa ni ji lta bu /
kuśalasya karmaṇo devamanuṣyagatisviṣṭa vipākalā bhaścintyaḥ / akuśalasya karmaṇo hīnāsu tisṛṣu durgatiṣu aniṣṭavipākalābhaścintyaḥ
# bsam gyis mi khyab pa ni ji lta bu zhe na / / las dge ba'i rnam par smin pa lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du 'dod pa ni bsam gyis khyab pa'o /
ayaṃ cintyaḥ / yena karmaṇā sattvānāmātmabhāvavipākavaicitryamabhunirvarttate so 'cintyaḥ / tadeva kuśalākuśalaṃ karmasthānavastuhetuvipākaprakārādiprabhederacintyam / vividhavāhyavastuvaicitryābhinirvarttakaṃ karmācintyam / maṇimantraupadhimuṣṭiyogapratisaṃyuktaṃ karmācintyam
# mi dge ba'i las kyi rnam par smin pa sems can dmyal ba dang dud 'gro dang yi dags kyi ngan song ngan 'gro log par ltung ba rnams su mi 'dod pa zhes bya ba ni bsam gyis khyab pa'o / / las 'dis ni sems can rnams kyi lus sna tshogs su 'gyur zhes bya ba 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab po / / las dge ba dang mi dge ba de nyid gnas dang dngos po dang rgyu dang rnam par smin pa dang rab tu dbye bas ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o / / phyi'i dngos po sna tshogs mngon par 'grub par byed pa'i las bsam gyis mi khyab po / / nor bu dang sngags dang sman dang mkhyud dpyad dang ldan pa'i las bsam gyis mi khyab po /
yogināṃ prabhāvakarmacintyuam
# rnal 'byor pa thams cad kyi mthu'i las bsam gyis mi khyab po /
bodhisattvānāṃ vaśitābhiḥ kriyamāṇaṃ karmā citnyam
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang gi las bsam gyis mi khyab ste /
tadyathā āyurvaśitayā cittavaśitayā pariṣkāravaśitayā karmavaśitayā upapattivaśitayā adhimuktivaśitayā praṇidhānavaśitayā ṛddhivaśitayā jñānavaśitayā dharmavaśitayā / evaṃ ca bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmevamādibhirvaśitābhiryatkarma kriyate tadacintyam
# 'di lta ste / / tshe la dbang ba dang sems la dbang ba dang yo byad la dbang ba dang las la dbang ba dang skye ba la dbang ba dang mos pa la dbang ba dang smon lam la dbang ba dang rdzu 'phrul la dbang ba dang ye shes la dbang ba dang chos la dbang ba'i phyir ro /
sarveṣāṃ buddhānāṃ vuddhakṛtyānuṣṭhānaṃ karmācintyam
# sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bsgrub pa'i phyir phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab po /
tathā ca samudayasatyaṃ samāsato lakṣaṇaprabhedena caturvidham / hetulakṣaṇaṃ samudayalakṣaṇaṃ prabhavalakṣaṇaṃ pratyalakṣaṇaṃ ca
# de dag mdor bsdu na kun 'byung ba'i bden pa'i mtshan nyid rnam par bzhir rig par bya ste / / rgyu'i mtshan nyid dang kun 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid dang rab tu skye ba'i mtshan nyid dang rkyen gyi mtshan nyid do /
hetulakṣaṇaṃ katamat / punarbhavavāsanāyā āhārakaṃ kāraṇaṃ heturiti hetulakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam
# rgyu'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na / / yang srid pa'i bag chags 'jog pa'i byed rgyu yin pa'i phyir rgyu'i mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
samudayalakṣaṇaṃ katamat
# kun 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
teṣāṃ teṣāmupacitavāsanānāṃ sattvānāṃ tasmiṃstasmin sattvanikāye udayasya kāraṇamiti  samudayalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam
# sems can bag chags bsags pa de dang de dag sems can gyi ris de dang der kun 'byung ba'i byed rgyu yin pa'i phyir kun 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
prabhuvalakṣaṇaṃ katamat
# rab tu skye ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
pratyātmaṃ santānānāṃ sarvaprakāraprakarṣodbhavasya kāraṇamiti prabhavalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam
# so so rang dang rnams dang mchog tu 'byung ba'i byed rgyu yin pa'i phyir rab tu skye ba'i mtshan nyid du blta'o /
pratyalakṣaṇaṃ katamat
# rkyen gyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
sattvānāṣānpaprāptyatyayakāraṇamiti pratyayakāraṇaṃ veditavyam
# gzhan dang gzhan 'thob pa dang 'da' ba'i byed rgyu yin pa'i phyir rkyen gyi mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
atha viniścaye satyaparicchede prathame tṛtīyo bhāgaḥ / nirodhasatyaṃ katamat / lakṣaṇataḥ gāmbhīryataḥ saṃvṛtitaḥ paramārthataḥ aparipūritaḥ paripūritaḥ niralaṃkārataḥ sālaṃkārataḥ śeṣataḥ aśeṣataḥ agrataḥ paryāyataśca nirodhasatyaṃ veditavyam
# bam po bzhi pa / / 'gog pa'i bden pa gang zhe na / / mtshan nyid dang zab pa dang brda dang don dam pa dang yongs su ma rdzogs pa dang yongs su rdzogs pa dang rgyan med pa dang rgyan dang bcas pa dang lhag ma dang bcas pa dang lhag ma med pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa dang rnam grangs kyis kyang 'gog pa'i bden par rig par bya'o /
lakṣaṇataḥ katamat
# mtshan nyid kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
tathatāyāmārya mārge kleśānāmanutpādo yo nirodhāśrayo nirodhako nirodhasvabhāvo vā
# de bzhin nyid dang lam dang nyon mongs pa mi 'byung ba ste / / gang du 'gog pa dang gang gis 'gog pa dang gang 'gog pa'o /
tannirodhasatyalakṣaṇam
# bcom ldan 'das kyis skad du /
yaduktaṃ bhagavatā cakṣuḥ śrotre ghrāṇajivhākāyāḥ
# gang du mig dang rna ba dag / / de bzhin sna dang lce dang lus /
manaśca teṣu āyataneṣu nāmarūpayorātyantikanirodho na śeṣaḥ iti
# yid dang de bzhin ming dang gzugs / / ma lus par ni 'gog 'gyur ba / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
yaccoktaṃ tadāyatanaṃ veditavyaṃ yathā cakṣuśca nirudhyate rūpasaṃjñā ca virajyate yāvat manaśca nirudhyate dharmasaṃjñā ca virajyate iti
# yang gsungs pa / / gang du mig 'gag pa dang kha dog gi 'du shes med par 'gyur ba dang chos kyi bar du 'gag pa dang chos kyi 'du shes med par 'gyur ba de ni gnas su rig par bya'o zhe'o /
anena nayena ālambanānāṃ prāpaṇaṃ tathatāyāmālambanādūrdhvaṃ sāsravāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ nirodhaḥ / tannirodhasatya lakṣaṇam
# rnam grangs 'dis na de bzhin nyid la dmigs pa gang du zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po 'gag pa de 'gog pa'i mtshan nyid do /
gāmbhīryataḥ katamat
# zab pas ji lta bu zhe na /
yat teṣāṃ saṃskārāṇāmuparamānnirodhaḥ / tathoparamāt teṣāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ nirodho nānyo vācyaḥ nānanyo vācyaḥ nāpyanyo nāpyananyo vācyaḥ na naivānyo nānanyo vācyaḥ
# 'du byed de dag gi 'jig pa las 'gog pa de gzhan zhes kyang mi bya / / gzhan ma yin pa zhes kyang mi bya / / gzhan yang yin la gzhan ma yin pa yang yin zhes kyang mi bya / / gzhan pa'ang ma yin la gzhan ma yin pa'ang ma yin zhes kyang mi bya'o /
kutaḥ / niṣprapañcataḥ
# de ci'i phyir zhe na /
asmiṃstvarthe prapañcotpattiḥ na saṃcintyā na mārgeṇa na nyāyena na kuśalaprayogeṇa cintyā iti / yaduktaṃ bhagavatā teṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ spraṣṭāvyayatanānāṃ kṣayo virāgo nirodho vyupaśamo 'staṃgama ityevamādi
# spros pa med pa'i phyir ro / / spros pa ni skabs 'dir tshul bzhin ma yin pa sems pa yin te / / bcom ldan 'das kyis ji skad du reg pa'i skye mched drug po dag zad pa dang rnam par zhig pa dang 'gog pa dang nye bar zhi ba dang nub pa las gzhan yod do zhe na / / spros pa med pa spros par byed do / / gzhan med do zhe'am / / yod kyang yong la med kyang med do zhe'am /
syādanyaḥ syādananyaḥ syādanyo 'pi nānyo 'pi  syānnaivānyo nānanyo 'pi iti niṣprapañca prapañca utpadyate / yāvat ṣaḍāyatanāni tāvat prapañcāḥ
# gzhan yod pa'ang ma yin med pa'ang ma yin zhe na / / yang spros pa med pa spros par byed do / / ji srid du skye mched drug yod pa de srid du spros pa'o /
yadā ṣaḍāyatanānāṃ nirodhaśchedaḥ tadā prapañcānāṃ viratiḥ
# skye mched drug 'gags pas spros pa med pa ste / / mya ngan las 'das par bstan to zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o; /
saṃvṛtitaḥ katamat
# brdas ji lta bu zhe na /
laukikamārgairvījanigraheṇa yo nirodho labhyate
# 'jig rten pa'i lam gyis sa bon nyams smad pas 'gog pa gang yin pa ste /
ato bhagavatā tadāṃśikanirvāṇamityucyate / paramārthataḥ katamat
# de'i phyir bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i rnam grangs su de'i yan lag gis mya ngan las 'das par gsungs so / / don dam pas ji lta bu zhe na /
āryaprajñayā bījanirmūlanena yo nirodho labhyate
# 'phags pa'i shes rab kyis sa bon kun tu bcom pas 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
aparipūritaḥ katamat
# yongs su ma rdzogs pas ji lta bu zhe na /
śaikṣāṇāṃ strotāpannaphalasaṃgraheṇa vā sakṛdāgamiphalasaṃgraheṇa vā anāgāmiphalasaṃgraheṇa vā yo nirodhaḥ
# rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bur bsdus pa'am / / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bur bsdus pa'am / / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bur bsdus pa'ang rung ste / / slob pa rnams kyi 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
paripūritaḥ katamat
# yongs su rdzogs pas ji lta bu zhe na /
aśaikṣyāṇāmarhattvaphalasaṃgraheṇa yo nirodhaḥ
# dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bur bsdus pa mi slob pa rnams kyi 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
niralaṃkārataḥ katamat
# rgyan med pas ji lta bu zhe na /
prajñāvimuktānāmarhatāṃ yo nirodhaḥ
# shes rab kyi rnam par grol ba'i dgra bcom pa rnams kyi 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
sālaṃkārataḥ katamat
# rgyan dang bcas pas ji lta bu zhe na /
ubhayabhāga vimuktānāṃ traividyānāṃ ṣaḍabhijñānāmarhatāṃ yo nirodhaḥ
# gnyi ga'i cha las rnam par grol ba rig pa gsum dang mngon par shes pa drug dang ldan pa'i dgra bcom pa rnams kyi 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
śeṣataḥ katamat / sopadhiśeṣo yo nirodhaḥ / aśeṣataḥ katamat
# lhag ma dang bcas pas ji lta bu zhe na / / phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa'i 'gog pa gang yin pa'o / / lhag ma med pas ji lta bu zhe na /
nirupadhiśeṣo yo nirodhaḥ
# phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i 'gog pa gang yin pa'o /
agrataḥ katamat / buddhānāṃ bodhisattvānāmapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇasaṃgraheṇa yo nirodhaḥ
# khyad par du 'phags pas ji lta bu zhe na / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das par bsdus pa'i 'gog pa gang yin pa ste /
sparśavihāriṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ sattvānāṃ hitasukhādhiṣṭhānataḥ
# sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba nye bar gnas pa'i phyir ro /
paryāyataḥ katamat
# rnam grangs kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
aśeṣaprahāṇaṃ pratiniḥsargaḥ vyantībhāvaḥ kṣayo virāgo nirodho vyupaśamo 'staṃgama ityevamādi / kimupādāyocyate aśeṣaprahāṇam / pariśiṣṭāni padānyupādāya / kimupādāyocyate pratiniḥsargaḥ
# ma lus par spangs pa dang nges par spangs pa dang byang bar gyur pa dang zad pa dang 'dod chags dang bral ba dang 'gog pa dang rnam par zhi ba dang nub pa'o / / zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / ci'i phyir ma lus par spangs pa zhes bya zhe na / / tshig lhag ma rnams kyi phyir ro / / ci'i phyir nges par spangs pa zhes bya zhe na / / kun nas dkris pa bor ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir byang bar gyur pa zhes bya zhe na /
paryavasthānapratiniḥsaraṇatāmupādāya / kimupādāyocyate kṣayaḥ / darśanamārgeṇa pratipakṣavisaṃyogalābhatā mupādāya
# bag la nyal mthar phyin par byed pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir zad pa zhes bya zhe na / / gnyen po mthong ba'i lam gyis bral ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāyocyate virāgaḥ / bhāvanāmārgeṇa pratipakṣavisaṃyogalābhatāmupādāya / kimupādāyocyate nirodhaḥ / āyatyāṃ tatphaladuḥkhānutpattitāmupādāya / kimupādāyocyate vyupaśamaḥ / dṛṣṭe dharme tatphalacettaduḥkhāsamudācāratāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir 'dod chags dang bral ba zhes bya zhe na / / gnyen po bsgom pa'i lam gyis bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir 'gog pa zhes bya zhe na / / phi ma la de'i 'bras bu sdug bsngal mi skye ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir rnam par zhi ba zhes bya zhe na / / mthong ba'i chos la de'i 'bras bu sdug bsngal rgyu ba med pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāyocyate 'staṃgamaḥ
# ci'i phyir nub pa zhes bya zhe na /
sopadhiśeṣa nirodhatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarasaṃskṛtamityucyate / lakṣaṇatrayavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punardurdarśa ityucyate
# phung po'i lhag ma rnam 'jig pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir 'dus ma byas zhes bya zhe na / / mtshan nyid gsum dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir blta dka' ba zhes bya zhe na /
carmacakṣuṣo divyacakṣuṣaśca  gocarātikamaṇatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaracalamityucyate / matiṣu saṃcārabirahamāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaramata mityucyate / tṛṣṇātrayavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaramṛtamityucyate
# sha dang lha'i mig gi spyod yul las shin tu 'das pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir g yo ba med pa zhes bya zhe na / / 'gro bar 'pho ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir mi 'dud pa zhes bya zhe na / / sred pa gsum dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir 'chi ba med pa zhes bya zhe na /
skandhamāravirahatāmupādāya / kimuipādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaranāsravamityucyate / sarva kleśamāravirahatāmupādāya
# phung po'i bdud dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir zag pa med pa zhes bya zhe na / / nyon mongs pa'i bdud dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarlayanamityucyate / anavadyaprītisukhasaṃniśrayatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punardvīpamityucyate / traidhātukaparicchedatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punastrāṇamityucyate / sarvamahāduḥkhopadravāpagamatāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir gnas zhes bya zhe na / / kha na ma tho ba med pa'i dga' ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir gling zhes bya zhe na / / khams gsum las yongs su chad pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir skyob pa zhes bya zhe na / / gnod pa thams cad bzlog pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ śaraṇamityucyate / āśayaprayogayoravandhyapadasthānatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ parāyaṇamityucyate
# ci'i phyir mgon zhes bya zhe na / / der bsam pa dang sbyor ba byas pa 'bras bu yod pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir dpung gnyen zhes bya zhe na /
sarvasya paramāryatvasyāgamanapadasthāṇatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaracyutamityucyate
# 'phags pa'i mchog nyid du 'gro ba'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir 'chi 'pho med pa zhes bya zhe na /
jātivirahatāmupādāya
# skye ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya sa nirodha punarnirvāramityucyate
# ci'i phyir rims nad med pa zhes bya zhe na /
sarvakleśasantāpavirahatāṃ sarvecchālābhaduḥkhamahāsantāpavirahatāṃ copādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarniṣpadāridāhamiotyute / sarva śokaparidevanāduḥkhadaurmanasya vikṣepavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ kṣemamityucyate / hiṃsā bhayarahitavihārapadasthānatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ śivamityucyate / lābhavastupadasthāna tāmupādāya
# 'dod pas phongs pa thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir yongs su gdung ba med pa zhes bya zhe na / / mya ngan dang smre bsngags 'don pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba dang 'khrug pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir bde ba zhes bya zhe na / / 'jig pa med par gnas pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir zhi ba zhes bya zhe na / / phan pa'i dngos po'i phyir ro; /
kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ sauvarṇikamityucyate paramārthasukhādhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir bde gzhi zhes bya zhe na / / don dam pa'i bde ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaḥ svastyayanamityucyate / tatsukhaprayogaprāptipadasthānatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarogyamityucyate / sarvāvaraṇaro gavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarārnijyamityucyate / sarvavikṣepavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarnirvāṇamityucyate
# ci'i phyir dge bar gyur pa zhes bya zhe na / / sbyor ba bde ba 'thob pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir nad med pa zhes bya zhe na / / sgrib pa thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir mi g yo ba zhes bya zhe na / / g yeng ba thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya zhe na /
animittaśāntamahā sukhavihārapadasthānatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarajātamityucyate
# mtshan ma med cing zhing la bde bar gnas pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir ma skyes pa zhes bya zhe na /
pratisaṃdhyupapattivirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarabhūtamityucyate / taduttarakālotpattivirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaraskṛtamityucyate
# nyid mtshams sbyor ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir ma byung ba zhes bya zhe na / / de'i 'og tu 'byung ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir ma byas pa zhes bya zhe na /
pūrvāntakarmakleśabalavadā vedhavirahatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punarasaṃskṛtamityucyate / vartamānakarma kleśānabhisaṃskāra padasthānatāmupādāya / kimupādāya sa nirodhaḥ punaranutpannamityucyate / anāgatasantatyutpādavirahatāmupādāya
# sngon gyi mtha'i las dang nyon mongs pa'i 'phen pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir 'dus ma byas zhes bya zhe na / / da ltar nyon mongs pa 'du mi byed pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir skye ba med pa zhes bya zhe na / / ma 'ongs pa'i rgyud 'byung ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
tathā nirodhasatyasya samāsataścatvāro lakṣaṇaprabhedāḥ / nirodhalakṣaṇaṃ śāntalakṣaṇaṃ praṇītalakṣaṇaṃ niḥsaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ ca / kimupādāya nirodhalakṣaṇam / kleśavisaṃyogatāmupādāya
# yang 'gog pa'i bden pa'i mtshan nyid rnam pa bzhir rig par bya ste / / 'gog pa'i mtshan nyid dang zhi ba'i mtshan nyid dang gya nom pa'i mtshan nyid dang nges par 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid do / / ci'i phyir 'gog pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na / / nyon mongs pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya śāntalakṣaṇam / duḥkhavisaṃyogatāmupādāya / kimupādāya praṇītalakṣaṇam
# ci'i phyir zhi ba'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na / / sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir gya nom pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
sukhaśucyadhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya
# gtsang ba dang bde ba'i dngos po yin pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya niḥsaraṇalakṣaṇam / nityahitādhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir nges par 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na / / rtag pa dang phan pa'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
atha viniścaye satyaparicchede prathame caturtho bhāgaḥ / mārgasatyaṃ katamat / yena duḥkhaṃ parijānīte samudayaṃ prajahāti nirodhaṃ sākṣātkaroti mārgaṃ bhāvayati / etat saṃkṣepeṇa mārgasatyalakṣaṇamityucyate / punaḥ mārgaḥ pañcavidhaḥ / saṃbhāramārgaḥ prayogamārgaḥ darśanamārga bhāvanāmārgaḥ niṣṭhāmārgaśca
# lam gyi bden pa gang zhe na / / lam gang gis sdug bsngal yongs su shes pa dang kun 'byung ba spong ba dang 'gog pa mngon du byed pa dang lam bsgom pa ste / / 'di ni lam gyi mtshan nyid mdor bsdus pa'o / / yang lam rnam pa lnga ste / / tshogs kyi lam dang sbyor ba'i lam dang mthong ba'i lam dang bsgom pa'i lam dang mthar phyin pa'i lam mo /
saṃbhāramārgaḥ katamaḥ
# tshogs kyi lam gang zhe na /
pṛthagjanānāṃ śīlam indriyadvārarakṣā bhojane mātrājñatā prathamarātrau taduttararātriṣu vā nityamamiddhaṃ vīryabhāvanā śamathavipaśyanā saṃprajanyavihāraśca
# so so'i skye bo'i tshul khrims dang dbang po'i sgo bsdams pa dang zas kyi tshod shes pa dang nam gyi cha stod dang nam gyi chad smad la mi nyal bar rnal 'byor la brtson pa dang shes bzhin du gnas par mngon par dga' ba'o /
yadvā punaranyadaupaniṣadaṃ kuśalam śrutamayī prajñā cintāmayī prajñā bhāvanāmayī prajñā / tadbhāvanayā abhisamayavimokṣasthānabhājanāṃ pratilabhate
# yang gang rgyur gyur pa'i dge ba gzhan dang thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba dang bsgoms pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyang ste / / de bsgoms pas mngon par rtogs pa dang rnam par thar par 'gyur ba'i gnas kyi snod nyid du 'gyur ro /
prayogamārgaḥ katamaḥ
# sbyor ba'i lam gang zhe na /
yaḥ saṃbhāramārgaḥ sa prayogamārgaḥ / yastu prayogamārgaḥ sana saṃbhāramārgaḥ
# tshogs kyi gang yin pa sbyor ba'i yang de yin no / / sbyor ba yin la tshogs ma yin pa yang yod de /
saṃbhāramārgopacitāni nirvedhabhāgīyāni kuśalamūlāni ūṣmagataḥ mūrdhānaḥ satyānukūlakṣānti laukikāgradharmaśca
# tshogs bsags pa'i nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams te / / de ni dro bar 'gyur ba dang rtse mo dang bden pa'i rjes su mthun pa'i bzod pa dang 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog rnams so /
ūṣmagataṃ katamat
# dro bar gyur pa gang zhe na /
pratyātmaṃ satye pvālokalabdhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaśca
# so so rang gis bden pa rnams la snang ba thob pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o /
mūrdhānaṃ katamat
# rtse mo gang zhe na /
pratyātmaṃ satyeṣvālokavṛddhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaśca / satyānukūlakṣāntiḥ katamā
# so so rang gis bden pa rnams la snang ba mched pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o / / bden pa'i rjes su mthun pa'i bzod pa gang zhe na /
pratyātmaṃ satyeṣvekadeśapraviṣṭānusṛtaḥ  samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaśca
# so so rang gi bden pa rnams kyi phyogs gcig la zhugs pa dang rjes su song ba'i ring nge 'dzin dang shes rab mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o /
laukikāgradharmaḥ katamaḥ
# 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gang zhe na /
pratyātmaṃ satyeṣvānantaryacittasamādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaśca
# so so rang gis bden pa rnams la de ma thag pa'i sems kyi ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o /
darśanamārgaḥ katamaḥ / samāsato laukikā gradharmānantaramanupalambhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaśca
# mthong ba'i lam gang zhe na / / mdor bsdu na 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gi mjug thogs su mi dmigs pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ste /
samasamālambyālambanajñāmapi tat / pratyātmamapanītasattvasaṃketadharmasaṃketasarvato 'panītobhayasaṃketālambanadharmajñānamapi tat
# dmigs par bya ba dang dmigs par byed pa mnyam pas mnyam par shes par byed pa yang de yin te / / so so rang la sems can gyi brda dang chos kyi brda bsal ba dang thams cad du gnyi ga'i brda bsal ba la dmigs pa'i chos shes pa yang de yin no /
prabhedaśaḥ śunardarśanamārgo laukikāgradharmānantaraṃ duḥkhe dharmajñānakṣāntiḥ, duḥkhe dharmajñānaṃ duḥkhe 'nvayajñānakṣāntiḥ duḥkhe 'nvayajñānaṃ samudaye dharmajñānakṣāntiḥ samudaye dharmajñānaṃ samudaye 'nvayajñānakṣāntiḥ samudaye 'nvayajñānaṃ nirodhe dharmajñānakṣāntiḥ nirodhe dharmajñānaṃ nirodhe 'nvayajñānakṣāntiḥ nirodhe 'nvayajñānaṃ mārge dharmajñānakṣāntiṃ mārge dharmajñānaṃ mārge 'nvayajñānakṣāntiḥ mārge 'nvayajñānam / evaṃca ṣoḍaśa jñānakṣāntibhirdarśanamārgaprabhedāḥ
# yang mthong ba'i lam la rab tu dbye na / / 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gi mjug thogs su sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang sdug bsngal la chos shes pa dang sdug bsngal la rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa dang sdug bsngal la rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa dang kun 'byung la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang kun 'byung la chos shes pa dang kun 'byung la rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa dang kun 'byung bla rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa dang 'gog pa la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang 'gog pa la chos shes pa dang 'gog pa la rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa dang 'gog pa la rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa dang lam la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang lam la chos shes pa dang lam la rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa dang lam la rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa'o /
dukhaṃ katamat
# sdug bsngal gang zhe na /
duḥkhasatyam / duḥkhe dharmaḥ katamaḥ
# sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'o / / sdug bsngal la chos gang zhe na /
duḥkhasatyādhipateyaḥ śāsanadharmaḥ
# sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos bstan pa rnams so /
dharmajñānaṃ katamat
# chos shes pa gang zhe na /
prayogamārge satyādhipateyaṃ dharmavicāraṇājñānam / jñānakṣāntiḥ katamā
# sbyor ba'i lam la sdug bsngal gyi dbang du byas pa las byung ba'i chos la rnam par dpyod pa'i shes pa'o / / bzod pa gang zhe na /
pūrvādhipatibalavicāraṇāmupādāya pratyātmaṃ duḥkhasatye pratyakṣānubhāvinī anāsravā prajñā / yayā prajñāyā duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyān sarvakleśān prajahāti
# sngar rnam par dpyad pa'i dbang du byas nas / / so so rang la sdug bsngal gyi bden pa mngon sum du gyur pa'i zag pa med pa'i shes rab ste / / gang gis sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa spong ba ste /
tasmāducyate duḥkhe dharmajñānakṣāntiriti
# sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i bzod pa zhes bya'o /
duḥkhe dharmajñānaṃ katamat / kṣāntyanantaraṃ yena jñānena pūrvoktebhyaḥ kleśebhyo vimuktiṃ sākṣātkaroti
# sdug bsngal la chos shes pa gang zhe na / / shes pa gang gis bzod pa'i mjug thogs su rnam par grol ba mngon du byed pa'o /
tasmāducyate duḥkhe dharmajñānamiti / duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣāntiḥ katamā / duḥkhe dharmajñānakṣāntyāṃ duḥkhe dharmajñāne ca pratyātmaṃ pratyakṣānubhāvinī anāsravā prajñā utpadyate yaduttaramanvaya eṣa āryadharmāṇām / tasmāducyate duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣāntiḥ
# sdug bsngal la rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa gang zhe na / / sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i mjug thogs su sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang sdug bsngal la chos shes pa 'di gnyis 'phags pa'i chos rnams kyi rgyu'o zhes so so rang la mngon sum du gyur pa'i zag pa med pa'i shes rab bo /
duḥkhe anvayajñānaṃ katamat / tadanantaramanāsravaṃ jñānamutpadyate / yena jñānena duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣāntimupadhārayati / tad duḥkhe 'nvayajñānamityucyate / tadvadanyeṣu satyeṣu yathāyogyam / kṣāntirjñānakṣayo jñeyaḥ / tatra avasthāyāṃ dharmakṣāntijñānaiḥ grāhyāvanoghaḥ
# sdug bsngal la rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa gang zhe na / / shes pa gang gis rjes su rtogs par shes pa'i bzod pa de nges par 'dzin pa'o / / de bzhin du bden pa lhag ma rnams la yang bzod pa dang shes pa rnams ci rigs su shes par bya'o / / de la chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang shes pa rnams kyis ni gzung ba rtogs so /
anvayakṣāntijñānairgrāhakāvabodhaḥ / api ca eṣu sarveṣu kṣāntijñāneṣu animittaprekṣāvihārī veditavyaḥ
# rjes su rtogs pa'i bzod pa dang shes pa rnams kyis ni 'dzin pa rtogs so / / bzod pa dang shes pa thams cad la yang mtshan ma med par gnas pa'i rnal 'byor can du rig par bya'o /
ime ṣoḍaśa cittakṣaṇā darśanamārga ākhyātaḥ
# sems kyi skad cig bcu drug po 'di dag ni mthong ba'i lam ma /
jñeye jñānotpattiparisamāptirekaścittalakṣaṇo veditavyaḥ
# sems kyi skad cig ni shes bya la shes pa 'byung ba yongs su rdzogs par rig par bya'o /
sarvaṃ hi mārgasatyaṃ caturbhiḥ prakārairanugantavyam / vyavasthānataḥ vikalpanataḥ anubhavataḥ paripūritaśca
# chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdul med cing dri ma dang bral ba skyes so zhes gang gsungs pa de ni mthong ba'i lam gyi dbang du mdzad nas gsungs pa ste /
vyavasthānataḥ katamat
# chos la bzod pa rnams kyis ni rdul med pa'o /
yathāsvamadhigamaniṣṭhāprāptāḥ śrāvakādayaḥ
# chos shes pa rnams kyis ni dri ma dang bral ba'o /
tatpṛṣṭhalabdhena jñānena prāpaṇanimittapramāṇaiḥ nāmapadavyañjanakāyaiḥ mārgasatyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti / vikalpanataḥ katamat / abhisamayaprayuktā laukikena jñānena yathāvyavasthānaṃ vikalpoyanto yadabhyasyanti / anubhavataḥ katamat / tathābhyasyanto mayā ?yadādito darśanamārgākhyāṃ lokottarāṃ niṣprapañcāvasthāṃ pratyātmamanubhavati / paripūritaḥ katamat / tadūrdhvaṃ yāmāśrayaparivṛttiṃ paripūrya yāvadadhigamaniṣṭhāṃ prāpnuvanti / tena punaradhigamaniṣṭhāprāptāstatpṛṣṭhalabdhena jñānena nāmapadavyañjanakāyaiḥ mārgasatyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti / yaduktaṃ sūtre virajño vītamalaṃ dharmeṣu dharmacakṣurūdapādi iti / taddarśanamārgamadhikṛtyoktam / tatra dharmakṣāntibhirvirajaḥ dharmajñānairvītamalam parijñayā prahāṇena mārgaśuddhilābhena ca / yaduktaṃ sūtre dṛṣṭadharmā prāptadharmā viditadharmā paryavagāḍhadharmā sarvaiḥ tīrṇakāṃkṣaḥ tīrṇavicikitsaḥ aparapratyayaḥ śāstuḥ śāsano 'nanyaneyaḥ dharmeṣu vaiśāradyaprāpta iti tadapi darśanamārgamadhikṛtyoktam / dṛṣṭadharmā dharmakṣāntibhiḥ / prāptadharmā dharmajñānaiḥ / viditadharmā anvayakṣāntibhiḥ / paryavagāḍhadharmā anvayajñānaiḥ / sarvaiḥ tīrṇakāṃkṣaḥ svādhigame kṣāntijñānaiḥ kāṃkṣābhāvena / tīrṇavicikitsaḥ parādhigame tadavasthasya vimatyabhāvena / aparapratyayaḥ mārgabhāvanāyāṃ na parataḥ svayaṃ kuśalāvarjanena / śāstuḥ śāsane 'nanyaneyaḥ buddhaśāsane  'nyatīrthyairaneyatāmupādāya / dharmeṣu vaiśāradyaprāptaḥ adhigamanāramya paripraśnadharmeṣu alīnacittatāmupādāya / bhāvanāmārgaḥ katamaḥ / darśanamārgādūrdhvaṃ laukiko mārgo lokottaramārgaḥ mṛdumārgo madhyamārgo 'dhimātro mārgaḥ prayogamārgaḥ ānantaryamārgaḥ vimuktimārgaḥ viśeṣamārgaśca / laukiko mārgaḥ katamaḥ / laukikaṃ prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ dvitīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ caturthaṃ dhyānamākāśānattyāyatanaṃ vijñānānantyāyatanamākiñcatyāyatanaṃ naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanaṃ ca / ta ete dhyānārūpyāḥ saṃkleśavyavadānavyavasthāna viśuddhibhirveditavyāḥ / kathaṃ saṃkleśataḥ / catvāryavyākṛtamūlāni tṛṣṇā dṛṣṭirmāno 'vidyā ca / tṛṣṇayā āsvāda saṃkleśena saṃkliśyate / dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭyuttaradhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate / mānena mānottaradhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate
# yongs su shes pa dang spangs pa las kyang lam rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro / / chos mthong ba / / chos thob pa / / chos rig pa / / chos rtogs pa / / som nyi las rgal ba / / the tshom las rgal ba / / gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa / / ston pa'i bstan pa'i bstan pa las gzhan gyis mi bkri ba / / chos rnams la mi 'jigs pa thob pas zhes gang gsungs pa de yang mthong ba'i lam gyi dbang du mdzad nas gsungs pa ste / / chos la bzod pa rnams kyi chos mthong ngo / / chos shes pa rnams kyis chos thob bo / / rjes su rtogs pa'i bzod pa rnams kyis chos rig go / / rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa rnams kyis chos rtogs so / / thams cad kyis rang gis thob pa la som nyi las rgal to / / gzhan gyis thob pa las the tshom las rgal to / / lam sgom pa la gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog go / / mu stegs can rnams kyis mi 'phrogs pa'i phyir ston pa'i bstan pa las gzhan gyis mi bkri'o / / chos rnams la mi 'jigs pa thob pa ni yongs su dri ba'i chos dang lung du bstan pa'i chos ni 'dir chos su 'dod de / / sems zhum pa med pa'i phyir de la mi 'jigs pa thob bo / / bsgom pa'i lam gang zhe na / / mthong ba'i lam las gong du gyur pa 'jig rten pa'i lam dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam dang lam chung ngu dang lam 'bring dang lam chen po dang sbyor ba'i lam dang bar chad med pa'i lam dang rnam par grol ba'i lam dang khyad par gyi lam mo / / 'jig rten pa'i lam gang zhe na / / 'jig rten pa'i bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa dang gsum pa dang bsam gtan bzhi pa dang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang ci yang med pa'i skye mched dang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched de / / bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa de dag kyang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang rnam par gzhag pa dang rnam par dag pas rig par bya'o / / kun nas nyon mongs pas ji lta bu zhe na / / lung du ma bstan pa'i rtsa ba bzhi po / / sred pa dang lta ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa'o / / sred pas ni ro myong ba'i kun nas nyon mongs pas kun nas nyon mongs so / / lta bas ni lta ba shas ches ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs so / / nga rgyal gyis ni nga rgyal shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs so /
avidyayā vicikitsottaradhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate
# ma rig pas ni the tshom shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs so /
tathā ca saṃkliṣṭacetasāṃ rūpārūpyāvacarāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ pravarttante
# de ltar sems kun nas nyon mongs pa dag la gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams 'byung ngo /
kathaṃ vyavadānataḥ
# rnam par byang bas ji lta bu zhe na /
śuddhakā dhyānārūpyāḥ kuśalatvād vyavadātā ityucyante
# dag pa pa'i bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa rnams kyang dge ba'i phyir rnam par byang ba zhes bya'o /
kathaṃ vyavasthānataḥ / aṅgavyavasthānataḥ samāpattivyavasthānataḥ mātrāvyavasthānataḥ saṃjñākaraṇavyavasthānaśca
# rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na / / yan lag rnam par gzhag pa dang snyoms par 'jug pa rnam par gzhag pa dang tshad rnam par gzhag pa dang ming du gdags pa rnams par gzhag pas so /
kathamaṅgavyavasthānataḥ
# yan lag rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ pañcāṅgam / pañcāṅgāni vitarko vicāraḥ prītiḥ sukhaṃ cittaikāgratā ca
# bsam gtan dang po la yan lag lnga ste / / yan lag lnga ni rtog pa dang dpyod pa dang dga' ba dang bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid do /
dvitīyaṃ dhyānaṃ caturaṅgam / catvāryaṅgāni adhyātmasaṃprasādaḥ prītiḥ sukhaṃ cittaikāpratā ca / tṛtīyaṃ dhyānaṃ pañcāṅgam / pañcāṅgāni upekṣā smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyaṃ sukhaṃ cittaikāgratā ca
# bsam gtan gnyis pa la yan lag bzhi ste / / yan lag bzhi ni nang rab tu dang ba dang dga' ba dang bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid do / / bsam gtan gsum pa la yan lag lnga ste; yal lag lnga ni btang snyoms dang dran pa dang shes bzhin dang bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid do /
caturthaṃ dhyānaṃ caturaṅgam / catvāryaṅgāni upekṣāpariśuddhiḥ smṛtipariśuddhiḥ aduḥkhāsukhā vedanā cittaikāgratā ca / pratipakṣāṅgamupādāya anuśaṃsāṅgamupādāya tadubhayāśrayasvabhāvāṅgaṃ copādāya ārupyeṣvaṅgavyavasthānaṃ nāsti / śamathaikarasatāmupādāya
# bsam gtan bzhi pa la yan lag bzhi ste / / yan lag bzhi ni btang snyoms yongs su dag pa dang dran pa yongs su dag pa dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid do / / gnyen po'i yan lag dang phan yon gyi yan lag dang de gnyi ga'i gnas kyi rang bzhin gyi yan lag gi phyir ro / / gzugs med pa rnams na ni zhi gnas su ro gcig pa nyid kyi phyir yan lag rnam par gzhag pa med do; /
kathaṃ samāpattivyavasthānataḥ
# snyoms par 'jug pa rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
saptabhirmanaskāraiḥ prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ samāpadyate / evaṃ yāvannaivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanaṃ ca / sapta manaskārāḥ katame
# yid la byed pa bdun gyis bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par 'jug ste / / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi bar du yang de bzhin no / / yid la byed pa bdun gang zhe na /
lakṣaṇaprati saṃvedī manaskāraḥ ādhimokṣikaḥ prāvivejaḥ ratisaṃgrāhakaḥ mīmāṃsakaḥ prayoganiṣṭhaḥ prayoganiṣṭhāphalaśca  manaskāraḥ
# mtshan nyid rab tu rig pa'i yid la byed pa dang mos pa las byung ba dang rab tu dben pa las byung ba dang dga' ba sdud pa dang dpyod pa dang sbyor ba'i mtha' dang sbyor ba'i mtha'i 'bras bu yid la byed pa'o /
kathaṃ mātrāvyavasthānataḥ / prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ suduparibhāvitaṃ madhyaparibhāvitamadhimātraparibhāvitaśca
# tshad rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na / / bsam gtan dang po la chung ngur yongs su bsgoms pa dang 'bring dang chen por yongs su bsgoms pa'o /
[tadyathā] prathamaṃ dhyānametraṃ śiṣṭāni dhyānānyārūpyāśca / mṛdumadhyādhimātraparibhāvitasya prathamasya dhyānasya phalaṃ trividhā prathamā dhyānopapattiḥ
# bsam gtan dang po la ji lta bar bsam gtan lhag ma rnams dang gzugs med pa rnams kyang de bzhin no / / bsam gtan dang po la chung ngu dang 'bring dang cher yongs su bsgoms pa'i 'bras bu ni bsam gtan dang po'i skye ba gsum mo; /
yathā prathamasya dhyānasya evaṃ śiṣṭānāṃ dhyānānāṃ trividhā dhyānopapattiḥ / ārūpyeṣu sthānāntarābhāvamupādāyopapattibhedo nāsti / tatra mṛdumadhyādhimātraparibhāvitatvādārūpyāṇāmupapattāvuccanīcatā hīnapraṇītatā prajñāyate
# bsam gtan dang po la ji lta bar bsam gtan lhag ma rnams kyi yang de bzhin te / / bsam gtan gyi skye ba rnam pa gsum gsum mo / / gzugs med pa na ni gnas gzhan med pa'i phyir skye ba tha dad pa yang med do / / de na chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen por yongs su bsgoms pas gzugs med pa rnams su skye ba mthon po dang dma' ba dang ngan pa dang bzang por mngon no /
kathaṃ saṃjñākaraṇavyavasthānataḥ
# ming du gdags pa rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
prathamadhyānasaṃgṛhītānyāvataḥ samādhīn buddhabodhisattvāḥ samāpadyante / teṣāṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhā nāmābhijñā api na bhavanti
# bsam gtan dang pos bsdus pa'i ting nge 'dzin ji snyed la / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi ming yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyis mi shes so /
yathā prathamadhyānasaṃgṛhītānevamavaśiṣṭadhyānasaṃgṛhītānyaduta dhyānapāramitāṃ niśritya
# bsam gtan dang pos bsdus pa ji lta bar bsam gtan lhag ma rnams dang gzugs med pas bsdus pa rnams kyang de bzhin te / / 'di ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brten nas so /
kathaṃ viśuddhitaḥ
# rnam par dag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
prāntakoṭikaṃ prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ yāvannaiva saṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanaṃ viśuddhirityucyate
# rab kyi mtha'i cha las byung ba bsam gtan dang po nas 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi bar du rnam par dag pa zhes bya'o /
lokottaro mārgaḥ katamaḥ / bhāvanāmārge duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgajñānāni dharmajñānānvayapakṣyāṇi taiśca saṃprayuktaḥ samādhiḥ prathamaṃ vā dhyānaṃ yāvadākiñcanyāyatanaṃ naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanaṃ, laukikameva aparisphuṭaṃ saṃjñāpracāratāmupādāya
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gang zhe na / / bsgom pa'i lam la sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba dang; 'gog pa dang lam shes pa rnams te / / chos shes pa dang rjes su rtogs pa shes pa'i phyogs dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang bsam gtan dang po nas ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi bar du'o / / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched ni 'du shes kyi rgyu ba yongs su mi gsal ba'i phyir 'jig rten pa nyid de /
tata ścānimittamityucyate
# de'i phyir mtshan ma med pa zhes bya'o /
yathoktaṃ bhagavatā yāvadeva saṃjñāsamāpattiḥ tāvadājñāprativedha iti / nirodhasamāpattirlokottarā manuṣyeṣvabhinirhiyate / manuṣyeṣva bhinirhṛtā manuṣyeṣurūpadhātau vā saṃmukhīkriyate
# bcom ldan 'das kyis ji skad du / / ji tsam du 'du shes kyi snyoms par 'jug pa de tsam du kun shes par rtogs so zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ste / / mi rnams kyi nang du mngon par bsgrub bo / / mi rnams kyi nang du mngon par grub nas / / mi rnams kyi nang du'am / / gzugs kyi khams su mngon du byed do /
ārūpyeṣva syāḥ saṃmukhībhāvo nāsti
# gzugs med pa'i khams rnams su ni 'di mngon du 'gyur ba med de /
śāntavimokṣavipākavihārīṇāṃ tadyatnānārambhatāmupādāya / mṛdumārgaḥ katamaḥ
# zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa'i rnam par smin pas gnas pa rnams ni de la 'bad pa'i rtsom pa med pa'i phyir ro / / lam chung ngu gang zhe na /
mṛdumṛdurmṛdumadhyo mṛdvadhimātraśca yena traidhātukāvacarāṇā kleśānāṃ bhūmau bhūmāvadhimātrādhimātramadhimātramadhyamadhimātrāmṛduṃ kleśaprakāra prajahāti
# chung ngu'i dang chung ngu'i 'bring po dang chung ngu'i chen po ste / / gang gis sa dang sa na khams gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chen po'i chen po dang chen po'i 'bring po dang chen po'i chung ngu spong ba'o /
madhyo mārgaḥ katamaḥ
# lam 'bring po gang zhe na /
madhyamṛdurmadhyamadhyo madhyādhimātraśca yena traidhātukāvacarāṇāṃ kleśānāṃ bhūmau bhūmau madhyādhimātraṃ madhyamadhyaṃ madhyamṛduṃ kleśaprakāraṃ prajahāti / adhimātro mārgaḥ katamaḥ
# 'bring po'i chung ngu dang 'bring po'i 'bring po dang 'bring po'i chen po ste / / gang gis sa dang sa na khams gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa 'bring po'i chen po dang; 'bring po'i 'bring po dang 'bring po'i chung du spong pa'o / / lam chen po gang zhe na /
adhimātramṛduradhimātramadhyo 'dhimātrādhimātraśca yena traidhātukāvacarāṇāṃ kleśānāṃ bhūmau bhūmau mṛdvadhimātraṃ mṛdumadhyaṃ mṛdumṛduṃ kleśaprakāraṃ prajahāti
# chen po'i chung ngu dang chen po'i 'bring po dang chen po'i chen po ste / / gang gis sa dang sa na khams su gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chung ngu'i chen po dang chung ngu'i 'bring po dang chung ngu'i chung ngu spong ba'o /
prayogamārgaḥ katamaḥ
# sbyor ba'i lam gang zhe na /
yena kleśaṃ prajahāti
# gang gis nyon mongs pa spong ba'o /
ānantaryamārgaḥ katamaḥ
# bar chad med pa'i lam gang zhe na /
yasyānantaraṃ nirantaraḥ kleśaḥ prahīṇo bhavati
# gang gi 'og tu bar chad med par nyon mongs pa spong bar 'gyur ba'o /
vimuktimārgaḥ katamaḥ
# rnam par grol ba'i lam gang zhe na /
yena prahīṇe kleśe vimuktiṃ sākṣātkaroti
# gang gis nyon mongs pa spongs nas rnam par grol ba mngon du byed pa'o /
viśeṣamārgaḥ katamaḥ
# khyad par gyi lam gang zhe na /
tadanyasya kleśaprakārasya prayogānantaryavimuktimārgāḥ viśeṣamārgaḥ / api khalu kleśaprahāṇaprayogaṃ nirākṛtya dharmacintāyāṃ vā prayuktasya dharmavihāre vā samāpattiviśeṣe vā yo mārgaḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa de las gzhan pa la sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa dang rnam par grol ba'i lam ni khyad par gyi lam mo / / yang nyon mongs pa spong ba'i sbyor ba bsal nas / / chos sems pa'am / / zhugs pa'i chos la gnas pa'am / / snyoms par 'jug pa'i khyad par gyi lam gang yin pa'o /
api khalu vaiśeṣikān guṇānabhinirharato vā yo mārgaḥ / mārgabhāvanā katamā / pratilaṃbhabhāvanā niṣevaṇabhāvanā nirdhāvanabhāvanā pratipakṣabhāvanā ca / pratilambhabhāvanā katamā
# yang yon tan khyad par can rnams mngon par bsgrub pa'am / / gnas pa'i lam gang yin pa'o / / lam bsgom pa gang zhe na / / thob par bya ba'i phyir bsgom pa dang bsten pa'i bsgom pa dang bsal ba'i phyir bsgom pa dang gnyen po bsgom pa'o / / thob par bya ba'i phyir bsgom pa gang zhe na /
anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāmutpādāya yā bhāvanā / niṣevaṇabhāvanā katamā
# dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams bskyed pa'i phyir bsgom pa'o / / bsten pa'i bsgom pa gang zhe na /
utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye asaṃmoṣāya bhūyobhāvāya vṛddhivipulatāyai yā bhāvanā / nirdhāvanabhāvanā katamā
# dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams gnas pa dang mi nyams pa dang phyir zhing 'byung ba dang 'phel ba dang yangs par bya ba'i phyir gang bsgom pa'o / / bsal ba'i phyir bsgom pa gang zhe na /
utpannānāṃ pāpakānāmakuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāya yā bhāvanā
# sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spang ba'i phyir gang bsgom pa'o /
pratipakṣabhāvanā katamā
# gnyen po bsgom pa gang zhe na /
