anutpannānāṃ pāpakānāmakuśakunāṃ dharmāṇāmanutpādāya  yā bhāvanā / api khalu mārga utpadyamānaḥ svāṃ vāsanāmava sthāpayati sā pratilambhabhāvanā / sa eva saṃmukhībhūto bhāvanāṃ gacchati sā niṣevaṇabhāvanā
# sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams mi bskyed pa'i phyir gang bsgom pa'o / / yang lam skye ba na rang gi bag chags 'jog pa de ni thob par bya ba'i phyir bsgom pa'o / / de nyid mngon du gyur nas bsgom par 'gyur ba de ni bsten pa'i bsgom pa'o /
svamāvaraṇaṃ vijahāti sā nirdhāvanabhāvanā / vihīna ścāvaraṇamāyatyāmanutpattidharmatāyāmavasthāpayati sā pratipakṣabhāvanā / api khalu caturvidhaḥ pratipakṣaḥ vidūṣaṇāpratipakṣaḥ prahāṇapratipakṣaḥ ādhārapratipakṣaḥ dūrībhāvapratipakṣaśca pratipakṣabhāvanetyucyate
# rang gi sgrib pa spong ba de ni bsal ba'i phyir bsgom pa'o / / sgrib pa spangs nas kyang phyi ma la mi skye ba'i chos can du 'jog pa de ni gnyen po bsgom pa'o / / yang gnyen po rnam pa bzhi ste / / rnam par sun 'byin pa gnyen po dang spong ba gnyen po dang rten gnyen po dang thag bsring ba gnyen po ni gnyen po bsgom pa zhes bya'o /
vidūṣaṇāpratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ
# rnam par sun 'byin pa gnyen po gang zhe na /
sāsraveṣu saṃskāreṣvādīnavadarśanam / prahāṇapratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams la nyes dmigs su blta ba'o / / spong ba gnyen po gang zhe na /
prayogāntaryamārgaḥ / ādharapratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ
# sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa'i lam mo / / rten gnyen po gang zhe na /
vimuktimārgaḥ
# rnam par grol ba'i lam mo /
dūrībhāvapratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ
# thag bsring ba gnyen po gang zhe na /
tadu parimo mārgaḥ / api khalu vastuparīkṣāmārgaḥ vyāvasāyiko mārgaḥ samādhiparikarmamārgaḥ abhisamayaprāyogiko mārgaḥ abhisamayaśliṣṭo mārgaḥ abhisamayamārgaḥ viśuddhinairyāṇiko mārgaḥ niśrayendriyabhinno mārgaḥ śikṣātrayapariśodhano mārgaḥ sarvaguṇanirhārako mārgaḥ mārgasaṃgrahamārgaśca mārga ityucyate / sa punareṣa yathākramaṃ saptatriṃśadabodhipakṣā dharmāḥ catasraḥ pratipadaḥ catvāri dharmapadāni śamathaai vipaśyanā triṇī cendriyāṇī
# de'i gong ma'i lam mo / / yang dngos po la yongs su rtog pa'i lam dang rtsol ba las byung ba'i lam dang ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyong bar byed pa'i lam dang mngon par rtogs pa la sbyor ba'i lam dang mngon par rtogs pa dang 'brel ba'i lam dang mngon par rtogs pa'i lam dang rnam par dag par nges par 'byin pa'i lam dang gnas dang dbang pos tha dad pa'i lam dang bslab pa gsum yongs su sbyong ba'i lam dang yon tan thams cad sgrub par byed pa'i lam dang lam sdud pa'i lam ni lam zhes bya ste / / de yang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun dang lam bzhi dang chos kyi gnas bzhi dang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong dang dbang po gsum dang go rims bzhin no /
smṛtyupasthānānāmālamvanaṃ svabhāvaḥ sahāyaḥ bhāvanā bhāvanāphalañca veditavyam
# dran pa gnye bar gzhag pa rnams ni / / dmigs pa dang ngo bo nyid dang grogs dang bsgom pa dang bsgoms pa'i 'bras bur rig par bya'o /
yathā smṛtyupasthānānāmevamavaśiṣṭānāṃ bodhipakṣāṇām / smṛtyupasthānānāmālambanaṃ katamat / kāyo vedanā cittaṃ dharmāḥ / api khalvātmāśrayavastu ātmopabhogavastu ātmavastu ātmasaṃkleśavyavadānavastu ca
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la ji lta bar byang chub kyi phyogs lhag ma rnams la'ang de bzhin no / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na / / lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos so / / yang bdag gi gnas kyi dngos po dang bdag gi longs spyod kyi gzhi dang bdag gi dngos po dang bdag kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i dngos po'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ / prajñā smṛtiśca / sahāyaḥ katamaḥ / tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / bhāvanā katamā
# ngo bo nyid gang zhe na / / shes rab dang dran pa'o / / grogs gang zhe na / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / bsgom pa gang zhe na /
adhyātmaṃ kāyādiṣu kāyādyanupaśyanā / yathā adhyātmamevaṃ bahirdhā adhyātmavahirdhā
# nang gi lus la sogs pa la lus la sogs pa'i rjes su lta ba'o / / nang la ji lta bar phyi dang nang dang phyi la yang de bzhin no /
adhyātmaṃ kāyaḥ katamaḥ
# nang gi lus gang zhe na /
yānyasmin kāye ādhyatmikāni rūpīṇyāyatanāni
# lus gang la nang gi skye mched gzugs can dag gang yin pa'o /
bahirdhākāyaḥ katamaḥ
# phyi'i lus gang zhe na /
bahirdhā rūpīṇyāyatanāni / adhyātmavahirddhā kāyaḥ katamaḥ
# phyi'i skye mched gzugs can rnams so / / nang dang phyi'i lus gang zhe na /
ādhyātmikāyatanasaṃbaddhāni  bāhyānyāyatanāni / indriyādhiṣṭhānāni pārasāntānikāni cādhyātmikāni rūpīṇyāyatayāni
# nang gi skye mched dang 'brel ba'i phyi'i skye mched dbang po'i gnas rnams dang gzhan gyi rgyud la yod pa'i nang gi skye mched gzugs can rnams so /
kāye kāyānupaśyanā katamā
# lus la lus kyi rjes su lta ba gang zhe na /
yā vikalpapratibimbakāyena prakṛtibimbakāyasya samatāpaśyanā / adhyātmaṃ vedanā katamā / adhyātmaṃ kāyamupādāyotpannā vedanā / bahirddhā vedanā katamā / bahirddhā kāyamupādayotpannā vedanā / adhyātmabahirddhā vedanā katamā / adhyātmābahirddhākāyamupādāyotpannāvedanā
# rnam par rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan gyi lus dang rang bzhin gyi gzugs kyi lus la mnyam pa nyid du lta ba gang yin pa'o / / nang gi tshor ba gang zhe na / / nang gi lus la brten nas byung ba'i tshor ba'o / / phyi'i tshor ba gang zhe na / / phyi'i lus la brten nas byung ba'i tshor ba'o / / nang dang phyi'i tshor ba gang zhe na / / nang dang phyi'i lus la brten nas byung ba'i tshor ba'o /
yathā vedanā evaṃ cittaṃ dharmāḥ
# tshor ba la ji lta bar sems dang chos la yang de bzhin no /
yathā kāye kāyānupaśyanā evaṃ vedanādiṣu vedanādyanupaśyanā yathāyogaṃ veditavyāḥ
# lus la lus kyi rjes su lta ba ji lta bar tshor ba la sogs pa la tshor ba la sogs pa'i rjes su lta ba yang de bzhin te ci rigs su sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
api khalu bhāvanā chando vīryaṃ vyāyāma utsāhaḥ utsūḍhiraprativāṇiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyaṃ apramādaśca / chandabhāvanā amanasikaropakleśapratipakṣeṇa / vīryabhāvanā kausīdyopakleśapratipakṣeṇa / vyāyāmabhāvanā layauddhatyopakleśapratipakṣeṇa / utsāhabhāvanā cetaso 'līnatvopakleśapratipakṣeṇa
# yang bsgom pa ni 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang rtsol ba dang; spro ba dang ma than pa dang phyir nur ba med pa dang dran pa dang shes bzhin dang bag yod pa'o / / yid la mi byed pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por 'dun pa bsgom mo / / le lo nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / bying ba dang rgod pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por rtsol ba bsgom mo / / sems zhum pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por spro ba bsgom mo /
utsūḍhibhāvanā viṣādaparisravaparikhedopakleśapratipakṣeṇa / aprativāṇibhāvanā kuśalapakṣeṇa alpamātra saṃtuṣṭyupakleśapratipakṣeṇa / smṛtibhāvanā bhagavataḥ śāsane saṃmoṣopakleśapratipakṣeṇa / saṃprajanyabhāvanā āpattivipratisāropakleśapratipakṣeṇa / apramādabhāvanā kuśaleṣu nikṣiptadhuratopakleśapratipakṣeṇa
# gnod pas yongs su skyo ba nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por ma than pa bsgom mo / / cung zad tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por phyir nur pa med pa bsgom mo / / gdams ngag brjed pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por dran pa bsgom mo / / ltung bas yid la gcags pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por shes bzhin bsgom mo / / brtson pa 'dor ba nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por bag yod pa bsgom mo /
bhāvanāphalaṃ katamat
# bsgoms pa'i 'bras bu gang zhe na /
catu rviparyāsaprahāṇaṃ catuḥ satyāvatāraḥ kāyādivisaṃyogaḥ
# phyin ci log spong ba dang bden pa la 'jug pa dang lus la sogs pa dang bral ba'o /
catuḥ samyakprahāṇānāmālambanaṃ katamat
# yang dag par spong ba rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
utpannānutpannavipakṣapratipakṣāḥ
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po skyes pa dang ma skyes pa'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ
# ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
vyāyāmaḥ / sahāyaḥ katamaḥ / tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / bhāvanā katamā
# brtson 'grus so / / grogs gang zhe na / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / bsgom pa gang zhe na / / gang 'dun pa skyed do / / 'bad do /
taduktaṃ sūtre chandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryamārabhate cittaṃ pragṛṇhāti cittaṃ pradadhāti / ityevamādibhiḥ padaistatravīryāśrayabhāvanā paridīpitā / āśrayaḥ chandaḥ / vīryamudyogaḥ
# brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / sems rab tu 'dzin to; / / rab tu 'jog go zhes bya ba ste / / 'di ni brtson 'grus bsgom pa gnas dang bcas pa'o / / gnas ni 'dun pa'o / / 'bad pa ni brtson 'grus so /
śamathagragrahopekṣānimittamanasikāreṣu chandaṃ janayati layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇe vīryamārabhate evaṃ tadanantaraṃ  cittaṃ pragṛṇhāti pradadhātīpratyucyate / bhāvanā phalaṃ katamat / aśeṣavipakṣahāniḥ pratipakṣapratilambhaḥ pratipakṣavṛddhiśca
# zhi gnas dang rab tu 'dzin pa dang btang snyoms kyi mtshan ma yid la byed pa la brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / bying ba dang; rgod pa sel ba yang brtson 'grus nyid de / / 'di ltar de'i 'og tu sems rab tu 'dzin pa dang rab tu 'jog pa smos so / / 'bras bu gang zhe na / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma lus par nyams pa dang gnyen po thob pa dang 'phel ba'o /
taducyate bhāvanāphalam / caturṛddhipādānāmālambanaṃ katamat / niṣpajñena samādhinā yatkaraṇīyaṃ kṛtyam / svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na / / ting nge 'dzin gyis grub pa'i bya ba'o / / ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
samādhiḥ / sahāyaḥ katamaḥ / chandovīryaṃ cittaṃ mīmāṃsā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# ting nge 'dzin to / / grogs gang zhe na / / 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
chandasamādhiḥ katamaḥ / yatsatkṛtya prayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na / / gang gus par sbyor ba la brten nas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
vīryasamadhiḥ katamaḥ
# brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
yatsātatya prayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# gang rgyun du sbyor ba la brten nas / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
cittasamādhiḥ katamaḥ / pūrvasamādhibhāvanāmāgamya svarasena spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# sems kyi ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na / / gang sngon ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pa la brten nas / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ katamaḥ
# dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
deśanādharmaśravaṇamāgamya pratyātmaṃ pratisaṃkhyāya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# gang gzhan gyis bstan nas chos rab tu rnams par 'byed pa la brten nas / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
punaḥ chandasamādhiḥ yat chandaṃ janayan spṛśati cittasyaikagratām
# yang 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang 'dun pa bskyed pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
vīryasamādhiḥ yat vīryamārapramāṇaḥ spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang 'bad cing brtson 'grus rtsom pa na / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
cittasamādhiḥ yat cittaṃ pradadhat spṛśati cittasyaigratām
# sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang sems rab tu 'jog pa na / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ yat cittaṃ pragṛṇhan spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām / bhāvanā katamā
# dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang sems rab tu 'dzin pa na / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o / / bsgom pa gang zhe na /
aṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāmabhyāsaḥ
# spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad goms par byed pa ste /
katame aṣṭau / chandaḥ vyāyāmaḥ śraddhā praśrabdhiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyaṃ cetanā upekṣā ca
# spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad ni / / 'dun pa dang rtsol ba dang dad pa dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang dran pa dang shes bzhin dang sems pa dang btang snyoms so /
te punaraṣṭau samāsataścaturdhā saṃgṛhyante
# 'di dag brgyad yin du zin kyang bzhir 'gyur te /
vyāyasāyikaḥ anugrāhakaḥ aupanivandhikaḥ prātipakṣikaśca
# 'bad pa dang phan 'dogs pa dang nye bar 'dogs pa dang gnyen po'o /
chandavīryacittamīmāṃsābhāvanā punardvividhā / nidānaṃ saṃkṣepavikṣepa parivarjanabhāvana alīnatvāvikṣepatadubhayāśrayānukūlabhāvanā ca
# yang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa rnams kyi sdud pa dang g yeng ba gzhi dang bcas par yongs su spangs pa dang zhum pa med pa dang g yeng ba med pa dang de gnyi ga'i gnas dang mthun pa bsgom mo /
phalaṃ katamat
# 'bras bu gang zhe na /
kuśalasamādhiparikarmataḥ yathākarmaṃ dharmābhijñā yathācittamabhijñāpradarśanam / api ca teṣu teṣu dharmeṣu adhigamaḥ prātiḥ karmaṇyatā vaśitā kāritraṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nānāvidhānāmṛdudhyādīnāṃ vastūnāṃ niṣpādanamadhiguṇānāṃ nirhāraśca / pañcendriyāṇāmālambanaṃ katamat
# de ltar ting nge 'dzin legs par yongs su spyang ba byas na / / chos mngon par shes par bya ba gang dang gang mngon du bya bar 'dod pa de dang de la sems mngon par gtod pa de rang rang gi gnas kyi chos rnams la mngon du 'gyur ba'i skal ba can du 'gyur ro / / dbang po rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
catvāryāryasatyāni
# 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams so /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ / śraddhā vīrya smṛtiḥ samādhiḥ prajñā ca / sahāya katamaḥ / tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / bhāvanā katamā
# ngo bo nyid gang zhe na / / dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab po / / grogs gang zhe na / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / bsgom pa gang zhe na /
yat śraddhendriyeṇa satyeṣu abhisaṃpratyayasamutthānaṃ prayogabhāvanā
# dad pa'i dbang po ni bden pa rnams la mngon par yid ches pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
vīryendriyeṇa satyeṣu utpannābhisaṃpratyayasyābhisaṃbodhyarthaṃ vyāyāmasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā
# mngon par yid ches pa skyes pa ni bden pa mngon par rtogs par bya ba'i phyir spro ba'i tshul gyis brtson 'grus bsgom par 'gyur ro /
smṛtīndriyeṇa satyeṣu ārabdhavīryasya smṛtisaṃprayogā dharmasaṃmopasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni bden pa rnams la nye bar gnas pa'i dran pa mi brjed pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
samādhīndriyeṇa satyeṣu saṃprayukta smṛteḥ cittaikāgratāsamutthānaprayogabhāvanā
# bden pa rnams la dran pa nye ba gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni sems rtse gcig pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
prajñendriyeṇa satyeṣu samāhitacittasya pravicayasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā / bhāvanāphalaṃ katamat / satyābhisamayasamutthānataḥ uṣmagatamūrdhaparikarmataśca kṣāntilaukikāgradharmanirhāraḥ
# bden pa rnams la mnyam par gzhag pa'i shes rab ni rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro / / 'bras bu gang zhe na / / bden pa myur du mngon par rtogs par byed pa dang dro bar gyur pa dang rtse mo dang bzod pa dang chos kyi mchog rnams bsgrub pa'o /
yathā pañcendriyāṇi tathā pañca balāni / eṣāṃ viśeṣaḥ taiḥ vipakṣāntarāyanirllekho 'navamudyateti balānītyucyante
# dbang po rnams la ji lta bar stobs rnams la yang de bzhin no; / / 'di ni bye brag yin te / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs nges par bsrabs pas / / mi brdzi ba'i phyir stobs rnams so /
sapta bodhyaṅgānāmālambanaṃ katamat
# byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ yathābhūtatā
# 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag gi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ
# ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
smṛtiḥ dharmavicayaḥ vīryaṃ prītiḥ praśrabdhiḥ samādhiḥ upekṣā ca / smṛtiḥ saṃniśrayāṅgam
# dran pa dang chos rnam par 'byed pa dang brtson 'grus dang dga' ba dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms so / / dran pa ni gnas kyi yan lag go /
dharmavicayaḥ svabhāvāṅgam
# chos rnam par 'byed pa ni ngo bo nyid kyi yan lag go /
vīryaṃ niryāṇāṅgam / prītiḥ anuśaṃsāṅgam
# brtson 'grus ni nges par 'byung ba'i yan lag go / / dga' ba ni phan yon gyi yan lag go /
praśrabdhiḥ / samādhiḥ upekṣā cāsaṃkleśāṅgam / asaṃkleśataḥ asaṃkleśāśrayataḥ asaṃkleśasvabhāvataśca / sahāyaḥ katamaḥ / tatsaṃprayuktāśrittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / bhāvanā katamā
# shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i yan lag ste / / gang gis kyang kun nas nyin mongs par mi 'gyur ba dang gang du yang kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ba dang kun nas nyin mongs pa gang yang med pa'o / / grogs gang zhe na / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / bsgom pa gang zhe na /
vivekaniśritaṃ virāganiśritaṃ nirodhaniśritaṃ vyavasargapariṇataṃ smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgam
# dran pa yang dag byung chub kyi yan lag / / dben pa la gnas pa / / 'dod chags dang bral ba la gnas pa / / 'gog pa la gnas pa / / rnam par spong bas yongs su bsgyur ba bsgom pa'o /
yathā smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgaṃ tathā yāvat upekṣāsaṃbodhyaṅgam
# dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag ji lta bar btang snyoms yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag gi bar du yang de bzhin no /
ebhiḥ catubhiḥ padairyathākramaṃ catuḥsatyālambanābodhyaṅgabhāvanā paridīpitā / bhāvanāphalaṃ katamat
# 'dis ni bden pa la dmigs pa byang chub kyi yan lag bsgom pa yongs su bstan to / / 'bras bu gang zhe na /
darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇam / aṣṭānāmāryamārgāṅgānāmālambanaṃ katamat
# mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa'o / / lam gyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
taduttarakālaṃ caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ yathābhūtatā
# de'i 'og tu 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams kyi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ / samyagdṛṣṭiḥ samyakkarmmāntaḥ samyagājīvaḥ samyagvyāyāmaḥ samyaksmṛtiḥ samyaksamādhiśca / samyagadṛṣṭiuḥ paricchedāṅgam / samyaksaṃkalpa parasaṃprāpaṇāṅgam
# ngo bo nyid gang zhe na / / yan lag brgyad de / / yang dag pa'i lta ba dang yang dag pa'i rtog pa dang yang dag pa'i ngag dang yang dag pa'i las kyi mtha' dang yang dag pa'i 'tsho ba dang yang dag pa'i rtsol ba dang yang dag pa'i dran pa dang yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin to / / yang dag pa'i lta ba ni yongs su gcod pa'i yan lag go / / yang dag pa'i rtog pa ni gzhan go bar byed pa'i yan lag go /
samyagvākkarmāntājīvāḥ parasaṃpratyapāṅgam / darśanaśīlājīvaviśuddhitāmupādāya
# yang dag pa'i ngag dang las kyi mtha' dang 'tsho ba ni gzhan yid ches par byed pa'i yan lag ste / / lta ba dang tshul khrims dang 'tsho ba rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro /
samyagvyāyāmaḥ kleśāvaraṇaviśodhanāṅgam / samyaksamādhiḥ vaiśeṣikaguṇāvaraṇa viśodhanāṅgam / sahāyaḥ katamaḥ / tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikādharmāḥ / bhāvanā katamā / bhāvanā tu bodhyaṅgavat / bhāvanā phalaṃ katamat
# yang dag pa'i rtsol ba ni nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i yan lag go / / yang dag pa'i dran pa ni nye ba'i nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par spyod pa'i yan lag go / / yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni yon tan khyad par can la sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i yan lag go / / grogs gang zhe na / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / bsgom pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag bzhin no / / 'bras bu gang zhe na /
paricchedaḥ parasaṃprāpaṇaṃ parasaṃpratyayaḥ kleśāvaraṇaviśodhanamupakleśāvaraṇaviśodhanaṃ vaiśeṣikaguṇāvaraṇaviśodhanaṃ ca
# yongs su gcod pa dang gzhan go bar byed pa dang; gzhan yid ches par byed pa dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa dang yon tan khyad par can la sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'o /
catasraḥ pratipadaḥ katamāḥ / duḥkhā pratipad dhandhābhijñā duḥkhā pratipat kṣiprābhijñā sukhā pratipad dhandhābhijñā sukhā pratipat kṣiprābhijñā
# lam bzhi gang zhe na / / mngon par shes pa bul la dka' ba dang mngon par shes pa myur la dka' ba dang mngon par shes pa bul la sla ba dang mngon par shes pa myur la sla ba ste /
prathamā mṛdvindriyāṇāmanupalabdhamauladhyānam
# dang po ni dbang po rtul po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan ma thob pa'i'o /
dvitīyā tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmanupalabdhamauladhyānam
# gnyis pa ni dbang po rnon po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan ma thob pa'i'o /
tṛtīyā mṛdvindriyāṇāmupalabhamauladhyānam
# gsum pa ni dbang po rtul po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan thob pa'i'o /
caturthī tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmupalabdhamaula dhyānam / catvāri dharmapadāni katamāni
# bzhi pa ni dbang po rnon po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan thob pa'i'o / / chos kyi gnas bzhi gang zhe na /
alobhādveṣāṇāṃ samyak smṛtiḥ samyak samādhiḥ / alobhādveṣāṇāmadhiśīlaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ / samyaksmṛtānāmadhicittaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ / samyaksamādhitānāmadhiprajñaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ
# brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa dang yang dag pa'i dran pa dang yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin te / / brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa ni lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rnams par sbyong ba'o / / yang dag pa'i dran pa ni lhag pa'i sems so / / yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni lhag pa'i shes rab bo /
śamathaḥ katamaḥ
# zhi gnas gang zhe na /
adhyātmaṃ cittasya upanibandhaḥ sthāpanā saṃsthāpanā avasthāpanā upasthāpanā damanaṃ śamanaṃ vyupaśamanam ekotīkaraṇaṃ samādhānaṃ ca / vipaśyanā katamā
# 'di lta ste / / nang nyid la sems 'jog pa dang rgyun du 'jog pa dang blan te 'jog pa dang nye bar 'jog pa dang 'dul bar byed pa dang zhi bar byed pa dang rnam par zhi bar byed pa dang rtse gcig tu byed pa dang mnyam par 'jog pa'o / / lhag mthong gang zhe na / / 'di lta ste /
yā dharmān vicinoti pravivinoti parivitarkkayati parimīmāṃsamāpataye / ca kāma pratipakṣadauṣṭhulyanimittasaṃyojanataḥ kāmābhibhavānāṃ viparyāsataḥ aviparyastacittasyāvasthāpanataśca / api khalu śamathavipaśyanāmāgamya catvāro mārgāḥ
# chos rnams la rnam par 'byed pa dang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa dang yongs su rnam par rtog pa dang yongs su dpyod par byed pa ste / / gnas ngan len dang mtshan ma'i gnyen po nyid dang phyin ci log las 'byin pa dang phyin ci log ma yin pa la sems 'jog pa'i phyir ro / / yang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong la brten nas lam bzhir 'gyur te /
ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī na vipaśyanāyāḥ / tatprakāraṃ śamathaṃ niśritya vipaśyanāmāpanā
# la la ni zhi gnas thob pa yin gyi / / lhag mthong ni ma thob pa ste / / de zhi gnas la brten nas lhag mthong la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ vipaśyanāyā lābhī na śamathasya / tatprakārāṃ vipaśyanā niśritya śamathabhāvanā
# la la ni lhag mthong thob pa yin gyi zhi gnas ni ma thob pa ste / / de lhag mthong la brten nas zhi gnas la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ na śamathasya lābhī nāpi vipaśyanāyāḥ
# la la ni zhi gnas kyang thob pa ma yin la lhag mthong yang thob pa ma yin te /
tatsaṃbaddhacittasya layau ddhatyāpakarṣaṇād yugapadubhayamārga bhāvanā
# de chos la rgod pa mngon par tshar bcad pa'i sems kyis gnyi ga la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī vipaśyanāyāśca
# la la ni zhi gnas dang lhag mthong yan thob pa yin te /
tasya śamathavipaśyanobhayamārga yuktasya samaṃ yugapat pravṛttiḥ
# de zhi gnas dang lhag mthong yang 'dres par gyur nas mnyam par zung du 'jug go /
trīṇīndriyāṇi
# dbang po ni gsum ste /
ajñātamājñāsyāmīndriyam ājñendriyam ājñātāvīndriyaṃ  ca
# mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa dang kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po'o /
ajñātamājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ katamat
# mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
prayogamārge pañcadaśasu ca darśanamārgacittakṣaṇeṣu yadindriyam
# sbyor ba'i lam dang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bco lnga la gang dbang byed pa'o /
ājñendriyaṃ katamat
# kun shes pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
ṣoḍaśāt darśanamārgacittakṣaṇādrūdhvaṃ sarvasmin śaikṣamārge yadindriyam
# mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa la brten nas slob pa'i lam thams cad la gang dbang byed pa'o /
ājñātāvīndriyaṃ katamat
# kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
aśaikṣamārgeyadindriyam
# mi slob pa'i lam la gang dbang byed pa'o /
prathamadhyānabhūmikānāṃ bhāvanāmārge kāmāvacarāṇi kuśalamūlakānyapi bhāvanāṃ gacchanti
# bsam gtan dang po'i sa pa'i lam bsgom pa na 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bsgom par 'gyur te /
teṣu vibhutvalābhataḥ / yathā prathamadhyānabhūmikānāṃ kāmāvacarāṇi kuśalamūlakāni bhāvanāṃ gacchanti tathā sarvepāmūrdvabhūmikānāṃ bhāvanāmārge adhobhūmikāni kuśalamūlakāni bhāvanāṃ gacchanti
# de dag la dbang 'byor ba thob pa'i phyir ro / / bsam gtan dang po'i sa pa na 'dod pa na spyod pa rnams la ji lta ba de bzhin du sa gong ma ba'i lam thams cad bsgom pa na / / sa 'og ma ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bsgom par 'gyur te /
teṣu vibhutvalābhataḥ / niṣṭhāmārgaḥ katamaḥ
# de dag la dbang 'byor ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
vajropamaḥ samadhiḥ
# mthar phyin pa'i lam gang zhe na /
sarvadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratipraśrabdheḥ sarvasaṃyogānāṃ prahāṇāt sarvavisaṃyogānāmadhigamācca
# gnas ngan len thams cad rgyun gcod pa dang 'phrad pa'i 'thob pa rnams kyi rgyun chad pa dang bral ba'i 'thob pa rnams thob pa'i phyir /
tadanantaraṃ nirantarāśrayapravṛttiḥ prāptakṣayajñānam anutpādajñānaṃ daśāśaikṣā dharmāḥ
# rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la brten nas de ma thag tu gnas ma lus par gyur te / / zad pa shes pa dang mi skye ba shes pa'o /
katame daśa / aśaikṣasya samyagdṛṣṭiryāyada śaikṣasya samyaksamādhiḥ aśaikṣasya samyagvimokṣaḥ aśaikṣasya samyag jñānaṃ ca / evamādayo dharmā niṣṭhāmārga ucyate
# mi slob pa'i chos bcu yang yin te / / mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba nas / / mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bar dang mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i rnam par grol ba dang mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i shes pa'o /
katamāni sarvadauṣṭhulyāni / saṃ kṣepataścaturviśatiḥ / tadyathā sarvatragamabhilāpadauṣṭhulyaṃ veditadauṣṭhulyaṃ kleśadauṣṭhulyaṃ karmadauṣṭhulyaṃ vipākadauṣṭhulyaṃ kleśāvaraṇādauṣṭhulyaṃ karmāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ vipākāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ nivaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ vitarkkadauṣṭhulyaṃ āhāradauṣṭhulyaṃ maithunadauṣṭhulyaṃ svapnadauṣṭhulyaṃ vyādhidauṣṭhulyaṃ jarādauṣṭhulyaṃ maraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ pariśramadauṣṭhulyaṃ dṛḍhadauṣṭhulyam audārikadauṣṭhulyaṃ madhyadauṣṭhulyaṃ sūkṣmadauṣṭhulyaṃ samāpattyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ jñeyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ ca
# gnas ngan len thams cad gang zhe na / / mngon par brjod pa'i gnas ngan len kun tu 'gro ba dang tshor ba'i gnas ngan len dang nyin mongs pa'i gnas ngan len dang las kyi gnas ngan len dang rnam par smin pa'i gnas ngan len dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas len dang las kyi sgrib pa'i gnas len dang rnam par smin pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas len dang grib pa'i gnas len dang rtog pa'i gnas len dang zas kyi gnas ngan len dang 'khrig pa'i gnas len dang rmi lam gyi gnas ngan len dang nad kyi gnas ngan len dang rga ba'i gnas ngan len dang 'chi ba'i gnas ngan len dang yongs su ngal ba'i gnas ngan len dang gnas ngan len brtan pa dang gnas ngan len chen po dang gnas ngan len 'bring po dang gnas ngan len chung ngu dang nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len to /
saṃyogaḥ katamaḥ / dauṣṭhulyāciteṣu saṃyogalābhateti vijñaptiḥ
# 'phrad pa'i 'thob pa rnams gang zhe na / / gnas ngan len bsags pa la 'thob pas zhes gdags so /
visaṃyogaḥ katamaḥ / dauṣṭhulyavikṣipteṣu visaṃyogalābhateti vijñaptiḥ / vajropamaḥ samādhiḥ katamaḥ
# 'bras ba'i 'thob pa rnams gang zhe na / / gnas ngan len zad pa la bral ba'i 'thob pa zhes gdags so / / rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
bhāvanāmārgagatasya taduttaraṃ saṃyojanaprahāṇamārgavasthāyāṃ yaḥ samādhiḥ prayogamārgasaṃgraho vā ānantaryamārgasaṃgraho vā / prayogamārgasaṃgrahastu tataḥ paraṃ sarvairāvaraṇairacchādyaḥ sarvāvarāṇānāṃ ca bhedaka iti / ānantaryamārgasaṃgrahastu yadanantaraṃ kṣayajñānānutpādajñānotpattiḥ
# sbyor ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa dang bar chad med pa'i lam gyis bsdus pa'o / / sbyor ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa ni gang phan chad sgrib pa thams cad kyis mi phyed cing / / sgrib pa thams cad ni shigs pa'o / / bar chad med pa'i lam gyis bsdus pa ni gang gi 'og tu zad par shes pa dang mi skye ba shes pa 'byung ba ste /
sa ca samādhiḥ nirantaraḥ dṛḍhaḥ ekarasaḥ vyāpī ca / etadarthapratibimbanārthaṃ  bhagavatoktaṃ tadyathā mahāśailaparvato 'khaṇḍo 'cchidro 'śuṣira ekaghanaḥ susaṃvṛtto daśadigvātākampyaśca
# ting nge 'dzin de yang bar med pa brtan pa / / sra ba / / ro gcig pa / / khyab pa'o / / 'di la dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dper na / / brag chen po ma grub pa / / ser ka med pa / / khong stong ma yin pa / / gcig 'dus pa / / shin tu mkhregs pa de ni shar phyogs kyi rlung gis kyang mi sgul cing mi g yos so /
katamā nāma nirantarāśrayapravṛttiḥ
# shar phyogs ji lta bar phyogs thams cad kyang de bzhin no zhes gsungs so /
aśaikṣamārgalābhinaḥ trividhā āśrayapravṛttiḥ / katamāstisraḥ / cittāśrayamapravṛttiḥ māryāśrapapravṛttiḥ dauṣṭhulyāśrayapravṛttiśca
# gnas ma lus par gyur pa gang zhe na / / gang mi slob pa'i lam thob pa'i sems kyi gnas gyur pa dang lam gyi gnas gyur pa dang gnas ngan len gyi gnas gyur pa'o /
kṣayajñānaṃ katamat
# zad pa shes pa gang zhe na /
hetukṣayeṇa yad śānaṃ labhyate kṣayaviṣayā lambanaṃ vā
# rgyu zad nas shes pa gang yin pa'am / / zad pa la dmigs pa'o /
anutpādajñānaṃ katamat
# mi skye ba shes pa gang zhe na /
phalaprahāṇena yad jñānaṃ labhyate phalānutpattiviṣayālambanaṃ vā
# 'bras bu spangs nas shes pa gang yin pa'am / / 'bras bu mi skye ba la dmigs pa'o /
daśāśaikṣā dharmāstu aśaikṣāṇāṃ śīlaskandhaṃ samādhiskandhaṃ prajñāskandhaṃ vimuktiskandhaṃ vimuktijñānadarśanaskandhaṃ cādhikṛtya veditavyāḥ
# mi slob pa'i chos bcu ni mi slob pa'i tshul khrims kyi phung po dang ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po dang shes rab kyi phung po dang rnam par grol ba'i phung po dang rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phung po'i dbang du byas par shes par bya'o /
tathā ca mārgasatyasya catvāraḥ prakārabhedāḥ / mārgalakṣaṇaṃ nyāyalakṣaṇaṃ pratipadlakṣaṇaṃ nairyāṇikalakṣaṇaṃ ca / kimupādāya mārgalakṣaṇam
# yang lam gyi bden pa'i rnam pa ni mtshan nyid bzhir rig par bya ste / / lam gyi mtshan nyid dang rigs pa'i mtshan nyid dang sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid dang nges par 'byin pa'i mtshan nyid do / / ci'i phyir lam gyi mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
tattvārthaparimārgaṇatāmupādāya / kimupādāya nyāyalakṣaṇam / kleśapratipakṣatāmupādāya
# de kho na'i don yongs su tshol ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir rigs pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na / / nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya pratipallakṣaṇam / cittāviparyāsapratipādanātāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na / / sems phyin ci ma log par sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya nairyāṇikalakṣaṇam
# ci'i phyir nges par 'byin pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
nityapadayānatāmupādāya
# rtag pa'i gnas su 'gro ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
satyeṣu ṣoḍaśākārāḥ laukikā lokottarāśca / laukikānāṃ lokottarāṇāṃ ca katamaḥ prabhedaḥ / jñeye akuśalapraveśakuśalyapraveśastrabhāvaprabhedataḥ sāvaraṇanirāvaraṇasvabhāvaprabhedataḥ savikalpanirvikalpasvabhāvaprabhedataśca / kena hetunā satyeṣu anityaduḥkhādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa lauaukikākārāḥ
# bden pa rnams la rnam par bcu drug ni 'jig rten pa yang yod 'jig rten las 'das pa yang yod de / / 'jig rten pa rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa dag byed brag ci yod ce na / / shes bya la legs par ma zhugs pa dang legs par zhugs pa dang sgrib pa dang bcas pa dang sgrib pa med pa dang; rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa dang rnam par rtog pa med pa'i phyir te /
tathāgata aprativedhataḥ kleśānuśayataḥ abhilāpamukhena prapañcanataśca / lokottarākārāḥ tadviparyayeṇa / lokottarākāreṣu varttamāno 'nityārthaṃ paśyati sākṣādanubhavati notvanityaṃ paśyati abhilāpaprapañcamukhena / yathā anityākārā anityārthe evaṃ śiṣṭhākarāḥ śiṣṭārtheṣu yathāyogaṃ veditavyāḥ / atha viniścaye dharmaparicchedo dvitīyo bhāgaḥ / dharmaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / āryaśāsanaṃ dvādaśāṅgadharmaḥ / katamāni dvādaśāṅgāni / sūtraṃ geyaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ gāthā udānaṃ nidānam avadānam itivṛtakaṃ jātakaṃ vaipulyam adbhutadharmaḥ upadeśaśca
# 'di ni bye brag go / / 'di ltar 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam pa la 'jug pa na mi rtag pa'i don mthong gi mi rtag pa nyid ces bya bar mthong ba ni ma yin no / / mi rtag pa nyid kyi don la ji lta ba de bzhin du rnam pa lhag ma rnams la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar rig par bya'o / / bden pa rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba ste / / kun las btus pa gnyis pa'o / / chos rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / chos zhes bya ba ni mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde dang lung du bstan pa'i sde dang tshigs su bcad pa'i sde dang ched du brjod pa'i sde dang gleng gzhi'i sde dang rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde dang de lta bu byung ba'i sde dang skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde dang shin tu rgyas pa'i sde dang rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde dang gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde'o /
sūtraṃ katamat
# mdo'i sde gang zhe na /
yadabhipretārthaṃ sūcanākāreṇa gadyabhāṣitam
# gang smos pa'i tshul gyis rkyang par gsungs pa ste /
daśānuśaṃsān saṃpaśyan tathāgataḥ sūcanākāreṇa dharmaṃ deśayati sukhaṃ vyavasthāpayati sukhaṃ deśayati / śrotāpi sukhamudgṛṇhāti dharmagauravatayā kṣipraṃ bodhi saṃbhārān paripūrayati āśudharmatāṃ pratividhyati / buddhe 'vetyaprasādaṃ labhate dharme saṃghe cāvetya prasādaṃ labhate
# phan yon bcu gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa mdor smos pa'i tshul gyis chos ston te / / rnam par gzhag par sla ba dang bshad sla ba dang gzung sla ba dang chos la gus pas myur du tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang myur du chos nyid rtogs par 'gyur ba dang sangs rgyas la shes nas dad pa thob pa dang chos dang dge 'dun la shes nas dad pa thob pa dang mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'i mchog la reg pa dang 'brel ba'i gtam gyis gtan la 'bebs pas dam pa rnams kyi sems mgu bar byed de /
paramadṛṣṭadharmasukhavihāraṃ spṛśati
# mkhas pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ba'o /
sāṃkathyaviniścayena satāṃ cittamārādhayati
# dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde gang zhe na /
paṇḍitaḥ paṇḍita iti saṃkhyāṃ gacchati / geyaṃ katamat
# mdo'i sde de nyid du dbus dang mtha' mar tshigs su bcad de dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'o /
sūtrāṇāṃ madhye vā ante vā gāthayā yad gīyate / sūtreṣu anirūpito 'rtho vā yad vyākhyāyate / ato geyamityucyate / vyākaraṇaṃ katamat / tat sthāneṣu samatikrāntānāmatītānāmārya śrāvakāṇāṃ prāptyutpattiprabhedavyākaraṇam / api ca sūtreṣu nirūīpitārthasya sphuṭīkaraṇam / vivṛtyābhisandhivyākaraṇāt / gāthā katamā / sūtreṣu pādayogena deśyate / dvipadī tripadī catuṣpadī paṃcapadī ṣaṭpadī vā / udānaṃ katamat
# yang drang ba'i don gyi mdo sde rtogs par byed pas dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'o / / lung du bstan pa'i sde gang zhe na / / gang las nyan thos 'das te shi ba'i 'dus byas pa dang 'byung ba lung ston pa'o / / yang nges ba'i don gyi mdo sde ni lung du bstan pa'i sde'o / / tshigs su bcad pa'i sde gang zhe na / / tshigs su sbyar nas gsungs pa ste / / de ni rtsa ba gnyis pa dang rtsa ba gsum pa dang rtsa ba bzhi pa dang rtsa ba lnga pa dang rtsa ba drug pa'o /
sūtreṣu kadācit tathāgatena āttamanaskena yadudāhṛtam / nidānaṃ katamat / pṛṣṭena yad bhāṣitam
# ched du brjod pa'i sde gang zhe na / / gang yin rangs nas brjod pa'o / / gleng gzhi'i sde gang zhe na /
sotpattikaṃ śikṣāprajñāptekaṃ vā / ato 'pi nidānam
# gang gi ched du gsungs pa dang byung ba dang bcas pa'i bslab pa bcas pa gsungs pa'o /
avadānaṃ katamat / sūtreṣu sadṛṣṭāntakaṃ bhāṣitam
# rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde gang zhe na / / dpe dang bcas par gsungs pa'o /
itivṛttakaṃ katamat
# de lta bu byung ba'i sde gang zhe na /
yadāryaśrāvakāṇāṃ pūrvalaukikaṃ vṛttaṃ deśayati / jātakaṃ katamat
# gang sngon gyi sbyor ba dang ldan pa'o / / skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde gang zhe na /
yat bodhisattvacaritapiṭakasaṃprayuktaṃ vṛttaṃ deśayati / vaipulyaṃ katamat
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang ldan pa'o / / shin tu rgyas pa'i sde gang zhe na /
bodhisattvapiṭakasaṃprayuktaṃ bhāṣitam
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod dang ldan pa'o /
yaducyate vaipulyaṃ tad vaidalyamapyucyate vaitulyamapyucyate
# shin tu rgyas pa ji lta ba de bzhin du rnam par 'thag pa dang mtshungs bral yang de bzhin no /
kimarthaṃ vaipulyamucyate
# ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa zhes bya zhe na /
sarvasattvānāṃ hitasukhādhiṣṭhānataḥ udāragambhīradharmadeśanātaśca
# sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i gnas yin pa dang rgyas pa dang rgya che ba dang zab ba'i rnam par chos bstan pa'i phyir ro /
kimarthamucyate vaidalyam
# ci'i phyir rnam par 'thag pa zhes bya zhe na /
sarvāvaraṇavidalanataḥ
# sgrib pa thams cad rnam par 'thag pa'i phyir ro /
kimarthamucyate vaitulyam
# ci'i phyir mtshungs bral zhes bya zhe na /
upamānadharmāṇāṃ tulanābhāvataḥ
# mtshungs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
adbhutadharmaḥ katamaḥ
# rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde gang zhe na /
yatra śrāvakabodhisattvatathāgatānāṃ paramā dbhutāścaryadharmāṇāṃ deśanā / upadeśaḥ katamaḥ
# gang las nyan thos dang byang chub sems dpa' dang sangs rgyas rnams kyi ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos bstan pa'o /
sarvagambhoragūḍha dharmalakṣaṇānāmaviparītaṃ vyākhyānam / evaṃ sūtrādīni dvādaśāṅgānyāryaśāsanāni triṣu piṭakeṣu saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti / katamāni trīṇi / sūtrapiṭakaṃ vinayapiṭakam abhidharmapiṭakaṃ ca / tāni punardvividhāni / śrāvakapiṭakaṃ bodhisattvapiṭakaṃ ca / sūtraṃ geyaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ gāthā udānaṃ caitāni pañca śrāvakāṇāṃ piṭakasya sūtrapiṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti / nidānamavadānamitivṛttakaṃ jātakaṃ caitāni catvāri dvayoḥ piṭakayoḥ saparivāre vinayapiṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti
# gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde gang zhe na / / gang du chos kyi mtshan nyid phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'o / / mdo'i sde la sogs pa 'di dag ni sde snod gsum du 'gyur te / / mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde dang lung du bstan pa'i sde dang tshigs su bcad pa'i sde dang ched du brjod pa'i sde gang yin pa 'di ni nyan thos kyi mdo sde'i sde snod do / / gleng gzhi'i sde dang rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde dang da lta bu byung ba'i sde dang skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde 'khor dang bcas pa 'di ni 'dul ba'i sde snod do /
vaipulyamadbhutadharmaśca ete dve bodhisattvapiṭakasya sūtrapiṭake saṃgṛhīte bhavataḥ
# shin tu rgyas pa'i sde dang rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde gang yin pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i mdo sde'i sde snod do /
upadeśa ekaḥ śrāvakabodhisattvapiṭakayoḥ abhidharmapiṭake saṃgṛhīto bhavati / kimupādāya tathāgatasya piṭakatrayavyavasthānam
# gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde ni gnyi ga'i chos mngon pa'i sde snod do / / ci'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis sde snod gsum rnam par gzhag ce na /
vicikitsopakleśapratipakṣakā matāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam / antadvayānuyogopakleśapratipakṣakāmatāmupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam / svayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśagrahopakleśapratipakṣakāmatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam
# nye ba'i nyon mongs pa the tshom gyi gnyen po'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa mtha' gnyis dang ldan pa'i gnyen po'i phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / rang gi lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po'i phyir chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
punaḥ śikṣātrayavyutpattikāmatāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam / adhiśīlādhicittaśikṣāniṣpādanakāmatāmupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam / adhiprajñaśikṣāniṣpādanakāmatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam
# yang bslab pa gsum brjod pa'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / lhag pa'i tshul khrims dang lhag pa'i sems kyi bslab pa bsgrub pa'i phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / lhag pa'i shes rab kyi bslab pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
punaḥ samyag dharmārthavyutpattikāmatāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam / dharmārthasākṣātkriyāpadasthānaprabhāvitā mupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam / jñānināṃ sāṃkathyaviniścayadharmasaṃbhogasukha vihārāśrayatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam
# yang chos dang don brjod pa'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam pa ci'i phyir gzhag go / / chos dang don mngon du bya ba'i gzhi'i gnas kyi phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / 'bel ba'i gtam gyis gtan la 'bebs pas chos la rdzogs par longs spyod pas bde ba la reg par gnas par bya ba'i phyir /
sa eṣa piṭakatrayasaṃgṛhīto dharmaḥ kasya gocaraḥ
# chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go / / chos 'di dag gang gi spyod yul yin zhe na /
śrutamaya cintāmayabhāvanāmayānāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ gocaraḥ
# thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba dang bsgoms pa las byung ba'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams kyi spyod yul lo /
yaduktaṃ sutre cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ sālambanāḥ sākāraḥ sāśrayāḥ sasaṃprayogāśca
# sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ni dmigs pa dang bcas pa dang rnam pa dang bcas pa dang gnas dang bcas pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa zhes kyang bya'o /
teṣāmasmin dharme ālambanaṃ katamat
# chos kyi nang nas de dag gi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
sūtrādikam / ākāraḥ katamaḥ
# mdo'i sde la sogs pa'o / / rnam pa gang zhe na /
skandhādayastatsaṃprayuktāścārthāḥ
# phung po la sogs pa dang ldan pa'i don rnams so /
āśrayaḥ katamaḥ / paravijñaptiḥ smṛtirvāsanā ca
# gnas gang zhe na; gzhan las rnam par rig pa dang dran pa dang bag chags so /
saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ
# mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
anyo 'nyasahāyabhāvena ālambane ākāraiḥ saṃpratipattiḥ
# gcig gi grogs gcig yin pa'i tshul gyis rnam pas dmigs pa yang dag par rtogs pa'o /
dharme ālambanaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ
# chos la dmigs pa'i rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepeṇa caturvidhaḥ ākhyātaḥ / vyāpyālambanaṃ caritaviśodhanālambanaṃ kauśalyālambanaṃ kleśaviśodhanālambanaṃ ca
# khyab pa'i dmigs pa dang spyod pa rnams par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa dang mkhas pa'i dmigs pa dang nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa'o /
vyāpyālambanaṃ punaścaturvidham / savikalpapratibimbālambanaṃ nirvikalpaprativimbālambanaṃ vastuparyantālambanaṃ kāryapariniṣpattyālambanaṃ ca
# khyab pa'i dmigs pa gang zhe na / / rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs brnyan dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan dang dngos po'i mtha' dang dgos pa yongs su grub pa'o /
savikalpapratibimbālambanaṃ katamat / adhimuktimanaskāreṇa yat śamathavipaśyanāviṣayālambanam
# rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs brnyan gang zhe na / / mos pa yid la byed pas gang zhe gnas dang lhag mthong gi dmigs pa'o /
nirvikalpaprativimbālambanaṃ katamat / tattvamanaskāreṇa yat śamathavipaśyanāviṣayālambanam
# rnam par mi rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan gang zhe na / / de kho na yid la byed pas gang zhe gnas dang lhag mthong gi dmigs pa'o /
vastuparyantālambanaṃ katamat
# dngos po'i mtha' gang zhe na /
sarvadharmāṇāṃ kṣayabhāvikatā yathāvadbhāvikatā ca
# gang chos rnams kyi ji snyed yod pa dang ji lta ba bzhin du yod pa'o /
kṣayabhāvikatā katamā
# ji snyed yod pa ni /
skandhadhātvāyatanāni
# phung po dang khams dang; skye mched rnams so /
yathāvadbhāvikatā katamā
# ji lta ba bzhin du yod pa ni /
catvāri āryasatyāni ṣoḍaśākārāḥ tathatā sarve anityāḥ saṃskārāḥ sarve duḥkhā saṃskārāḥ sarve 'nātmāno dharmāḥ nirvāṇaṃ śāntaṃ śūnyamapraṇihitamanimittaṃ ca / kāryapariniṣpattyālambanaṃ katamat
# 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dang rnam pa bcu drug dang de bzhin nyid dang 'du byed thams cad mi rtag pa dang 'du byed thams cad sdug bsngal ba dang chos thams cad bdag med pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa zhi ba dang stong pa nyid dang smon pa med pa dang mtshan ma med pa'o / / dgos pa yongs su grub pa gang zhe na /
āśrayaparivṛttiḥ
# gnas gyur pa'o /
iyamāśrayaparivṛttiracintyā / ṣoḍaśākāreṣu śūnye kati ākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti / dvau / apraṇihite kati ākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti / ṣaṭ / animitte katyākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti / aṣṭau / caritaviśodhanālambanaṃ pañcavidham
# rnam pa bcu drug gi nang nas stong pa nyid kyi rnam pa du zhe na / / gnyis so / / smon pa med pa'i rnam pa du zhe na / / drug go / / mtshan ma med pa'i rnam pa du zhe na / / brgyad do / / spyod pa rnams par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
bhūyorāgacaritānāmaśubhaviṣayālambanam
# 'dod chags la spyod pa rnams kyi ni mi sdug pa'o /
bhūyodveṣacaritānāṃ karuṇābhāvanā viṣayālambanam
# zhe sdang la spyod pa rnams kyi ni byams pa'o /
bhūyomohacaritānāṃ nikāyapratyayatā pratītyasamutpādaviṣayālambanam
# gti mug la spyod pa rnams kyi ni rkyen 'di las byung ba rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'o /
madamānacaritānāṃ dhātuprabhedaviṣayālambanam
# nga rgyal la spyod pa rnams kyi ni khams rab tu dbye ba'o /
vitarkkacaritānāmavatārāprativāṇi smṛtiviṣayālambanam
# rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa rnams kyi ni dbugs 'byung ba dang rngub ba rjes su dran pa'o /
kauśalyālambanaṃ pañcavidham
# mkhas pa'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
skandhakauśalyaṃ dhātukauśalyam āyatanakauśalyaṃ pratītyuasamutpādakauśalyaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ ca / sthānāsthānakauśalyena kamarthaṃ paśyati
# phung po la mkhas pa dang khams la mkhas pa dang skye mched la mkhas pa dang rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'o / / gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa ji ltar blta zhe na /
jñeye pratityasamutpādakauśalyaṃ paśyati / sthānāsthānakauśalyapratītyasamutpādakauśalyayoḥ kaḥ prabhedaḥ
# rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa las blta'o / / rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa bye brag ci yod ce na /
yat dharmā dharmānabhiniṣyandayanti nahyeṣāṃ nirhetuko nāpi viṣamahetuka utpāda itīdaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam / hetuphalānurūpye vedayitotpāda itīdaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyam
# chos rnams las chos rnams mngon par 'byung ba'i phyir rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa'i rgyu yongs su spangs pas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa'o / / rgyu dang mthun par 'bras bu 'byung ba yongs su gzung ba'i phyir gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'o /
kleśaviśodhanalambanaṃ katamat
# nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
yad adhobhūmikānāmaudarikatā ūrdhvabhūmikānāṃ śāntatā tathatā catvāryasatyāni ca
# sa 'og ma rnams kyi ni rags pa nyid do / / sa gong ma rnams kyi ni zhi ba nyid do /
etāni kleśaviśodhanālambanāni nāma
# de bzhin nyid dang 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'o /
tatra dharmamīmāṃsākāmena katibhiryuktibhirvicāryate
# chos la brtson pa chos la rnam par dpyod pa na rigs pa du zhig gis rnam par dpyod ce na /
catasṛbhiryuktibhiḥ / apekṣāyuktiḥ kāryakāraṇayuktiḥ upapattisādhanayuktiḥ dharmatāyuktiśca
# bzhis dpyod de / / ltos pa'i rigs pa dang bya ba byed pa'i rigs pa dang gtan tshigs bsgrub pa'i rigs pa dang chos nyid kyi rigs pa'o; /
apekṣāyuktiḥ katamā
# ltos pa'i rigs pa gang zhe na /
yā saṃskārāṇāmutpattau pratyayāpekṣā
# gang 'du byed rnams 'byung ba na rkyen la ltos pa'o /
kāryakāraṇayuktiḥ katamā
# bya ba byed pa'i rigs pa gang zhe na /
pṛthaglakṣaṇānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ kāryakāraṇāni
# gang rang gi mtshan nyid tha dad pa'i chos rnams so so rang gi bya ba byed pa'o /
upapattisādhanayuktiḥ katamā
# gtan tshigs bsgrub pa'i rigs pa gang zhe na /
upapattisādhanārthaṃ sādhyasyārthasya prāmāṇāviruddha upadeśaḥ / dharmatāyuktiḥ katamā / anādikālāt svalakṣaṇasāmānyalakṣaṇasthitadharmeṣu yā dharmatāpariniṣpattiḥ sā dharmatā
# gang bsgrub pa'i don tshad ma dang mi 'gal bar ston pa'o / / chos nyid kyi rigs pa gang zhe na / / thog ma med pa'i dus nas rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid gnas pa'i chos rnams la chos nyid du grags pa'o /
iti dharmeṣu vicāraṇā / dharmeṣu katamāḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti
# chos la rigs pas dpyod pa la brtson pa'i kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
catasraḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti / nāmaparyeṣaṇā vastuparyeṣaṇā svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā ca / nāmaparyeṣaṇā katamā
# kun tu tshol ba bzhi ste / / ming kun tu tshol ba dang dngos po kun tu tshol ba dang ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba dang bye brag tu 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba'o / / ming kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
dharmeṣu nāmakāyapadakāyavyañjanakāyānāmapariniṣpannaṃ svalakṣaṇamiti  yā santīraṇā / vastuparyeṣaṇā katamā / dharmāṇāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāmapariniṣpakṣaṃ khalakṣaṇamiti yā saṃtīraṇā / svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā katamā / dharmāṇā mabhidhānābhidheyasaṃbandhe svabhāvaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatāsantīraṇā / viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā katamā / dharmāṇāmabhidhānābhidheyasambandhe viśeṣaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatāsantīraṇā
# gang ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams kyi rang gi mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par rtog pa'o / / dngos po kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na / / gang de bzhin du phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyi mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par rtog pa'o / / ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na / / gang brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel pa la ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtog pa'o / / khyad par du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na / / gang brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel pa la khyad par du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtog pa'o /
iti dharmaparyeṣaṇābhāvanā / dharmeṣu yathābhūtaparijñānāni katamāni saṃbhavanti
# chos kun tu tshol ba la brtson pa'i yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin tu yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
catvāri yathābhūtaparijñānāni / nāmaparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ vastuparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ
# yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa bzhi ste / / ming tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa dang dngos po tshol bar rtogs pa dang ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa dang khyad par du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa'o /
nāmaparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat / yathābhūtasya nāmānupalabdhijñānam
# ming tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na / / ming mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
vastuparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat
# dngos po tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
yathābhūtasya vastulakṣaṇānupalabdhijñānam
# de bzhin du dngos po'i mtshan nyid mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat / yathābhūtasya dravyasvabhāvānupalabdhijñānam
# ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na / / ngo bo nyid rdzas su mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat / yathābhūtasya dravyaviśeṣānupalabdhijñānam / dharmamāśritya samādhiprayuktasya yogabhūmiḥ katamā jñeyā
# khyad par du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na / / bye brag rdzas su mi dmigs par shes pa'o / / chos la ting nge 'dzin par brtson pa'i rnal 'byor gyis gang zhe na /
pañcākārāḥ / ādhāraḥ ādhānam ādarśaḥ ālokaḥ āśrayaśca
# de ni rnam pa lngar blta ste / / gzhi dang skyed pa dang me long lta bu dang snang ba dang gnas so /
ādhāraḥ katamaḥ
# gzhi gang zhe na /
saṃbhṛtabodhisaṃbhārasya ūṣmagatādiṣu āryasatyeṣu ca yad vāhuśrutyam / ādhānaṃ katamat
# tshogs bsags pa'i bden pa las brtsams te mang du thos pa nyid do / / skyed pa gang zhe na /
tadālambano yoniśo manaskāraḥ
# de la dmigs pa tshul bzhin yid la byed pa'o /
ādarśaḥ katamaḥ
# me long lta bu gang zhe na /
tadālambanaḥ sanimittaḥ samādhiḥ
# de la dmigs pa'i ting nge 'dzin mtshan ma dang bcas pa'o /
ālokaḥ katamaḥ
# snang ba gang zhe na /
grāhyagrāhakānupalabdhijñānam
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
etadadhikṛtya suṣṭhu uktaṃ buddhena bhagavatā / pratibimbaṃ manaḥ paśyan bodhisattvaḥ samāhitaḥ
# 'di la dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis / / byang chub sems dpa' mnyam gzhag pa / / yid kyi gzugs brnyan mthong bas na /
vyāvarttya viṣaye saṃjñā svasaṃjñāmupadhārayan
# don gyi 'du shes ldog de nas / / rang gi 'du shes nges par gzungs /
evamātmasthacitto 'sau grāhyābhāvaṃ vibodhayet
# de ltar rang gi sems gnas nas / / gzung ba med par rtogs par bya /
tataśca grāhakābhāvaṃ nopalambhaṃ spṛśettataḥ
# de yi 'og tu 'dzin med par / / de nas mi dmigs reg par bya /
iti / āśrayaḥ katamaḥ / āśrayaparivṛttiḥ / kathaṃ dharmeṣu dharmakuśalo bhavati
# zhes legs par gsungs so / / legs par bka' stsal to / / gnas gang zhe na / / gnas gyur pa'o / / ji ltar na chos rnams la chos la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
bahuśrutatāmupādāya / kathamarthakuśalo bhavati
# mang du thos pa nyid kyi phyir ro / / ji ltar na don la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
abhidharme abhivinaye lakṣaṇajñatāmupādāya / kathaṃ vyañjanakuśalo bhavati / sva niruktavyañjanajñatāmupādāya
# chos mngon pa dang 'dul ba mngon pa'i mtshan nyid shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro / / ji ltar na yi ge la mkhas pa yin zhe na / / nges pa'i tshig bzang po'i yi ge shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
kathaṃ niruktikuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na nges pa'i tshig la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
ātmātmīyeti janapadaniruktimanabhiniviśyānuvyavahārajñatāmupādāya
# bdag go bdag go zhes yul mi'i nges pa'i tshig la mngon par ma zhen par rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
kathaṃ pūrvāntāparāntānusandhikuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mthar 'brel pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
pūrvānte udgrahaṇaṃ tāmaparānte niḥsaraṇaṃ tāmupādāya
# sngon gyi mthar gzung bas dang phyi ma'i mthar nges par 'byung bar bya ba shes pa nyid kyi phyir /
kathaṃ dharmeṣu dharmavihārī bhavati / bhāvanāmanāgamya kevalaśrutacintāprayogeṇa na dharmavihārī bhavati
# ji ltar na chos rnams la chos la gnas pa nyid yin zhe na / / bsgom pa la ma brten par thos pa dang sems pa'i sbyor ba 'ba' zhig gis kyang chos la gnas pa ma yin la /
śrutacintāmanagamya kevalabhāvanāprayogeṇa na dharmavihārī bhavati
# zos pa dang sems pa la ma brten par bsgom pa la sbyor ba 'ba' zhig gis kyang chos la gnas pa ma yin gyi /
ubhayamāgamyobhayavihāreṇa dharmavihārī bhavati
# gnyi ga la brten te gnyi ga la gnas na / / chos la gnas pa yin no /
udgrahāya svādhyāyadeśanābhiḥ śrutamayaṃ draṣṭavyam
# 'dzin pa dang kha ton byed pa dang bshad pas thos pa las byung bar blta'o /
samadhiprayogāsantuṣṭibhyāṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ draṣṭavyam
# ting nge 'dzin la sbyor ba dang chog par mi 'dzin pas bsgoms pa las byung bar blta'o /
prayogaḥ sātatyasatkṛtyaprayogeṇāviparītaprayogeṇa ca draṣṭavyaḥ
# sbyor ba ni rgyun du chud pa dang gus par sbyor ba dang ma log par sbyor bar blta'o /
asantuṣṭiranāsvāditottaśamayaprayogeṇa draṣṭavyā
# chog par mi 'dzin pa ni ro mi myang ba dang gong du zhig gnas la sbyor bar blta'o /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ pāramitāpiṭakamucyate / pāramitānāṃ saṃkhyānirddeśatāmupādāya lakṣaṇanirddeśatāmupādāya kramanirdeśatāmupādāya niruktinirdeśatāmupādāya bhāvanānirdeśatā mupādāya prabhedanirdeśatāmupādāya saṃgrahanirdeśatāmupādāya vipakṣanirdeśatāmupādaya guṇavarṇananirdeśatāmupādāya anyo 'nyaviniścayatāṃ copādāya
# ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sde snod ces bya zhe na / / der pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi grangs bstan pa dang mtshan nyid bstan pa dang go rims bstan pa dang nges pa'i tshig bstan pa dang bsgom pa bstan pa dang rab tu dbye ba bstan pa dang bsdus pa bstan pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs bstan pa dang yon tan gyi bsngags pa bstan pa dang gcig la gcig nges par bstan pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyaṃ audāryaṃ gāmbhīrya ca deśyate
# ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la rgya che ba dang zab par bstan ce na /
sarvākārajñatāma udāragambhīratāmupādaya
# rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rgya che ba dang zab pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā audāryagāmbhīryaṃ nādhimucyante uttrasanti / dharmatāviyuktatāmupādāya  anavaropitakuśalamūlatāmupādāya pāpamitraparigrahatāṃ copādāya
# ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la sems can kha cig rgya che ba dang zab par mi mos shing skrag par 'gyur zhe na / / chos nyid dang bral ba dang dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa dang sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs su zin pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā adhimucyante
# ci'i phyir shun tu rgyas pa la sems can kha cig mos kyang nges par 'byung bar mi 'gyur zhe na /
adhimucyamānā api na niryānti / svayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśa sthāpitayā
# bdag nyid lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa la gnas pa dang don la sgra ji bzhin du mngon par zhen pa'i phyir ro / / 'di la dgongs nas /
idaṃ ca sandhāyoktaṃ bhagavatā mahādharmādarśe dharmaparyāye bodhisattvasya yathāruta mayoniśo dharmānvicinvataḥ aṣṭāviṃśatirasadṛṣṭaya utpadyante
# bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi me log chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs las gsungs pa / / byang chub sems dpa' sgra ji bzhin du tshul bzhin ma yin par chos rnam par 'byed pa la /
aṣṭāviṃśatirasadṛṣṭayaḥ katamāḥ / nimittadṛṣṭiḥ prajñaptyapavādadṛṣṭiḥ parikalpāpavādadṛṣṭiḥ tattvāpavādadṛṣṭiḥ parigrahadṛṣṭiḥ pariṇatidṛṣṭiḥ anavadyatādṛṣṭiḥ niḥsaraṇadṛṣṭiḥ avajñādṛṣṭiḥ prakopadṛṣṭiḥ viparītadṛṣṭiḥ prasavadṛṣṭiḥ anabhyupagamadṛṣṭiḥ kusṛtidṛṣṭiḥ satkāradṛṣṭi dṛḍhamūḍhatādṛṣṭiḥ mūladṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭāvadṛṣṭadṛṣṭiḥ prayoganirākaraṇadṛṣṭiḥ anairyāṇikadṛṣṭiḥ āvaraṇopacayadṛṣṭiḥ apuṇyaprasavadṛṣṭiḥ vaiphalyadṛṣṭiḥ nigrāhyadṛṣṭiḥ abhyākhyānadṛṣṭiḥ akathyadṛṣṭiḥ mahādṛṣṭiḥ abhimānadṛṣṭiśca
# lta ba ngan pa nyi shu rtsa brgyad 'byung ste / / lta ba ngan pa nyid shu rtsa brgyad bo dag gang zhe na / / mtshan mar lta ba dang btags pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang kun tu rtog pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang de kho na la skur ba 'debs pa'i lta ba dang yongs su 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang bsgyur ba'i lta ba dang kha na ma tho ba med par lta ba dang nges par 'byung bar lta ba dang dpa' za ba'i lta ba dang rab tu 'khrug pa'i lta ba dang phyin ci log tu lta ba dang 'phel ba'i lta ba dang khas mi len pa'i lta ba dang ngan g yo'i lta ba dang bkur sti'i lta ba dang rmongs pa brten pa'i lta ba dang rtsa ba'i lta ba dang lta ba la lta ba ma yin par lta ba dang sbyor ba sel ba'i lta ba dang nges par 'byin pa ma yin par lta ba dang / / sgrib pa sogs pa'i lta ba dang bsod nams ma yin pa 'phel ba'i lta ba dang 'bras bu med pa'i lta ba dang chad pas bcas pa'i lta ba dang skur ba 'debs pa'i lta ba dang bsnyad pa ma yin pa'i lta ba dang lta ba chen po dang mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyi lta ba'o; /
yaduktaṃ vaipulye niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā iti / tatra ko 'bhisandhiḥ
# shin tu rgyas pa las chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med do zhes gang gsungs pa de la dgongs pa gang yin zhe na /
svayamabhāvatāmupādāya svenātmanābhāvatāmupādāya sve bhāve 'navasthitātma tāmupādāya bālagrāhavaccālakṣaṇatāmupādāya / api khalu parikalpite svabhāve lakṣaṇaniḥsvabhāvatāmupādāya paratantre utpattiniḥsvabhāvatāmupādāya pariniṣpanne paramārthaniḥsvabhāvatāmupādāya
# bdag nyid kyis mi 'byung ba dang rang gi bdag nyid du med pa dang rang gi ngo bo la mi gnas pa dang byis pas gzung ba bzhin du mtshan nyid med pa'i phyir ro / / yang kun tu brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mtshan nyid ngo bo nyid med pa dang gzhan gyi dbang la skye ba ngo bo nyid med pa dang yongs su grub pa la don dam pa ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir ro /
anutpannā aniruddhā ādiśāntāḥ prakṛtiparinirvṛtā iti ko 'bhisandhiḥ
# ma skyes pa ma 'gags pa gzod ma nas zhi ba rang bzhin gyis mya ngan las 'das pa zhes 'byung ba'i dgongs pa gang zhe na /
yathā niḥsvabhāvāstathā anutpannāḥ
# ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa de ltar ma skyes so /
yathā anutpannāstathā aniruddhāḥ
# ji ltar ma skyes pa de ltar ma 'gags so /
yathā anutpannāścāniruddhāśca tathā ādiśāntāḥ
# ji ltar ma skyes pa dang ma 'gags pa de ltar gzod ma nas zhi'o /
yathā ādiśāntā stathā prakṛtiparinirvṛtāḥ
# de ltar rang bzhin gyis yongs su mya ngan las 'das so /
api khalu catvāro 'bhiprāyāḥ / yairvaipulye tathāgatānāmabhiprāyo 'nugantavyaḥ / samatābhiprāyaḥ kālāntarābhiprāyaḥ arthāntarābhiprāyaḥ pugdalāśayābhiprāyaśca / catvāro 'bhisandhayo yaivapulye tathāgatānāmabhisandhiranugantavyaḥ
# yang gang dag gis shin tu rgyas pa la de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi dgongs pa khong du chud par bya ba'i dgongs pa bzhi ste / / mnyam pa nyid la dgongs pa dang dus gzhan la dgongs pa dang don gzhan la dgongs pa dang gang zag gi bsam pa la dgongs pa'o /
avatāraṇābhisaṃdhiḥ lakṣaṇābhisandhiḥ pratipakṣābhisandhiḥ pariṇāmanābhisandhiśca / vaipulye dharmasamādhikuśalo bodhisattvaḥ kathaṃ pratyavagantavyaḥ / pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ / pratikṣaṇaṃ sarvadauṣṭhulyāśrayaṃ drāvayati / nānātvasaṃjñāvigatāṃ ca dharmārāmaratiṃ pratilabhate
# gang dag gis shin tu rgyas pa la de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ldem por dgongs pa khong du chud par bya ba'i ldem por dgongs pa bzhi ste / / gzhug pa la ldem por dgongs pa dang mtshan nyid ldem por dgongs pa dang gnyen po la ldem por dgongs pa dang bsgyur ba la ldem por dgongs pa'o /
aparicchinnākāraṃ vāpramāṇāṃ dharmāvabhāsaṃ saṃjñānāti / viśuddhabhāgīyāni cāsyāvikalpitāni nimittāni samudācaranti
# shin tu rgyas pa la byang chub sems dpa' chos la tig nge 'dzin du mkhas par ji ltar khong du chud par bya zhe na / / rnam pa lnga ste /
dharmakāyaparipūri pariniṣpattaye cottarāduttarataraṃ hetumayaparigrahaṃ karoti / tatra pañcavidhāyāṃ bhāvanāyāṃ phalaṃ pañcavidhaṃ nirvattirtamiti darśayati / pañcavidhā bhāvanā saṃbhinnabhāvanā animittabhāvanā anābhogabhāvanā uttaptabhāvanā parivṛttinibhaḥ? bhāvanā yathākramam
# skad cig re re la gnas ngan len gyi gnas thams cad 'jig par byed pa dang sna tshogs kyi 'du shes dang bral te chos kyi dga' ba la dga' ba thob pa dang chos kyi snang ba rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa thams cad du tshad med pa yang dag par shes pa dang de la rnam par dag pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i mtshan ma rnams kun tu 'byung ba dang chos kyi sku yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang yongs su bsgrub pa'i phyir gong ma bas kyang chos gong ma'i rgyu yongs su 'dzin par byed pa'o / / ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa'i chos la bdug pa dang phye ma la sogs pas mchod par 'os kyi /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyadharmo dhūpamālyādibhiḥ pūjyo na tathā śrāvakadharmaḥ sarvasattvahitasukhādhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya
# nyan thos kyi chos la de lta ma yin zhe na / / sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i gzhir gyur pa'i phyir ro /
abhidharmasamuccaye dharmaviniścayo nāma tṛtīyaḥ samuccayaḥ / mahāyānābhidharmasamuccayaśāstre viniścaye prāptiparicchede tṛtīye prathamo bhāgaḥ / prāptiviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / saṃkṣepato dvividhaḥ / pudgalavyavasthānataḥ abhisamaya vyavasthāpanataśca draṣṭavyaḥ / pudgalavyavasthānaṃ katamat / samāsataḥ saptavidham / roga caritaprabhedataḥ niryāṇaprabhedataḥ ādhāraprabhedataḥ prayogaprabhedataḥ phalaprabhedataḥ dhātuprabhedataḥ caryāprabhedataśca
# chos rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba ste / / kun las btus pa gsum pa'o / / bam po lnga pa ste tha ma'o / / 'thob pa rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / gang zag rnam par gzhag pa dang mngon par rtogs pa rnam par gzhag par blta'o / / gang zag rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na / / spyod pas rab tu dbye ba dang nges par 'byung bas rab tu dbye ba dang nye bar brtan pas rab tu dbye ba dang spyod bas rab tu bde ba dang 'bras bus rab tu dbye ba dag / / khams kyis rab tu dbye ba dang spyad pas rab tu dbye bas kyang gang zhag rnam par gzhag par blta'o /
rogacaritaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ
# spyod pas rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
saptavidhaḥ / rāgacaritaḥ dveṣacarita mohacaritaḥ mānacaritaḥ vitarkacaritaḥ samabhāgacaritaḥ mandarajaska caritaśca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# 'dod chags la spyod pa dang zhe sdang la spyod pa dang gti mug la spyod pa dang nga rgyal la spyod pa dang rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa dang cha mnyam pa la spyod pa dang nyon mongs pa chung ba'i gang zag go /
niryāṇaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ / trividhaḥ
# nges par 'byung bas rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
śrāvakayānikaḥ pratyekabuddhayānikaḥ mahāyānikaśca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# nyan thos kyi theg pa pa dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa dang theg pa chen po pa'i gang zag go /
ādhāraprabhedaḥ katamaḥ / trividhaḥ / asaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ saṃbhṛtāsaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraśca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# nye bar brtan pas rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na / / tshogs ma bsags pa dang tshogs bsags pa yang yin la ma bsags pa yang yin pa dang tshogs bsags pa'i gang zag go /
prayogaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ / śraddhānusārī dharmānusārī ca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# sbyor bas rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na / / dad pas rjes su 'brang ba dang chos kyis rjes su 'brang ba'i gang zag go /
phalaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ
# 'bras bus rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
saptaviṃśatividhaḥ / śraddhādhimuktaḥ dṛṣṭiprāptaḥ kāyasākṣī prajñāvimuktaḥ ubhayatobhāgavimuktaḥ strotāpattiphalapratipakṣakaḥ strotaāpannaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ sakṛdāgāmī anāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ anāgāmī arhattvaphalapratipannakaḥ arhan saptakṛdbhavaparamaḥ kulaṃkulaḥ ekavīcikaḥ antarāparinirvāyī upapadyaparinirvāyī anabhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī sābhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī ūrddvaṃstrotāḥ parihāṇadharmā arhan cetanādharmā arhan anurakṣaṇādharmā arhan sthitākampyaḥ arhan prativedhadharmā arhan akopyadharmā arhan ca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# dad pas mos pa dang mthong bas thob pa dang lus kyis mngon du byed pa dang shes rab kyis rnam par grol ba dang gnyi ga'i cha las rnam par grol ba dang rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu mngon du bya ba'i phyir zhugs pa dang rgyun tu zhugs pa dang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu mngon du bya ba'i phyir zhugs pa dang lan cig phyir 'ong ba dang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu mngon du bya ba'i phyir zhugs pa dang phyir mi 'ong ba dang dgra bcom pa nyid kyi 'bras bu mngon du bya ba'i phyir zhugs pa dang dgra bcom pa dang re ltar thogs na srid pa lan bdun pa dang rigs nas rigs su skye ba dang bar chad gcig pa dang bar mdor yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dang skyes nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dang mngon par 'du byed pa med par yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dang mngon par 'du byed pa dang bcas pas mya ngan las 'da' ba dang gong du 'pho ba dang dgra bcom pa yongs su nyams pa'i chos can dang bdag gcod pa'i chos can dang rjes su bsrung ba'i chos can dang gnas pa las mi g yo ba'i chos can dang rab tu rtogs pa'i 'os su gyur pa dang mi 'khrugs pa'i chos can gyi gang zag go /
dhātuprabhedaḥ katamaḥ
# khams kyis rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
kāmāvacaraḥ pṛthagjanaḥ śīkṣo 'śaikṣaśca
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo dang slob pa dang mi slob pa'o /
evaṃ trividhaḥ kāmāvacaro rūpāvacara ārupyāvacaraḥ / kāmāvacaro rūpāvacaraśca bodhisattvaḥ kāmāvacaraḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ acintyaśca tathāgataḥ pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# 'dod pa na spyod pa ji lta bar gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa yang de bzhin no / / 'dod pa dang gzugs na spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang 'dod pa na spyod pa'i rang sangs rgyas dang de bzhin gshegs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gang zag go /
caryāprabhedaḥ katamaḥ / saṃkṣepataḥ pañcavidhaḥ / adhimukticārī bodhisattvaḥ adhyāśayacārī bodhisattvaḥ nimittacārī bodhisattvaḥ animittacāri bodhisattvaḥ anabhisaṃskāracārī bodhisattvaśca pudgalaprabhedaḥ
# spyad pas rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na / / mos pas spyod pa can dang lhag pa'i bsam pas spyod pa can dang mtshan ma dang bcas par spyod pa can dang mtshan ma med par spyod pa can dang mngon par 'du byed pa med par spyod pa can gyi byang chub sems dpa'i gang zag go /
rāgacaritaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# 'dod chags la spyod pa gang zhe na /
tīvrā yatarāgaḥ / evaṃ dveṣacarito mohacarito mānacarito vitarkacaritaśca pudgalaḥ tīvrāyataviśiṣṭaḥ
# 'dod chags kyi shas che zhing rgyun ring ba'i gang zag go / / rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa'i bar du yang de bzhin te / / rnam par rtog pa'i shas che zhing rgyun ring pa'o /
samabhāgacaritaḥ  pudgalaḥ katamaḥ / prakṛtisthakleśaḥ
# cha mnyam pa la spyod pa gang zhe na / / nyon mongs pa rang bzhin du gnas pa'o /
mandarajaskacaritaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# nyon mongs pa chung ba gang zhe na /
prakṛtisthatanutarakleśaḥ
# nyon mongs pa shin tu srab pa'i rang bzhin du gnas pa'o /
śrāvakayānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# nyan thos kyi theg pa pa gang zhe na /
yaḥ samāpanno vā asamāpanno vā śrāvakadharmatāvihārī prakṛtyā mṛdvindriyaḥ svavimuktaye praṇihitaḥ vairāgyabhāvanayā vimuktāśayaḥ śrāvakapiṭakamavalambya vīryabhāvanayā dharmānudharmacārī duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# nyan thos kyis chos nyid nges pa'am / / ma nges pa la gnas pa dang rang bzhin gyis dbang po rtul po dang bdag rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir smon lam btab pa dang yid byung ba dang 'dod chags dang bral ba dang rnam par grol ba'i bsam pa can dang nyan thos kyi sde snod la dmigs pa nas chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub cing / / gang sdug bsngal gyi mthar phyin pa thob pa'o /
pratyekabuddhayānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ / yaḥ samāpanno vā asamāpanno vā pratyekabuddhadharmatāvihārī prakṛtyā madhyendriyaḥ svavimuktaye praṇihitaḥ vairāgyabhāvanayā vimuktāśayaḥ kevalabhāvanayā cādhigatavodhyāśayaḥ śrāvakapiṭakamavalambya vīryabhāvanayā dharmānudharmacārī anutpāditapūrvanirvedhabhāgīyaḥ utpāditapūrvanirvedhabhāgīyaḥ aprāptapūrvaphalaḥ abuddhalaukikaḥ adhyātma cetanayā ārya mārgasaṃmukhībhūtaḥ khaḍgaviṣāṇakalpaḥ ekavihārī pratyekajinaḥ varggacāri duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa gang zhe na / / rang sangs rgyas kyi chos nyid nges pa'am / / ma nges pa la gnas pa dang rang bzhin gyis dbang po 'bring dang bdag rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir smon lam btab pa dang yid byung ba dang 'dod chags dang bral ba dang rnam par grol bar bya ba'i bsam pa can dang bdag nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba'i bsam pa can dang nyan thos kyi sde snod nyid la dmigs nas chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa dang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa sngon ma bskyed pa'am / / nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa sngon bskyed pa / / sngon 'bras bu ma thob pa'am / / sngon 'bras bu thob pa'am / / gang yang rung ste / / sangs rgyas 'byung ba med par bdag nyid kyis lam mngon du byas nas / / bse ru lta bur gyur te / / gcig pu gnas pa'am / / rang rgyal bar gyur te / / tshogs dang spyod pa gang sdug bsngal gyi mthar phyin pa thob pa'o /
mahāyānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# theg pa chen po pa gang zhe na /
yaḥ samāpanno vā asamāpanno vā bodhisattvadharmatāvihārī prakṛtyā tīkṣṇendriyaḥ sarvasattvavimokṣāya praṇihitaḥ apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāśayaḥ bodhisattvapiṭakamavalambya vīryabhāvanayā dharmānudharmacārī sattvān paripācayati śuddhāṃ buddhabhūmiṃ bhāvayati vyākaraṇaṃ ca pratilabhate samyaksaṃbodhiṃ ca sākṣātkaroti
# byang chub sems dpa'i chos nyid nges pa'am / / ma nges pa la gnas pa dang rang bzhin gyis dbang po rno ba dang sems can thams cad rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir smon lam btab pa dang mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i bsam pa can dang byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod la dmigs nas chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub cing / / sems can rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed / / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang yongs su sbyong la lung bstan pa yang thob cing / / gang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o /
asaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ / satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamālambya mṛdumātrasamutthitaḥ śuddhaśraddhādhimuktaḥ mṛdumātrāmokṣabhāgīyasamanvāgataḥ aniyatajanmakālikaḥ
# tshogs ma bsags pa gang zhe na / / gang bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la dmigs nas mos pa dang dad pa chung ba'i gang zag ste / / de yang thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa chung zhing tshe rabs kyi dus nges pa med pa dang ldan pa'o /
saṃbhṛtāsaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ / satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamālambya madhyamātrasamutthitaḥ śuddhaśraddhādhimuktaḥ madhyamātramokṣabhāgīyasamanvāgato niyatajanmakālikaḥ / saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# tshogs bsags pa yang yin la tshogs ma bsags pa yang yin pa gang zhe na / / gang bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la dmigs nas mos pa dang dang dad pa bar ma'i gang zag ste / / de yang thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa 'bring / / tshe rabs nges pa'i dus dang ldan pa'o / / tshogs bsags pa'i gang zag gang zhe na /
satyādhipatayaṃ dharmamālambya adhimātrasamutthitaḥ śuddhaśraddhādhimuktaḥ adhimātramokṣabhāgīyasamanvāgataḥ  tajjanmakālikaḥ
# gang bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la dmigs nas mos pa dang dad pa chen po'i gang zag ste / / de yang thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa chen po tshe rabs de nyid kyi dus can dang ldan pa'o /
punaḥ asaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamālambya satyeṣu mṛdumātrasatya dharmanidhyānakṣāntisamanvāgato mṛdumātra nirvedhabhāgīyasanvāgata anivatajanmakālikaḥ
# yang tshogs ma bsags pa ni bden pa'i dbang du bya ba'i chos la dmigs nas bden pa rnams la chos la nges par sems pa'i bzod pa chung ngu dang ldan pa ste / / de yang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa chung ngu tshe rabs kyis dus nges pa med pa dang ldan pa'o /
saṃbhṛtāsaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamālambya satyeṣu madhyamātrasatya dharmanidhyānakṣāntisamanvāgataḥ madhyamātranirvedhabhāgīyasamanvāgato nithatajanmakālikaḥ
# tshogs bsags pa yang yin la ma bsags pa yang yin pa ni gang bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la dmigs nas bden pa rnams la chos la nges par sems dpa'i bzod pa 'bring dang ldan pa ste / / de yang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa 'bring tshe rabs kyi dus nges pa dang ldan pa'o /
saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamālambya satyeṣu adhimātrasatya dharmanidhyānakṣāntisamanvāgataḥ adhimātranirvedhabhāgīyasamanvāgataḥ tajjanmakālikaḥ / tatra trimātranirvedhabhāgīyo laukikāgradharmaṃ sthāpayitvā laukikāgradharmaprakṛtyaiva kṣaṇikaḥ aprāvandhikaḥ / tajjanmakālikaḥ abhisamayaṃ samāpadyamāno 'pūrvavastha mṛdumadhyādhimātramokṣabhāgīyebhyo [nirvedha]bhāgīyebhyaśca parihīyate / tacca samudācāraparihāṇito no tu vāsanāparihāṇitaḥ
# tshogs bsags pa ni gang bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la dmigs nas bden pa rnams la chos la nges par sems pa'i bzod pa chen po dang ldan pa ste / / de yang 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog ma gtogs par nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa chen po tshe rabs kyi de nyid kyi dus can dang ldan pa'o / / 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog ni rang bzhin gyis skad cig pa ste / / tshe rabs de nyid kyi dus can kho na'o / / thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa dang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa chung ngu dang 'bring rnams las yongs su nyams pa de ni kun tu 'byung ba yongs su nyams par zad kyi / / bag chags yongs su nyams pas yongs su nyams pa ni ma yin no /
śraddhānusārī pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# dad pas rjes su 'brang ba'i gang zag gang zhe na /
saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāro mṛdvindriyaḥ paropadeśamanusmṛtya yaḥ satyābhisamayāya prayujyate
# gang tshogs bsags pa dbang po rtul po pha rol gyis bstan pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas bden pa mngon par rtogs par bya ba'i phyir sbyor ba'o /
dharmānusārī katamaḥ
# chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba gang zhe na /
saṃbhṛtasaṃbhārastīkṣṇendriyaḥ svayameva satyādhipateyaṃ dharmamanusmṛtya yaḥ [satyābhi]samayāya prayujyate
# gang tshogs bsags pa dbang po rnon po bdag nyid kyis bden pa'i dbang du bya ba'i chos kyi rjes su 'brangs nas bden pa mngon par rtogs par bya ba'i phyir sbyor ba'o /
śraddhādhimuktaḥ katamaḥ
# dad pas smos pa gang zhe na /
phalakāle śraddhānusārī yaḥ pugdalaḥ
# dad pas rjes su 'brang ba'i gang zag gang 'bras bu ba'i dus na'o /
dṛṣṭiprāptaḥ katamaḥ
# mthong bas thob pa gang zhe na /
phalakāle dharmānusārī yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gang zag gang 'bras bu'i dus na'o /
kāyasākṣī katamaḥ
# lus kyi mngon du byed pa gang zhe na /
śaikṣaḥ aṣṭavimokṣadhyāyī yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang sgom pa rnam par thar par brgyad la bsam gtan pa'i gang zag go /
prajñāvimuktaḥ katamaḥ
# shes rab kyis rnam par grol ba gang zhe na /
kṣīṇāsravo bhotvaṣṭavimokṣadhyāyo yaḥ pugdalaḥ
# gang zag pa zad pa ste / / rnam par thar pa brgyad la bsam gtan pa ni ma yin pa'i gang zag go /
ubhayatobhāgavimu[ktaḥ kata]maḥ
# gnyi ga'i cha las rnam par grol ba gang zhe na /
kṣīṇāsravo 'ṣṭavimokṣadhyāyī yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang zag bzang ba dang rnam par thar pa brgyad la yang bsam gtan pa'i gang zag go /
strotāpattiphalapratipannakaḥ katamaḥ
# rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa gang zhe na /
nirvedhabhāgīyeṣu pañcadaśasu darśanamārgacittakṣaṇeṣu yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa la mthong ba'i lam gyis sems kyi skad cig bcom ldan la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
strota āpakṣaḥ katamaḥ
# rgyun tu zhugs pa gang zhe na /
ṣoḍaśe darśanamārgacittakṣaṇe yaḥpudgalaḥ
# gang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
darśanamārgaḥ satyakatvaniyāmāvakrāntiḥ
# mthong ba'i lam ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur ba la zhugs pa ste /
dharmābhi[samaye]pi saḥ
# chos mngon par rtogs pa yang de yin no /
kāmeṣvavītarāgaḥ pudgalaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāman strotaāpanno bhavati
# 'dod pa rnams las 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i gang zag ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas / / rgyun tu zhugs par 'gyur ro /
yadbhūyo vītarāgaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāman sakṛdāgāmī bhavati
# phal cher la 'dod chags dang bral ba ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas lan cig phyir 'ong bar 'gyur ro /
kāmebhyo vītarāgaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāmannanāgāmī bhavati
# 'dod pa rnams las 'dod chags dang bral ba ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas phyir mi 'ong bar 'gyur ro /
yadā darśana prahātavyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇāt [stota ā]panno bhavati / kena kāraṇena trayāṇāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇāt strotaāpanno bhavati
# gang gi tshe mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs nas rgyun tu zhugs par 'gyur na ci'i phyir kun tu sbyor ba gsum spangs nas rgyun tu zhugs pa zhes bya na /
pradhānasaṃgrahata 'bhavati
# gtso bo bsdu ba'i phyir ro /
prādhānyaṃ kimupādāya / anuccalanakāraṇatāmupādāya / uccalitasya mithyāniryāṇakāraṇatāmupādāya / samyaganiryāṇakāraṇatāṃ copādāya / api khalu jñeyavipra[tipatti]kāraṇatāmupādāya dṛṣṭivipratipattikāraṇatāmupādāya pratipakṣavipratipattikāraṇatāṃ copādāya
# ci'i phyir gtso bo zhes bya zhe na / / mi 'phags pa'i rgyu yin pa dang 'phags kyang log pas nges par 'byung ba'i rgyu yin pa dang yang dag pas nges par 'byung ba ma yin pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro / / yang shes bya la log par rtogs pa'i rgyun yin pa dang lta ba la log par rtogs pa'i rgyu yin pa dang gnyen po la log par rtogs pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ katamaḥ
# lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa gang zhe na /
bhāvanāmārge kāmāvacarāṇāṃ pañcaprakārāṇāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang bsgom pa'i lam la 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi rnam pa lnga spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
sakṛdāgāmī katamaḥ / bhāvanāmārge kāmāvacarasya ṣaṣṭhasya kleśaprakā[rasya pra] hāṇamārge yaḥ pugdalaḥ
# lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i gang zag gang zhe na / / bsgom pa'i lam la 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa drug pa spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
anāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ katamaḥ
# phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa gang zhe na /
bhāvanāmārge kāmāvacarāṇāṃ saptamāṣṭamānāṃ kleśaprakārāṇāṃ prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang bsgom pa'i lam la 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa bdun pa dang brgyad pa spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
anāgāmī pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# phyir mi 'ong ba'i gang zag gang zhe na /
bhāvanāmarge kāmāvacarasya navamasya kleśaprakārasya prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang bsgom pa'i lam la 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa dgu pa spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
yadā sarveṣāṃ kāmāvacarā[ṇāṃ bhāva]nāprahātavyānāṃ prahāṇādanāgāmī bhavati
# gang gi tshe 'dod pa na spyod pa'i bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs pas phyir mi 'ong bar 'gyur na /
kena kāraṇena pañcānāmavarabhāgīyānāṃ saṃyojanā prahāṇādanāgāmītyucyate / pradhānasaṃgrahamupādāya
# ci'i phyir tha ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba lnga spangs pas phyir mi 'ong ba zhes bya zhe na / / gtso bo bsdu ba'i phyir ro /
prādhānyaṃ kimupādāya / gatyavara kāraṇatāṃ dhātvaparakāraṇatāṃ copādāya
# ci'i phyir gtso bo zhes bya zhe na / / 'gro ba tha ma'i rgyu yin pa dang khams tha ma'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
arhattvaphalapratipannakaḥ katamaḥ
# dgra bcom pa nyid kyi 'bras bu la 'jug pa gang zhe na /
yāvadbhāvāgrikāṇāmaṣṭaprakārāṇāṃ [kleśānāṃ] prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang srid pa'i rtse mo pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi rnam pa brgyad spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
arhan  katamaḥ
# dgra bcom pa gang zhe na /
bhāvāmrikasya navamasya kleśaprakārasya prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang srid pa'i rtse mo pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa dgu pa spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
yadā traidhātukānāṃ kāmāvacarāṇāṃ sarvvakleśānāṃ prahāṇādarhan bhavati
# gang gi tshe khams gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs pas dgra bcom par 'gyur na /
kena kāraṇenordbhabhāgīyānāṃ prahāṇādarhannityucyate / pradhānasaṃgrahamupādāya / pradhāna saṃgrahaḥ ki[mupādāya] / vimokṣopādāna kāraṇatāmupādāya / ūrddvā parityāgakāraṇatāṃ copādāya
# ci'i phyir gong ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba rnam pa lnga spangs pas dgra bcom pa zhes bya zhe na / / gtso bo bsdu ba'i phyir ro / / ci'i phyir gtso bo bsdu ba zhes bya zhe na / / gong ma nye bar len pa'i rgyu yin pa dang gong ma yongs su mi gtong ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
saptakṛdbhavaraparamaḥ katamaḥ
# re ltar thogs na srid pa lan bdun pa gang zhe na /
strotaāpanna eva pudgalaḥ saptakṛtvo 'pi miśromiśra devamanuṣyeṣu bhavāt saṃsṛtya yo duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# rgyun tu zhugs pa'i gang zag nyid lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du lan bdun yan man du srid par 'khor bar byas nas gang sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
kulaṃkulaḥ katamaḥ
# rigs nas rigs su skye ba gang zhe na /
deveṣu vā kulātkulaṃ gatvā [manuṣye]ṣu vā yo duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du rigs nas rigs su song na gang sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma tho ba pa'o /
ekavīcikaḥ katamaḥ
# bar chad gcig pa gang zhe na /
sakṛdāgāmī deveṣveva yo duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# lan cig phyir 'ong ba lha rnams kyi nang nyid du gang sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
antarāparinirvāyī katamaḥ / upapattisaṃyojane prahīṇe abhinivṛttisaṃyojane aprahīṇe antarābhavamabhinirvarttayanneva yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti abhinivṛtto vā antarābhave upapattibhavagamanāya cetayannevayo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# bar mdor yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na / / skye ba'i kun tu sbyor ba ni spangs la mngon par 'grub pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni ma spangs pa ste / / bar ma dor srid pa mngon par 'grub pa na / / gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa dang bar ma dor srid pa mngon par 'grub pa skye ba'i srid par 'gro bar mi sems pa nyid na gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa dang mngon par bsams nas skye ba'i srid pa la mngon par 'jug pa ste /
