abhisaṃcetayitvā vā upapattibhavamabhisaṃprasthitaḥ [bhavānu]papatticchandaṃ yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti / upapadyaparinirvāyī katamaḥ / ubhayasaṃyojane aprahīṇe rūpadhātāvupapannamātra eva yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# skye ba'i srid pa ni ma thob pa na gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o / / skyes nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na / / gnyi gar kun tu sbyor ba ma spangs la gzugs kyi khams su skyes pa tsam nyid kyis gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
anabhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī katamaḥ
# mngon par 'du byed pa med par yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na /
upapannaḥ anabhisaṃskāreṇa yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# gang skyes nas mngon par 'du byed pa med par lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
abhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī katamaḥ / upapanno 'bhisaṃskāreṇa yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# mngon par 'du byed pa dang bcas pa'i yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na / / gang skyes nas mngon par 'du byed pas lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
ūrdhvaṃstrotāḥ katamaḥ
# gong du 'pho ba gang zhe na /
upapanno rūpāvacarāṇāṃ bhūmau bhūmau yāvadakaniṣṭhagān praviśya tannānāsrava mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti
# gang gzugs kyi khams su sa nas sar skye zhing 'ong min gyi bar du zhugs nas / / der lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
puna kaścid yāvad bhavāgragān mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti / api ca vyavakīrṇabhāvitasya caturthasya dhyānasya pañcaprakārā prabhedāḥ / mṛduparibhāvitaṃ madhyaparibhāvitamadhimātraparibhāvitamadhimātrādhimātrāparibhāvitamadhyādhimātraparibhāvitaṃ  ca
# la la ni srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du song nas lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o / / spel mar bsgoms pa ni bsam gtan bzhi pa la chung ngu yongs su bsgoms pa dang 'bring du yongs su bsgoms pa dang cher yongs su bsgoms pa dang ches char yongs su bsgoms pa dang shin tu ches cher yongs su bsgoms pas gnas gtsang ma rnams su skye'o /
taiḥ vyavakīrṇābhāvitasya caturthadhyānasya pañcaprabhedaiḥ yathākramaṃ paścasu śuddhāvāseṣūpapattiḥ / parihāṇadharmā arhan katamaḥ
# yongs su nyams pa'i chos can gyi dgra bcom pa gang zhe na / / dbang po rtul po myos kyang rung / / ma myos kyang rung / / gsod kyang rung / / mi gsod kyang rung ste /
mṛdvindriyaprakṛtiko vikṣipto vā avikṣipto vā cetayitvā vā acetayitvā vā dṛṣṭadharmasukha vihārāt parihāṇameti
# gang mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams pa'i skal pa can yin no / / bdag gsod pa'i chos can gang zhe na / / dbang po rtul po nyid myos kyang rung /
cetanādharmā arhan katamaḥ
# ma myos kyang rung / / mi gsod na /
mṛdvindriyaprakṛtiko vikṣipto vā avikṣipto vā acetayitvā dṛṣṭadharmasukhavihārāt parihāṇameti cetayitvā na parihāṇameti
# gang mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams par 'gyur pa'i skal pa can yin la / / gsod na skal pa can ma yin pa'o /
anurakṣaṇādharmā arhan katamaḥ
# rjes su bsrung ba'i chos can gang zhe na /
mṛdvindriyaprakṛtiko vikṣipto dṛṣṭadharmasukhavihārāt / parihāṇameti avikṣipto na parihāṇameti
# gang dbang po rtul po nyid myos na mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams par 'gyur ba'i skal ba can yin la / / ma myos na skal ba can ma yin pa'o / / gnas pa las mi bskyod pa gang zhe na /
sthitākampyaḥ arhan katamaḥ
# dbang po rtul po myos kyang rung / / ma myos kyang rung /
mṛdvindriya prakṛtiko vikṣipto vā avikṣipto vā dṛṣṭadharmasukhavihārāt na parihāṇameti nāpi indriyāṇyuttāpayati
# mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams par 'gyur ba'i skal ba can ma yin la / / dbang po rnams spyod ba'i skal ba can yang ma yin pa'i gang zag go / / rab tu rtogs pa'i 'os su 'gyur ba gang zhe na /
prativedhanādharmā arhan katamaḥ
# gang dbang po rtul po myos kyang tu rung / / ma myos kyang rung /
mṛdvindriyāprakṛtiko vikṣipto vā avikṣipto vā dṛṣṭadharmasukhaviharāt na parihāṇameti kevala mindriyā ṇyuttāpayati
# mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams par 'gyur ba'i skal pa can ma yin la; dbang po rnams sbyong ba'i skal ba can ni yin pa'i gang zag go / / mi 'khrugs pa'i chos can gang zhe na /
akopyadharmā arhan katamaḥ
# rang bzhin gyis dbang po rnon po ste / / myos kyang rung /
tīkṣṇendriyaprakṛtiko vikṣipto va avikṣipto vā na dṛṣṭadharmasukhavihārāt parihāṇameti
# ma myos kyang rung / / mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams par 'gyur ba'i skal ba can ma yin pa'o /
kāmāvacaraḥ pṛthagjanaḥ katamaḥ
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo gang zhe na /
kāmadhātāvupapanno bhavati āryadhaprāptaḥ pudgalaḥ ca
# gang 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur la 'phags pa'i chos rnams ma thob pa'i gang zag go /
kāmāvacaraḥ śaikṣaḥ katamaḥ
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i slob pa gang zhe na /
kāmādhātāvupapanno bhavati adharmaṃ ca prāptaḥ pudgalaḥ
# gang 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur te / / 'phags pa'i chos rnams thob la /
saṃyojanaṃ cāvaśiṣyate / kāmāvacaro 'śaikṣaḥ katamaḥ
# kun tu sbyor ba lhag ma dang bcas pa'i gang zag go / / 'dod pa na spyod pa'i mi slob pa gang zhe na /
kāmādhātāvupapanno bhavati āryadharmaṃ ca prāptaḥ pudgalaḥ / saṃyojanaṃ nāvaśiṣyate
# gang 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur te / / 'phags pa'i chos rnams thob la kun tu sbyor ba'i lhag ma med pa'i gang zag go /
yathā kāmāvacarāstrayaḥ tathā rūpāvacarā ārupyavacarā api
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i gang zag gsum ji lta bar gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i gsum la yang de bzhin du blta'o /
kāmāvacaro rūpāvacaro bodhisattvaḥ katamaḥ
# 'dod pa na spyod pa dang gzugs na spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' gang zhe na /
ārūpyadhātuvyavakarṣitena dhyānena saṃprayukto dhyānasukhairviharatīti kāmadhātāvapyupapanno rūpadhātāvapyupapannaḥ pudgala kāmāvacaraḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ katamaḥ / abuddhabhave kāmadhātau svataḥ pratyekabuddhabodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ
# gang gzugs med pa'i khams rnam par spangs pa'i bsam gtan dang ldan la / / bsam gtan gyi bde bas gnas shing 'dod pa'i khams sam / / gzugs kyi khams su skye ba'i gang zag go / / 'dod pa na spyod pa'i rang sangs rgyas gang zhe na / / gang sangs rgyas 'byung ba med par 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur te / / rang byang chub mngon du byed pa'i gang zag go /
acintyaḥ tathāgataḥ katamaḥ
# bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa gang zhe na /
kāmadhātau tuṣitabhavanayāsamārabhya yāvat mahāparinirvāṇaṃ darśayati sarvāṃ bodhisattvacaryāṃ buddhacaryāṃ mahācaryāṃ darśayatīti pudgalaḥ
# gang dga' ldan gyi gnas na gnas pa nas bzung ste / / yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i bar du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad dang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yang 'dod pa'i khams su ston pa'i gang zag go /
adhimukticārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ / adhimukticaryābhūmau sthito mṛdumadhyādhimātrabodhisattvakṣāntisamanvāgataḥ pudgalaḥ
# mos pas spyod pa can gang zhe na / / mos pas spyod pa'i sa la bzod pa chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po dang ldan pa'i gang zag gang yin pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o /
adhyāśayacārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# lhag pa'i bsam pas spyod pa can gang zhe na /
daśasu bhūmiṣu sthito yo bodhisattvaḥ
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
sanimittacārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# mtshan ma dang bcas pas spyod pa can gang zhe na /
pramuditāvimalāprabhākaryarciṣmatīsudurjayābhimukhībhūmiṣu sthito yo bodhisattvaḥ
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba dang dri ma med pa dang 'od byed pa dang 'od 'phro ba can dang shin tu sbyang dka' ba dang mngon du gyur pa la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
animittacārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ
# mtshan ma med par spyod pa can gyi gang zag gang zhe na /
duraṃgamabhūmau sthito yo bodhisattvaḥ
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i sa ring du song ba la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
anabhisaṃskāracārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamataḥ
# mngon par 'du byed pa med par spyod pa can gang zhe na /
acalā sādhumatīdharmameghāsu bhūmiṣu sthito yo bodhisattvaḥ
# gang byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g yo ba dang legs pa'i blo gros dang chos kyi sprin la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
punaḥ khalu strotaāpannaḥ pugdalo yaduktaḥ sa dvividhaḥ / kramanairyāṇikaḥ sakṛnnairyāṇikaśca
# rgyun tu zhugs pa'i gang zag ces gang gsungs pa la / / rgyun tu zhugs pa ni gnyis te / / rim gyis pa dang cig car nges par 'byin pa'o /
krasanairyāṇiko yathā purvamuktaḥ
# rim gyi pa ni ji skad bstan pa yin no /
sakṛnnairyāṇikaḥ satyābhisamayamabhisaṃpraviṣṭaḥ aprāpta samāpattimāśritya adhigatena lokottaramāgreṇa sakṛta traidhātukāvacarān sarvakleśān prajahāti prakāraśaḥ prajahāti
# cig car nges par 'byin pa ni gang bden pa rnams mngon par rtogs par byas nas / / mi lcogs pa med pa la brten te / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyis / / khams gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams rnam pas cig car spong ste /
dvayoḥ phalayo strotāpattiphalārhattvaphalayoḥ prajñāpyate
# 'di ni rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu dang; 'bras bu gnyis la gdags so /
sa ca pudgalo bhūyo dṛṣṭe dharme maraṇakāle ājñāmārāgayati
# phal cher ni mthong ba'i chos sam 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe kun shes pa thob par byed do /
yadi nārāgayati praṇidhānavaśena
# gal te mi byed na yang de smon lam gyi stobs can yin te /
tarhi praṇidhānavaśena kāmadhātāvevopapannaḥ avuddhabhave pratyekajinobhavati / atha viniścaye prāptiparicchede tṛtīye dvitīyo bhāgaḥ / abhisamayavyavasthānaṃ katamat / samāsato daśavidham / dharmābhisamayaḥ  arthābhisamayaḥ tattvābhisamayaḥ pṛṣṭhābhisamayaḥ ratnābhisamayaḥ asamudācārābhisamayaḥ niṣṭhābhisamayaḥ śrāvakābhisamayaḥ pratyekabuddhābhisamayaḥ bodhisattvābhisamayaśca
# smon lam gyi dbang gis 'dod pa'i khams nyid du skye ste / / sangs rgyas 'byung ba med na rang rgyal bar 'gyur ro / / mngon par rtogs pa rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na / / mngon par rtogs pa bcu ste / / chos mngon par rtogs pa dang don mngon par rtogs pa dang de kho na mngon par rtogs pa dang rjes la mngon par rtogs pa dang dkon mchog mngon par rtogs pa dang kun tu mi 'byung ba mngon par rtogs pa dang mthar thug pa mngon par rtogs pa dang nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa dang rang sangs rgyas kyi mngon par rtogs pa dang byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa'o /
dharmābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ / satyādhipateyeṣu dharmeṣu adhimātrasya adhimuktiprasādasya pratilambhaḥ yathāsaṃpratyayaṃ caryā ca / arthābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ satyādhipateyeṣu dharmeṣu adhimātrāyāḥ satyeṣu dhamanidhyānakṣānteḥ pratilambhaḥ
# chos mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na / / bden pa'i dbang du bya ba'i chos rnams la mos pa dang dad pa chen po thob pa'o / / don mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na / / nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i gnas skabs na bden pa'i dbang du bya ba'i chos rnams kho na la /
sā kṣānti nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāṃ gatā
# bden pa la chos nges par sems pa'i bzod pa chen po thob pa ste /
sā punastrividhena yoniśo manaskāreṇa prabhāvitā / sa trividhastu adhimātramṛduḥ adhimātramadhyo 'dhimātrādhimātraśca / tattvābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# bzod pa de yang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa chen po'i chung ngu dang chen po'i chen 'bring po dang chen po'i chen po dang rnam pa gsum gyis rab tu phye ba'o / / de kho na mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
ṣoḍaśe darśanamārgacittakṣaṇe ya āryamārgaṃ pratilabhate
# gang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug po dag thob pa'o /
darśanamārge punaḥ satye vyavasthāpanādyabhisamayāntikāni saṃmukhīkaroti / bhāvanāmārge tatsaṃvṛtijñānāni pratilabhate na tu saṃmukhīkaroti
# mthong ba'i lam la ni bden pa rnam par 'jog pa mngon par rtogs pa'i mtha' las byung ba kun rdzob shes pa rnams 'thob ste / / mngon du byed pa ni ma yin no /
bhāvanāmārge tatsaṃvṛtijñānabalena saṃmukhīkaroti / pṛṣṭhābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# de dag ni bsgom pa'i lam la mngon du byed do / / rjes la mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
sarvo bhāvanāmārgaḥ
# bsgom pa'i lam thams cad do /
ratnābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# dkon mchog mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
buddhe 'vetya prasādaḥ dharme 'tya prasādaḥ saṃghe 'vetya prasādaḥ
# sangs rgyas la shes nas dad pa dang chos dang dge 'dun la shes nas dad pa'o /
asamudācārābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# kun tu mi 'byung ba mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
akāraṇasaṃvaralābhāt śikṣāgatasya yadātmano narakakṣayaṃ tiryagyonikṣayaḥ pretayonikṣayaḥ avāṅpatanadurgatikṣayaḥ iti
# mi bya ba'i sdom pa gang thob pas slob pa 'di snyam du sems te / / bdag gi sems can dmyal ba zad do / / dud 'gro zad do / / yi dags zad do /
na punarupādāya tad durgatikarma durgativipāko 'bhinirvarttate / niṣṭhābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ / yathā mārgasatye niṣṭhāmārga uktaḥ
# ngan song ngan 'gro log par ltung ba zad do / / bdag yang ngan song ba'i las byas nas ngan song rnams su rnam par smin pa mngon par 'grub pa'i skal pa can ma yin no / / snyam pa'o / / mthar thug pa mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na; ji ltar lam gyi bden pa la mthar phyin pa'i lam bstan pa lta bu'o /
śrāvakābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
pūrvoktaḥ saptavidho 'bhisamayaḥ
# mngon par rtogs pa bdun po de dag nyid mdor bsdus te /
śrāvakāṇāṃ parato ghoṣamāgamya pratilambhataḥ śrāvakābhisamaya ityucyate / pratyekabuddhābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ / pūrvoktāḥ saptābhisamayāḥ / parato ghoṣamanāgamya pratilambhataḥ pratyekabuddhābhisamaya ityucyate
# nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o / / rang sangs rgyas kyi mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na / / mngon par rtogs pa bdun po de dag nyid gzhan gyi sgra la ma brten par thob pas rang sangs rgyas kyi mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o /
bodhisattvābhisamayaḥ katamaḥ
# byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa gang zhe na /
pūrvokteṣu saptābhisamayeṣu yā samudāgamakṣāntiḥ no tu sakṣātkiryā
# mngon par rtogs pa bdun po de dag nyid la byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag par 'grub pa'i bzod pa gang yin pa ste /
kevalaṃ bodhisattva pramuditābhūmau bodhisattvasya samyaktvaniyāmāvakrāntiḥ / sā bodhisattvābhisamayo veditavyāḥ
# mngon du byed pa ni ma yin no / / yangs rab tu dga' ba la byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa la zhugs pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o /
śrāvakābhisamayāt bodhisattvābhisamayasya ko viśeṣaḥ / saṃkṣepata ekādaśa / ālambanaviśeṣaḥ upastambhaviśeṣaḥ prativedhaviśeṣaḥ abhyupagamaviśeṣaḥ niryāṇaviśeṣaḥ parigrahaviśeṣaḥ vyavasthānaviśeṣaḥ pratiṣṭhāparivāraviśeṣaḥ abhijanmaviśeṣaḥ janmaviśeṣaḥ phalaviśeṣaśca
# nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa las byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa khyad par ci yod ce na / / dmigs pa'i khyad par dang nye bar rton pa'i khyad par dang rab tu rtogs pa'i khyad par dang khas len pa'i khyad par dang nges par 'byung ba'i khyad par dang yongs su 'dzin pa'i khyad par dang gnas dang g yog 'khor gyi khyad par dang btsun par skye ba'i khyad par dang skye ba'i khyad par dang 'bras bu'i khyad par ro /
phalaviśeṣaḥ punardaśavidhaḥ / āśrayaparivṛttiviśeṣataḥ guṇasamṛddhiviśeṣataḥ pañcākāraviśeṣataḥ trikāyaviśeṣataḥ nirvāṇaviśeṣataḥ miśropamiśrajñānaśaktilābhaviśeṣataḥ āvaraṇaviśuddhiviśeṣataḥ miśropamiśrakarmakriyāviśeṣataḥ abhisaṃbodhinirvāṇasandarśanopāyaviśeṣataḥ pañcākāraparitrāṇaviśeṣataśca veditavyaḥ
# 'bras bu'i khyad par ni gnas gyur ba'i khyad par dang yon tan phun sum tshogs pa'i khyad par dang rnam pa lnga'i khyad par dang sku gsum gyi khyad par dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i khyad par dang 'dres shing nye bar 'dres pa'i ye shes kyi nus pa thob pa'i khyad par dang sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i khyad par dang; 'dres pa dang nye bar 'dres pa'i las byed pa'i khyad par dang mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa ston pa'i thabs kyi khyad par dang yongs su skyob pa rnam pa lnga'i khyad par gyis kyang rig par bya'o /
apramāṇādivaiśeṣikaguṇānāṃ katamairabhisamayaiḥ saṃgrahaḥ
# tshad med pa la sogs pa yon tan khyad par can 'di dag mngon par rtogs pa gang gis bsdus she na /
pṛṣṭhābhisamayaniṣṭhābhisamayābhyāṃ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ / teṣāṃ saṃgrahaḥ punaḥ katamaḥ / apramāṇāni vimokṣāḥ abhibhvāyatanāni kṛtsāyatanāni araṇāpraṇīdhijñānam pratisaṃvidaḥ abhijñā lakṣaṇānuvyañjanāni pariśuddhayaḥ valāni vaiśāradyāni smṛtyupasthānāni arakṣāṇi asaṃpramoṣadharmatā vāsanāsamuddhātaḥ mahākaruṇā āveṇikā buddhadharmāḥ sarvākārajñatā ityevamādayo guṇā yathā sūtrāntareṣu nirdiṣṭāḥ / apramāṇāni katamāni
# rjes la mngon par rtogs pa dang mthar thug pa'i mngon par rtogs pas bsdus so / / de dag kyang tshad med pa rnams dang rnam par thar pa rnams dang zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams dang zad par gyi skye mched rnams dang nyon mongs pa med pa dang bsams nas shes pa dang so so yang dag par rig pa rnams dang mngon par shes pa rnams dang mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnams dang yongs su dag pa rnams dang stobs rnams dang mi 'jigs pa rnams dang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams dang bsrung ba med pa rnams dang bsnyel ba mi mnga' ba'i chos nyid dang bag chags legs par bcom pa dang thugs rje chen po dang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid de mdo sde las ji skad 'byung ba rnams so /
catvāri apramāṇāni / maitrī katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya sattvāḥ sukhena saṃprayujyeranniti vihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / karuṇā katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya sattvā duḥkhena viyujyeranniti vihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / muditā katamā
# byams pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten te sems can rnams la phan pa dang phrad par shog shig par bsam pa'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / snying rje gang zhe na / / sems can rnams la sdug bsngal dang bral bar shog shig par bsam pa'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / dga' ba gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya sattvāḥ sukhena na viyujyeranniti vihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / upekṣā katamā
# sems can rnams la bde ba dang mi 'bral bar shog shig par bsam pa'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / btang snyoms gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya sattvā hita labheranniti vihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# bsam gtan la brtan te sems can rnams la phan par bsam pa'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
vimokṣāḥ katame / aṣṭau vimokṣāḥ / kathaṃ rūpī rūpāṇi paśyatīti / dhyānaṃ niśritya adhyātmaṃ draṣṭari rūpasaṃjñāyā avibhāvānād draṣṭarī rūpasaṃjñāyāḥ saṃniveśanād vā dṛśya rūpādi paśyatīti vihārasamṛddho samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ yāvad nirmāṇāvaraṇād vimuktiḥ
# gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta ba ji lta bu zhe na / / 'di lta ste / / sprul pa'i sgrib pa las rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir bsam gtan la brten te; lta ba po bdag la gzugs su 'du shes pa dang ma bral ba'am / / gzhag pas kyang rung ste / / snang ba'i gzugs rnams la lta ba'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs rnams la lta ba ji lta bu zhe na /
kathamadhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī vahirddhā rūpāṇi paśyati
# lta ba po bdag la gzugs su 'du shes pa dang bral ba'am /
dhyānaṃ niśritya draṣṭari rūpasaṃjñāyā vibhāvanād arūpasaṃjñāyāḥ saṃniveśanādvā dṛśya rūpāṇi paśyatīti vihārasamṛddhau samādhi prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# gzugs med pa'i 'du shes gzhag pas kyang rung ste / / snang ba'i gzugs rnams la lta ba'i gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
kathaṃ śubhaṃ vimokṣaṃ kāyena sākṣātkṛtyopasaṃpadya viharatīti
# sdug pa'i rnam par thar pa lus kyis mngon sum du byas te rdzogs par byas nas gnas pa ji lta bu zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya adhyātmaṃ śubhāśubheṣu rūpeṣu anyonyāpekṣāsaṃjñāyā anyonyānugamasaṃjñāyā anyonyaikarasasaṃjñāyāśca labhāt tatra labdhe vihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat yāvat śubhaśubhanirmāṇāt saṃkleśotpattyāvaraṇācca vimuktiḥ / ākāśānantyāyatanavimokṣaḥ katamaḥ
# 'di lta ste / / sdug pa dang mi sdug pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa 'byung ba'i sgrib pa las rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir rang gis sdug pa dang mi sdug pa'i gzugs rnams la phan tshun ltos pa'i 'du shes dang phan tshun rjes su 'brel ba'i 'du shes dang phan tshun ro gcig pa'i 'du shes thob nas de la gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi rnam par thar pa gang zhe na / / thar pa'i rjes su mthun pa nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
vimokṣānukūlā kāśānantyāyatanavimokṣaḥ tathā vijñānānantyāyatanākiṃcanyāyatananaivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanavimokṣā api draṣṭavyaḥ yāvat vimokṣaḥ śānto vimokṣaḥ asaktyāvaraṇaṃ ca
# nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi rnam par thar pa ji lta bar rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang ci yang med pa'i skye mched dang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi rnam par thar pa yang de bzhin du blta bar bya ste / / 'di ltar zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa la chags pa'i sgrib pa las rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir ro /
saṃjñāvedayitanirodhavimokṣaḥ katamaḥ / naivasaṃjñānasaṃjñāyatanavimokṣaṃ niśritya samatikrāntānāṃ śiṣṭe śānte vimokṣe mokṣānusadṛśo vihāraḥ vihārasamṛddhau ca cittacaitasikānāṃ nirodhaḥ saṃjñāvedayitanirodhāvaraṇād vimuktyartham / abhibhvāyatanāni katamāni
# 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa'i rnam par thar pa gang zhe na / / 'di lta ste / / 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa la sgrib pa las rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi rnam par thar pa la brten te / / zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa la gnas pa las yang dag par 'das nas thar pa dang mthun par gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i gang sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams 'gog pa'o /
aṣṭāvabhibhvāyatanāni / pūrvāṇī catvāri abhibhvāyatanāni dvābhyāṃ vimokṣābhyāṃ vyavasthāpyante / uttarāṇi catvāri abhibhvāvatanāni ekena vimokṣeṇa vyavasthāpyante / tatra vimokṣairālambanamadhimucyate abhibhvāyataneṣu ālambanaprabhibhavati / vaśavarttanatā mupādāya / sattvasaṃkhyātāni asattvasaṃkhyātāni cāśritya rūpāṇi parittādhimātrāṇyucyante / śubhāśubhānyāśritya rūpāṇi suvarṇadurvarṇānyucyante / mānuṣyakadivyānyāśritya rūpāṇi hīnapraṇītānyucyante / śiṣṭāni yathā vimokṣeṣūktāni / ālambanābhibhavanatāmupādāya abhibhvāyatanānītyucyante / kṛtsnāyatanāni katamāni / daśa kṛtsnāyatanāni / kṛtsnaspharaṇālambanatāmupādāya kṛtsnāyatanānītyucyate / kṛtsnaspharaṇavihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ kṛtsnāyatanānītyucyante
# zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched bzhi ni rnam par thar pa gnyis kyis rig par bya'o / / bzhi ni rnam par thar pa gcig gis rig par bya'o / / rnam par thar pa rnams kyis ni dmigs pa la mos par byad do / / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams kyis ni dbang byed pa'i phyir zil gyis gnon to / / sems can dang sems can ma yin par gtogs pa'i gzugs rnams ni chung ngu dang chen po zhes bya'o / / mi'i dang lha'i rnams ni ngan pa dang bzang po rnams so / / lhag ma ni rnam par thar pa las 'byung ba ji lta ba bzhin no / / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams kyis dmigs pa zil gyis mnan nas zad par gyi skye mched rnams kyis zad par rgyas par byed par gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ni zad par gyi skye mched ces bya'o /
kimupādāya kṛtsnāyataneṣu pṛthivyādivyavasthāpanam
# ci'i phyir zad par gyi skye mched rnams las la sogs pa zad par gdags she na /
taiḥ kṛtsnāyatanaiḥ āśrayāśritarūpāṇi paśyatīti kṛtsnaspharaṇatāmupadaya
# gnas dang bcas pa'i gzugs la khyab par bya ba 'byor ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
śiṣṭāni yathāyogaṃ vimokṣavat / tathā ca kṛtsnāyatanaiḥ pariniṣpattirvimokṣāṇām
# lhag ma ni rnam par thar pa bzhin du ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyor ro / / zad par gyi skye mched rnams kyis ni rnam par thar pa rnams 'grub par byed do /
araṇā katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya kleśotpattyanurakṣāvihārasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# nyon mongs pa med pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten te gzhan gyi nyon mongs pa 'byung ba rjes su bsrung bar gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
praṇidhijñānaṃ katamat
# bsams nas shes pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya jñeya jñānapraṇidhisamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / pratisaṃvidaḥ katamāḥ
# bsam gtan la brten te 'di shes par bya'o zhes bsams nas yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
catasraḥ pratisaṃvidaḥ / dharmapratisaṃvid katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya sarvadharma paryāyeṣu avyāghātasamṛddhau samādhīḥ prajñāśeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# chos so so yang dag par rig pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas rnam grangs su gtogs pa rnams la thogs pa med pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
arthapratisaṃvid katamā
# don so so yang dag par rig pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya lakṣaṇe abhiprāye  cāvyāghātasamṛddau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# mtshan nyid dang dgongs pa la thogs pa med pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
niruktipratisaṃvid katamā
# nges pa'i tshig so so yang dag par rig pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya janapadabhāpāyāmanuvyavahāre dharmanirvacane ca avyāghāta samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# yul mi'i skad dang chos kyi nges pa'i tshig la thogs pa med pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
pratibhānapratisaṃvid katamā
# spobs pa so so yang dag par rig pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya dharmaprabhedeṣu avyāghātasamṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / abhijñā katamāḥ / ṣaḍabhijñāḥ / ṛddhyabhijñā katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya vicitrarddhivikurvita samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / divyaśrotrābhijñā katamā
# chos rab tu dbye ba la thogs pa med pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / rdzu 'phrul gyi mngon par shes pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / lha'i rna ba'i mngon par shes pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya vicitrāṇāṃ śabdānāmanuśravasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / cetaḥparyāyābhijñā katamā
# sgra sna tshogs nyan pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / sems kyi rnam grangs mngon par shes pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya parasattveṣu cittacaritaparyāya praveśasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhi prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# sems can gzhan dag gi sems kyi spyod pa la 'jug pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
pūrvanivāsānusmṛtyabhijñā katamā
# sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i mngon par shes pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya pūrvāntacaryānusmaraṇasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / cyutyupapādābhijñā katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya sattvānāṃ cyutyupapādaprakāra saṃdarśanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / āsravakṣayābhijñā katamā / dhyānaṃ niśritya āsravakṣayajñānasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# sngon gyi mtha'i spyod pa rjes su dran pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / 'chi 'pho dang skye ba mngon par shes pa gang zhe na / / sems can rnams kyi 'chi 'pho dang skye ba mthong ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / zag pa zad pa mngon par shes pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas zag pa zad pa shes pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
lakṣaṇānuvyañjanāni katamāni / dhyānaṃ niśritya lakṣaṇānuvyañjanairvibhrājamānasandarśanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayūktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ tatsamutthitavipākāśca / pariśuddhayaḥ katamāḥ
# mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnams gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos brgyan pa'i sku kun tu ston pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams dang de las byung ba'i rnam par smin pa'o /
catasraḥ pariśuddhayaḥ / āśrayapariśuddhiḥ katamāḥ / dhyānaṃ niśritya yathākāmamaśrayasyopādāne sthānaparityāgānāṃ samṛddhau yaḥ samādhīḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / ālambanapariśuddhiḥ katamā
# gnas yongs su dag pa gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas / / ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gnas len pa dang bzhugs pa dang; yongs su gtong ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / dmigs pa yongs su dag pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya yathākāmamālambananirmāṇapariṇāmanajñānānāṃ samṛddhau yaḥ samādhi prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / cittapariśuddhiḥ katamā
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du dmigs pa sprul pa dang sgyur ba mkhyen pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / thugs yongs su dag par gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya yathākāmaṃ samādhimukhavaśavarttisamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / jñānapariśuddhiḥ katamā
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo la dbang sgyur ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / mkhyen pa yongs su dag pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya yathākāmaṃ dhāraṇīmukhasandhāraṇasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# bsam gtan la brten nas ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gzungs kyi sgo kun tu 'dzin pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
balāni katamāni / baśa tathāgatabalāni / sthānāsthānabalaṃ katamat dhyānaṃ niśritya sarvaprakāra sthānāsthānajñānasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# gnas dang gnas ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs gang zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas gnas dang gnas ma yin pa thams cad mkhyen pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
karmasvakajñānabalaṃ katamat
# las bdag gir bya ba mkhyen pa'i stobs gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya sarvaprakāra karmasvakajñānasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# las bdag gir bya ba rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
śiṣṭāni balāni yathāyogaṃ veditavyāni / vaiśāradyāni katamāni
# stobs lhag ma rnams la yang de bzhin du ji ltar mthun du rig par bya'o /
catvāri vaiśāradyāni / abhisaṃbodhivaiśāradyaṃ katamat
# mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa la mi 'jigs pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya svārthamevārabhya sarvākārajñeyābhisaṃbodhipratijñāpratiṣṭhāpanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# bsam gtan la brten nas rang gi don las brtsams te / / shes bya rnam pa thams cad mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par zhal gyis 'che ba 'jog pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
āsravakṣayavaiśāradyaṃ katamat
# zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa la mi 'jigs pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya svārthamevārabhya sarvākārasravakṣayapratijñā pratiṣṭhāpanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / antarāyikadharmavaiśāradyaṃ katamat
# rang gi don las brtsams te / / zag pa'i rnam pa thams cad zad par zhal gyis 'che ba 'jog pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / bar du gcod pa'i chos la mi 'jigs pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya parārthamārabhya sarvākārāntarāyikadharmapratijñāpratiṣṭhāpanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / nairyāṇikapratipadavaiśāradyaṃ katamat
# gzhan gyi don las brtsams te / / bar du gcod pa'i chos rnam pa thams cad ston par zhal gyis 'che ba 'jog pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / nges par 'byin pa'i lam la mi 'jigs pa gang zhe na /
dhyānaṃ niśritya parārthamārabhya sarvākāra nairyāṇikamārgadharma pratijñāpratiṣṭhāpanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# bsam gtan la brten nas gzhan gyi don las brtsams te / / nges par 'byin pa'i lam gyi rnam pa thams cad ston par zhal gyis 'che ba 'jog pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
smṛtyupasthānāni katamāni
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa gsum gang zhe na /
trīṇyeva smṛtyupasthānāni
# tshogs yongs su sdud pa ste /
gaṇaparikarṣaṇe sarvākārasaṃkleśāsamudācārasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ purvavat
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa thams cad kun tu mi 'byung ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
arakṣāṇi katamāni / trīṇyeravārakṣāṇi
# bsrung ba med pa rnam pa gsum gang zhe na /
gaṇaparikarṣaṇe yathākāmamavavādānuśāsanīprayogasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# tshogs yongs su sdud pa nyid la ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gdams pa dang rjes su bstan par sbyor ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
asaṃpramoṣadharmatā katamā
# bsnyel ba mi mnga' ba'i chos nyid gang zhe na /
sarvākārasya yathāvat kṛtassa bhāṣitasya cābhilapanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# ji lta ba bzhin du mdzad pa dang gsungs pa'i rnam pa thams cad mngon par brjod pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
vāsanāsamudghātaḥ katamaḥ
# bag chags legs par bcom pa gang zhe na /
sarvajñasya sataḥ asarvajñaceṣṭitāsamudācārasamṛddau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / mahākaruṇā katamā / nirantaraṃ sarvaprakāraduḥkhālambanakaruṇāvihārasamṛddau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# thams cad mkhyen par gyur pas / / thams cad mkhyen pa ma yin pa'i g yo ba kun tu mi 'byung ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no / / thugs rje chen po gang zhe na / / rgyun mi 'chad par sdug bsngal la dmigs pa'i thugs rje la gnas pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
āveṇikā buddhadharmāḥ katame
# sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams gang zhe na /
aṣṭādaśāveṇikā buddhadharmāḥ / asādhāraṇa kāyavāṅganaskarthapariśuddhi samṛddau sāśrayāṇāṃ saphalānāṃ tathāgatendriyāṇamaprāptyāmaparihāṇisamṛddhau asādhāraṇa karmasamudācārasamṛddhau asādhāraṇajñānavihārasamṛddhau ca yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi phrin las thun mong ma yin pa yongs su dag pa yang dag par 'byor ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbang po gnas dang 'bras bu dang bcas pa rnams ma thob pa'i yongs su nyams pa med pa yang dag par 'byor ba dang thun mong ma yin pa'i phrin las mdzad pa yang dag par 'byor ba dang ye shes la gnas pa thun mong ma yin pa yin pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
sarvākārajñatā katamā
# rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gang zhe na /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ sarvākārajñatāsamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ / eteṣāṃ guṇānamabhinirhāraḥ katamaḥ / viśuddhāni catvāri dhyānāni niśritya anyatīrthīyaḥ śrāvako bodhisattvo vā abhinirharati catvāri apramāṇānyevaṃ pañcābhijñāḥ
# phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yang dag par 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gang yin pa dang; de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so / / yon tan 'di rnams ji ltar mngon par bsgrub ce na / / phyi rol pa'am / / nyan thos sam / / byang chub sems dpa' yang rung ste / / dag pa'i bsam gtan bzhi la brten nas / / tshad med pa rnams mngon par bsgrub po / / tshad med pa rnams ji lta bar mngon par shes pa lnga yang de bzhin no / / yon tan lhag ma rnams ni nyan thos sam / / byang chub sems dpa'am /
śeṣān guṇān prāntakoṭikaṃ caturthaṃ dhyānaṃ niśritya śrāvako bodhisattvastathāgato vābhinirharati
# de bzhin gshes pa yang rung ste / / rab kyi mthar phyin pa'i bsam gtan bzhi pa la brten nas mngon par bsgrub bo /
tatpunaḥ kimupādāya / dhyānasanniśrayeṇa yathāvyavasthānamanasikāravahulīkāratāmupādāya
# de yang ci'i phyir zhe na / / bsam gtan la brten nas ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa bzhin du lan mang du yid la byed pa'i phyir ro /
ta ete guṇā dvividhāḥ
# yon tan 'di dag ni rnam pa gnyis te /
svakāritrapratyupasthānāśca vaihārikāśca
# rang gi bya ba la nye bar gnas pa dang gnas pa las gyur ba'o /
ye svakāritrapratyupasthānāḥ te lokottarapṛṣṭhalabdhāḥ saṃvṛtijñānasvabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ
# rang gi bya ba la nye bar gnas pa gang yin pa de dag ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes la thob pa kun rdzob shes pa'i rang bzhin du blta'o /
ye punarvaihārikāste lokottarajñānasvabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ / apramāṇaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# gnas pa las gyur pa gang yin pa de dag ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes kyi rang bzhin du blta'o / / tshad med pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
vipakṣaṃ jahāti
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs spong ngo /
anukampāvihāritayā puṇya saṃbhāraṃ paripūrayati sattvaparipāke ca na parikhidyate / vimokṣaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# thugs brtse bar gnas pas bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par mdzad do / / sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa la mi skye'o; / / rnam par thar pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
nirmāṇakarmābhinirharati
# sprul pa'i las mngon par bsgrub bo /
śubhanirmāṇe na saṃkliśyate śānteṣu vimokṣeṣu na sajjati / paramapraśāntena cāryavihāreṇa viharati
# dge ba sprul pa la kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ro / / zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa rnams la mi chags so /
adhimucyanatā mupādāya / abhibhvāyatanaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti / trayāṇāṃ vimokṣāṇāmālambanaṃ vaśe varttayatyālambanābhibhavanatāmupādāya
# mos pa'i phyir 'phags pa'i gnas pa mchog tu rab tu zhi ba'i gnas pas gnas so / / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / dmigs pa zil gyis gnon pa'i phyir rnam par thar pa gsum po dag gi dmigs pa la dbang sgyur bar mdzad do /
kṛtsnāyatanaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# zad par gyi skye mched rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
vimokṣālambanaṃ pariniṣpādayati kṛtsnaspharaṇatāmupādāya
# zad par rgyas par mdzad pa'i phyir rnam par thar pa'i dmigs pa yongs su bsgrub par mdzad do /
araṇayā kiṃ karma karoti
# nyon mongs pa med pas las ci mdzad ce na /
ādeyavacano bhavati / praṇidhijñānena kiṃ karma karoti
# gzung ba'i tshig tu 'gyur ro / / bsams nas shes pas las ci mdzad ce na /
bhūtabhavyavarttamānaṃ vyākaroti bahumataśca bhavati lokasya
# byung ba dang 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang da ltar gyi lung ston pa dang 'ji rten na mang pos bkur bar 'gyur ro /
pratisaṃvidbhiḥ kiṃ karma  karoti
# so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
deśanayā sattvacittāni saṃtoṣayati
# bshad pas sems can rnams kyi sems tshim par mdzad do /
abhijñābhiḥ kiṃ karma karoti / śāsane kāyakarmaṇā āvarjayati
# mngon par shes pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / lus kyi las kyis bstan pa la 'dun par mdzad do / / ngag gi las kyis 'dun par mdzad do /
vākkarmaṇā cittādeśanayāvarjayati sattvacaritaṃ ca jñātvā āgatiṃ ca gatiṃ ca niḥsaraṇe sattvān yathāvadavavadate
# sems kun brjod pas kyang 'dun par mdzad do / / sems can gyi spyod pa dang 'ong ba dang 'gro ba mkhyen pas sems can rnams nges par 'byung ba la ji lta ba bzhin du 'doms so /
lakṣaṇānuvyañjanaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# mtshan nyid dpe byed bzang po rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
darśanamātrakeṇa mahāpuruṣatve saṃpratyayaṃ janayati cittānyabhiprasādayati
# mthong ma thag tu skyes bu chen po nyid du yid ces par mdzad do / / sems kyang mngon par dang bar mdzad do /
pariśuddhibhiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# yongs su dag pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
saṃcintya bhavopapattiṃ parigṛṇhāti
# bsams bzhin du srid par skye ba yongs su 'dzin to /
ākāṅkṣayankalpaṃ vā kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā tiṣṭhati āyuḥsaṃskārān vā utsṛjati
# bzhed nas bskal pa'am bskal pa las lhag par bzhugs so / / tshe'i 'du byed kyang 'dor ro /
dharmavaśavarttī bhavati samādhivaśavartī saddharmaṃ ca sandhārayati / balaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti / ahetuviṣamahetuvādaṃ pratyākhāyākṛtābhyāgamavāde ca samyaga bhyudayamārgaṃ deśayati sattvacittacaritāni cānupraviśya deśanābhājanatāṃ cāśayaṃ cānuśayaṃ cālambanaṃ ca saṃbhāraṃ ca bhavyatāṃ ca niḥsaraṇaṃ ca yathāvanniḥśreyasamārgaṃ deśayati
# chos la dbang sgyur ro / / ting nge 'dzin la dbang sgyur ro / / dam pa'i chos kyang yang dag par 'dzin to / / stobs rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa rgyur smra ba dang ma byas pa dang phrad par smra ba bsal nas yang dag par mngon par mtho ba'i las ston to / / sems can gyi sems kyi spyod pa dang bshad pa'i snod dang; bsam pa dang bag la nyal dang dmigs pa dang tshogs dang 'os su 'gyur pa dang nges par 'byung ba yang rjes su rtogs nas ji lta ba bzhin du nges par legs pa'i lam ston to /
sarvamārāṃśca nigṛṇhāti sarvatra ca praśnaṃ pṛcchati pṛṣṭo vyākaroti / vaiśāradyaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# bdud thams cad kyang tshar gcod do / / thams cad du dri ba dris pa yang lung ston to / / mi 'jigs pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
parṣadi samyagātmanaḥ śāstṛtvaṃ vyavasthāpahati codakāṃścānyatīrthyānnigṛṇhāti / smṛtyupasthānaiḥ kiṃ karma gaṇamavavadate samanuśāsti
# 'khor gyi nang du bdag ston pa yang dag pa yin par rnam par 'jog go / / rgol ba gzhan mu stegs can rnams kyang tshar gcod do / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / kun nas nyon mongs pa can ma yin pas tshogs yongs su sdud do /
asaṃmoṣadharmatayā kiṃ karma karoti / buddhakṛtyaṃ na hāpayati / vāsanāsamudghātena kiṃ karma karoti / niḥkleśaḥ kleśapratirūpāṃ ceṣṭānnadarśayati / mahākaruṇayā kiṃ karma karoti
# bsrung ba med pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / rgyun mi 'chad par tshogs la 'doms so / / yang dag par rjes su ston to / / bsnyel ba med pa'i chos nyid kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mi 'dor ro / / bag chags legs par bcom pas las ci mdzad ce na / / nyon mongs pa med pas nyon mongs pa lta bu'i spyod pa mi ston to / / thugs rje chen pos las ci mdzad ce na /
ṣaṭkṛtvo rātriṃdivasena lokaṃ vyavalokayati
# nyin mtshan lan drug tu 'jig rten la rnam par gzigs so /
āveṇikairbuddhadharmaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti
# sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kyis las ci mdzad ce na /
sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhān kāyavāṅmanaskarmapariśuddhyā prāptyā cāreṇa vihāreṇa vābhibhavati
# sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi phrin las yongs su dag pa dang 'thob pa dang gshegs pa dang bzhugs pas kyang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad zil gyis gnon to /
sarvākārajñatayā kiṃ karma karoti / sarvasattvānāṃ sarvasaṃśayāṃ śchinatti dharmanetrīñca dīrghakālamavasthāpayati yena paripakṣā ? kṣyāḥ sattvāḥ paripacyante paripakāśca vimucyante
# rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis las ci mdzad ce na / / sems can thams cad kyi the tshom gcod do / / chos kyi tshul yang yun ring du 'jog go / / des sems can yongs su ma smin pa rnams ni smin par mdzad do; / / yongs su smin pa rnams ni rnam par grol bar mdzad do /
eṣvabhisamayeṣūttarottaraṃ viśiṣṭaṃ mārgaṃ labhamānaḥ pūrvakaṃ hīnaṃ mārgaṃ vijahāti saṃkalanaprahāṇaṃ ca sākṣātkaroti
# mngon par rtogs pa 'di dag la gong nas gong du khyad par du 'phags pa'i lam thob na lam snga ma dman pa ni 'dor ro / / bsdoms te spong ba yang mngon sum du byed do /
nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau śrāvakaḥ sarvammārgasamavasargavihānyā vijahāti no tu bodhisattvaḥ / ataeva bodhisattvā akṣayakuśalamūlā akṣayaguṇā ityucyante
# phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su nyan thos ni lam thams cad rgyun yang dag par gcod pa'i rnam par 'dor bas rnams par spong ste / / byang chub sems dpa' ni ma yin no / / de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa dang yon tan mi zad pa zhes kyang bya'o /
yānyavyākṛtavastūni vyavasthāpitāni kimupādāya / ayoniśaḥparipraśna tāmupādāya
# lung du mi ston pa'i dngos po gang dag rnam par gzhag pa ci'i phyir zhe na / / tshul bzhin ma yin pa yongs su 'dri ba'i phyir ro /
ayoniśaḥ paripraśnatā kimupādāya
# ci'i phyir tshul bzhin ma yin pa yongs su 'dri zhe na /
hetuphalasaṃkleśavyavadānacintāpasrivarjanatāmupādāya
# rgyu dang 'bras bu dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba la sems pa yongs su spangs pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena bodhisattvo bodhimanava vadyāmavakrāntaḥ strotāpanno na bhavati / strotaḥpratipattyapariniṣpannatāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa la zhugs na / / rgyun tu zhugs par mi 'gyur zhe na / / rgyun la 'jug pa yongs su ma grub pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena sakṛdāgāmī na bhavati / apramāṇasaṃcintya bhavopaprattiparigrahatāmupādāya
# ci'i phyir lan cig phyir 'ong bar mi 'gyur zhe na / / bsams bzhin du srid par skye ba tshad med pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇenānāgāmī na bhavati
# ci'i phyir phyir mi 'ong bar mi 'gyur zhe na /
dhyānairvihṛtya kāmadhātāvupapadyānatāmupādāya
# bsam gtan rnams kyis gnas shing 'dod pa'i khams su skye ba'i phyir ro /
bodhisattvaḥ satyānyabhi samayena labdhvā daśasu mūmiṣu bhāvanāmārgeṇa jñeyāvaraṇapratipakṣamārgaṃ bhāvayati na kleśāvaraṇapratipakṣamārgam
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bden pa rnams mngon par rtogs par byas nas / / sa bcu rnams su bsgom pa'i lam la shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po'i lam sgom gyi nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po ni ma yin te /
tathā ca bodhiprāptaḥ kleśāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaṃ ca vijahāti arhan tathāgataśca saṃpadyate
# de byang chub thob pa na nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa cig car spong ngo / / cig car dgra bcom pa dang de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur ro /
sa ca bodhisattvaḥ sarvakleśāprahāṇāt mantroṣadhayo viṣamiva sarvakleśān abhibhavati sarvān kleśān doṣāṃśca notpādayati sarvāsu bhūmiṣu arhanniva kleśān prajahāti
# de nyon mongs pa ma spangs su zin kyang / / sngags dang sman gyis song ba'i dug lta bu dang dper na spangs pa'i dgra bcom pa ltar sa thams cad du nyon mongs pa'i nyes pa mi skyed do; /
api khalu bodhisattvo jñeyeṣu bhāvanākuśalo bhavati upāyeṣu bhāvanākuśalo bhavati abhūtaparikalpeṣu bhāvanākuśalo bhavati nirvikalpeṣu bhāvanākuśalo bhavati tena kālena kālamindriyāṇyuttāpayati
# yang byang chub sems dpa' shes bya la mkhas pa dang thams la mkhas pa dang yang dag pa ma yin par rnam par rtog pa la mkhas pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa la mkhas par bya'o / / dus dus su dbang po rnams sbyang bar bya'o /
jñeyaṃ katamat
# shes bya gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepeṇa ṣaḍvidham
# de yang rnam pa drug tu blta ste /
bhrāntiḥ bhrāntyāśrayaḥ abhrāntyāśrayaḥ bhrāntyabhrāntiḥ abhrāntiḥ abhrāntiniṣyandaśca
# 'khrul pa dang 'khrul pa'i gnas dang ma 'khrul pa'i gnas dang 'khrul pa yang ma yin la ma 'khrul pa yang yin pa dang ma 'khrul pa dang na 'khrul pa'i rgyu mthun pa'o /
upāyakauśalyaṃ katamat / saṃkṣeparāścaturvidham / sattvaparipākakauśalyaṃ buddhadharmaparipuraṇakauśalyaṃ kṣiprābhijñākauśalyaṃ mārgānupacchedakauśalyaṃ ca
# thabs la mkhas pa gang zhe na / / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba la mkhas pa dang sangs rgyas kyis chos yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la mkhas pa dang mngon par shes pa myur ba la mkhas pa dang lam rgyun mi 'chad pa la mkhas pa'o /
abhūtaparikalpaḥ katamaḥ
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepato daśavidhaḥ / mūlavikalpaḥ nimittivikalpaḥ nimittapratibhāsavikalpaḥ nimittavikāravikalpaḥ nimittipratibhāsavikāravikalpaḥ paropanītavikalpaḥ ayoniśovikalpaḥ yoniśovikalpaḥ abhiniveśavikalpaḥ vikṣepavikalpaśca
# rtsa ba'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshan ma'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshan mar snang ba'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshan mar 'gyur ba'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshan mar snang ba 'gyur ba'i rnam par rtog pa dang gzhan gyis bstan pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang tshul bzhin gyi rnam par rtog pa dang mngon par zhen pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang rnam par g yeng ba'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
sa punaḥ daśavidhaḥ / abhāvavikalpa bhāvavikalpaḥ samāropavikalpaḥ apavādavikalpaḥ ekatvavi kalpaḥ pṛthaktvavikalpaḥ svabhāvavikalpaḥ viśeṣavikalpaḥ yathānāmārthavikalpaḥ yathārthanāmavikalpaśca
# rnam par g yeng ba'i rnam par rtog pa yang dngos po med par rnam par rtog pa dang dngos por rnam par rtog pa dang sgro 'dogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang gcig pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa dang tha dad pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa dang ngo bo nyid du rnam par rtog pa dang khyad par du rnam par rtog pa dang ming ji lta ba bzhin du don du rnam par rtog pa dang don du ji lta ba bzhin du ming du rnam par rtog pa'o /
nirvikalpatā katamā
# rnam par mi rtog pa nyid gang zhe na /
samāsatastrividhā / santuṣṭinirvikalpatā aviparyāsanirghikalpatā niṣprapañcanirvikalpatā ca / tā imāstitraḥ pṛthagjanaśrāvakabodhisattvānāṃ yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ
# chog par 'dzin pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid dang phyin ci ma log pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid dang spros pa med pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid de / / so so'i skye bo rnams dang nyan thos rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang go rims bzhin no; /
yāsau nimittato niṣprapañcanirvikalpatā tasyāḥ punaḥ abhāvasya pañca nimittāni
# spros pa med pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid yid la byed pa med pas ma yin / / yang dag par 'das pas ma yin / / rnam par zhi bas ma yin /
na amanasikārataḥ na manasikārasamatikramataḥ na vyupaśamataḥ na svabhāvataḥ na ālambane 'bhisaṃskārataśca / api khalu ālaṃbane 'nabhisaṃskārataḥ
# ngo bo nyid kyis ma yin / / dmigs pa las mngon par 'du byed pas ma yin par blta ste / / 'on kyang dmigs pa la mngon par 'du byed pa med par blta'o /
bodhisattvaḥ prakṛtyā tīkṣṇendriyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ indriyāpyuttāpayatīti / tīkṣṇamṛdvindriyamāśritya tīkṣṇamadhyendriyamabhinirharati / punaḥ tīkṣṇamadhyendriyamāśritya tīkṣṇatīkṣṇendriyamabhinirharati / iti abhidharmasamuccaye prāptiviniścayo nāma caturthaḥ samuccayaḥ
# byang chub sems dpa' ni rang bzhin gyis dbang po rnon po yin na / / ji ltar dbang po rnams sbyong zhe na / / dbang po rnon po chung ngu la brten te rnon po 'bring mngon par bsgrub bo / / dbang po rnon po 'bring la brten te rnon po'i chen po mngon par bsgrub po / / 'thob pa rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba ste /
atha mahāyānabhidharmasamuccayaśāstre viniścayabhāge sāṃkathyaparicchedaścaturthaḥ / sāṃkathyaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / saṃkṣepataḥ saptavidhaḥ / arthaviniścayaḥ vyākhyāviniścayaḥ prabhidyasaṃdarśanaviniścayaḥ saṃpraśnaviniścayaḥ saṃgrahaviniścayaḥ vādaviniścayaḥ abhisandhiviniścayaśca / arthaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / yatra ṣaḍarthānārabhya viniścayo bhavati / katame  ṣaḍarthāḥ / svabhāvārthaḥ hetvarthaḥ phalārthaḥ karmārthaḥ yogārthaḥ vṛttyarthaśca / svabhāvārthastraṃyaḥ svabhāvāḥ
# kun las btus pa bzhi pa'o / / 'brel pa'i gtam gyis rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / rnam pa bdun te / / don rnam par nges pa dang rnam par bshad pa rnam par nges pa dang rab tu phye nas kun tu bstan pa rnam par nges pa dang yang dag par dri ba rnam par nges pa dang bsdu ba rnam par nges pa dang smra ba rnams par nges pa dang ldem po rung dgongs pa rnam par nges pa'o / / don rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / don drug las brtsams nas gang rnam par nges pa'o / / don drug gang zhe na / / ngo bo nyid kyi don dang rgyu'i don dang 'bras bu'i don dang las kyi don dang ldan pa'i don dang 'jug pa'i don to / / ngo bo nyid kyi don ni ngo bo nyid gsum mo /
hetvarthastrayo hetavaḥ / utpattihetuḥ pravṛttihetuḥ siddhihetuśca / phalārthaḥ pañcaphalāni / vipākaphalaṃ niṣyandaphalaṃ adhipatiphalaṃ puruṣakāraphalaṃ visaṃyogaphalaṃ ca / karmārthaḥ pañca karmāṇi / upalabdhikarma kāritrakarma vyāvasāyakarma pariṇatikarma prāptikarma ca
# rgyu'i don ni skye ba dang 'byung ba dang 'grub pa'i rgyu'o / / 'bras bu'i don ni rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu dang rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu dang bdag po'i 'bras bu dang skyes bu byed pa'i 'bras bu dang bral ba'i 'bras bu'o / / las kyi don ni dmigs pa'i las dang byed pa'i las dang 'bad pa'i las dang sgyur ba'i las dang 'thob pa'i las so /
yogārthaḥ pañca yogāḥ / sāmūhiko yogaḥ ānubandhiko yogaḥ sāṃbandhiko yogaḥ āvasthiko yogaḥ vaikāriko yogaśca
# ldan pa'i don ni mang po las gyur pa dang rjes su 'ching ba las gyur pa dang 'brel pa las gyur pa dang gnas skabs las gyur pa dang 'gyur ba las gyur pa'i ldan pa'o /
vṛttyarthaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ / lakṣaṇavṛttiḥ avasthānavṛttiḥ viparyāsavṛttiḥ aviparyāsavṛttiḥ prabhedavṛttiśca
# 'jug pa'i don ni mtshan nyid kyi 'jug pa dang rten la 'jug pa dang phyin ci log gi 'jug pa dang phyin ci log ma yin pa'i 'jug pa dang rab tu dbye ba'i 'jug pa'o /
vyākhyāviniścayaḥ katamaḥ
# rnam par bshad pa rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
yena sūtrāntān vyācaṣṭe / sa punaḥ katamaḥ
# gang gis mdo sde rnams rnam par bshad par byed pa ste / / de yang gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepeṇa ṣaḍvidhaḥ / parijñeyavastu parijñeyo 'rthaḥ parijñopaniṣad parijñā parijñāphalam tatpravedanā ca / api khalu caturdaśa mukhāni vyākhyāviniścayasya
# yongs su shes par bya ba'i dngos po dang yongs su shes par bya ba'i don dang yongs su shes par bya ba'i rgyu dang yongs su shes pa dang yongs su shes pa'i 'bras bu dang de rab tu shes pa'o / / yang rnam par bshad pa'i sgo bcu bzhi ste /
katamāni caturdaśa / vyākhyāsaṃgrahamukham vastusaṃgrahamukham aṅgopāṅgamukham uggarottaranirhāramukham pratikṣepamukham akṣarapariṇāmamukham nāśānāśamukham pudgalavyavasthānamukham prabhedavyavasthānamukham nayamukham parijñādimukham balā balamukham pratyāhāramukham abhinirhāramukhaṃ ca
# bcu bzhi ni rnam par bshad pa'i bsdu ba'i sgo dang dngos po bsdu ba'i sgo dang yan lag dang nye ba'i yan lag gi sgo dang gong nas gong du mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo dang spong ba'i sgo dang yi ge yongs su bsgyur ba'i sgo dang chud za ba dang chud mi za ba'i sgo dang gang zag rnam par gzhag pa'i sgo dang rab tu dbye ba rnam par gzhag pa'i sgo dang tshul gyi sgo dang; yongs su shes pa la sogs pa'i sgo dang stobs dang stobs ma yin pa'i sgo dang bzlos te brjod pa'i sgo dang mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo'o /
prabhidyasaṃdarśanaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ
# rab tu phye nas kun tu bstan pa gtan la dbab pa gang zhe na /
yathānirdiṣṭeṣu skandhādiṣu dharmeṣu yathāyogamekāvacarakaḥ pūrvapadakaḥ paścātpadakaḥ dvikoṭikaḥ trikoṭikaḥ catuṣkoṭikaḥ oṃkāritaḥ prātikṣepika ityevamādayaḥ
# ji skad du bstan pa'i chos rnams la ci rigs su sbyar te / / gcig nas rtogs pa dang tshig gong ma dang sbyor ba dang tshig 'og ma dang sbyor ba dang mu gnyis pa dang mu gsum pa dang mu bzhi pa dang de bzhin no zhes bya ba dang spong ba'o /
saṃpraśnaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ
# yang dag par 'dri ba rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
aṣṭākārakāyadeśena aṣṭākārayāyadeśane ca  praśnavyākaraṇena sarvasatyamithyā viniścayaḥ / api khalu catvāraḥ saṃpraśna viniścayamārgāḥ
# rnam par brgyad de / / ci zhes bstan pa yang dag par 'dri ba rnam par nges pa dang ci zhes bstan pa la ji lta bar gang zhes bstan pa la yang de bzhin no / / yang rnam par nges pa'i lam bzhi ste /
dūṣakaḥ pratiṣṭhāpakaḥ chedakaḥ bodhakaśca / saṃgrahaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / daśabhiḥ sthānaiḥ saṃgṛhīto viniścayaḥ / katamāni daśa sthānāni / kṛtyānuṣṭhānaviniścayasthānam avatāraviniścayasthānam adhimuktiviniścayasthānam yuktiviniścayasthānam sāṃkathyaviniścayasthānam prativedhaviniścayasthānam viśuddhiviniścayasthānam abhinirhārapadaprabhedaviniścayasthānam anābhogābhogamātrasarvārthasiddhiviniścayasthānaṃ ca / vādaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ
# sun 'byin par byed pa dang sgrub par byed pa dang gcod par byed pa dang khong du chud par byed pa'o / / bsdu ba rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / gnas bcus rnam par nges pa bsdus par 'gyur te / / gnas bcu gang zhe na / / bya ba bsgrub pa rnam par nges pa dang 'jug pa rnam par nges pa dang mos pa rnam par nges pa dang rigs pas rnam par nges pas dang 'phel ba'i gtam gyis rnam par nges pa dang rab tu rtog pas rnam par nges pa dang rnam par dag pas rnam par nges pa dang mngon par bsgrubs pas rnam par nges pa dang tshig rab tu dbye bas rnam par nges pa dang lhun gyis grub pa dang rtsol ba tsam gyis don thams cad bsgrub pa rnam par nges pa'o / / smra ba rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepataḥ saptavidhaḥ / vādaḥ vādādhikaraṇaṃ vādādhiṣṭhānaṃ bādālaṃkāraḥ vādanigrahaḥ vādaniḥsaraṇaṃ bāde bahukarā dharmāśca
# smra ba dang smra ba'i zhal che ba dang smra ba'i gzhi dang smra ba'i rgyan dang smra ba chad pas bcad pa dang smra ba las 'byung ba dang smra ba la gces spras byed pa'i chos rnams so /
prathamo vādaḥ punaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ / vādaḥ pravādaḥ vivādaḥ apavādaḥ anuvāda avavāśca
# smra ba gang zhe na / / smra ba dang rmad khyer ba smra ba dang rtsod pa smra ba dang tshig ngan smra ba dang mthun par smra ba dang gdams pa smra ba'o /
vādaḥ sarvalokavacanam
# smra ba ni tshig brjod pa thams cad do /
pravādaḥ lokānuśruto vādaḥ / lokajñānapravādataḥ
# rmad khyer ba smra ba ni 'jig rten na grags pa'o /
vivādaḥ parasparaṃ viruddhayorvāde 'vasthānam
# rtsod pa smra ba ni phan tshun mi mthun par gnas pa'o /
apavādaḥ parasparaṃ kopasaṃrambhapāruṣyanacanam
# tshig ngan smra ba ni phan tshul tshig rlung pos nye bar gnas pa'o /
anuvādaḥ viśuddhajñānadarśanānukūlaḥ sāṃkathyaviniścayaḥ
# mthun par smra ba ni ye shes mthong ba rnam par dag pa dang mthun pa'i 'brel ba'i gtam rnam par nges pa'o; /
avavādaḥ sattvānāṃ asamāhitacittānāṃ cittasamādhānāya samāhitacittānāṃ vimokṣalābhāya deśanāvādaḥ
# gdams pa smra ba ni sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa mnyam par gzhag par bya ba dang sems mnyam par gzhag pa rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir bstan pa'o /
dvitīyaṃ vādādhikaraṇaṃ rājakulaṃ vā prajākulaṃ vā prāmāṇikānāṃ sahāyakānāṃ dharmārthakuśalānāṃ śramaṇabrāhmaṇānāṃ nādasabhā vā / tṛtīyaṃ vādādhiṣṭhānaṃ yadadhiṣṭhāya vādaḥ kriyate
# smra ba'i zhal che ba ni rgyal po bzhugs pa dang bskos pa 'du ba'i sa dang 'dus pa dang; tshad mar rung ba'i zla grogs rnams dang dge sbyong dang bram ze chos dang don la mkhas pa rnams so /
saṃkṣepato dvividham / sādhyaṃ sādhanaṃ ca
# smra ba'i gzhi ni bsgrub pa dang sgrub pa'o /
sādhyaṃ dvividham / svabhāvo viśeṣaśca
# bsgrub pa ni ngo bo nyid dang khyad par ro /
sādhanāni aṣṭau / pratijñā hetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ upanayaḥ nigamanaṃ pratyakṣaṃ anumānaṃ āptāgamaśca
# sgrub pa ni dam bca' ba dang gtan tshigs dang dpe dang nye bar sbyar ba dang mjug sdud pa dang mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa dang yid ches pa'i lung ngo /
sādhyasya svabhāvaḥ ātmasvabhāvo dharmasvabhāvo vā / viśeṣaḥ ātmaviśeṣo dharmaviśeṣo vā / pratijñā sādhyasya svarucitārthasya parasaṃprāpaṇavijñāpanā
# ngo bo nyid bsgrub pa ni bdag gi ngo bo nyid dang chos kyi ngo bo nyid do / / khyad par ni bdag gi khyad par dang chos kyi khyad par ro / / dam bca' ba ni bdag 'dod pa bsgrub pa'i don gzhan la go bar ston pa'o /
hetuḥ tasminneva sādhye apratītasyārthasya saṃpratyayanimittaṃ pratyakṣopalambhānupalambhasamākhyānam
# gtan tshigs ni bsgrub pa de nyid la ma grags pa'i don yid ches par byed pa'i rgyu mngon sum du dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa bsnyad pa'o /
dṛṣṭānta dṛṣṭa antena adṛṣṭāsya antasya samīkaraṇasamākhyānam
# dpe ni mtha' mthong ba dang mtha' ma mthong ba mtshungs par sbyar zhing bsnyad pa'o /
upanayaḥ śiṣṭatajjātīya rmmāpagamāya nayatvasamākhyānam
# nye bar sbyar ba ni de'i rigs kyi chos lhag ma de dang 'dra ba la de'i chos sbyar ba'i tshul gyis mthun par bsnyad pa'o /
nigamanaṃ niṣṭhāgamanasamākhyānam
# mjug sdud pa ni mthar phyin par bsnyad pa'o /
prasvasatprakāśābhrānto 'rthaḥ
# mngon sum ni rang gi don yod cing snang la ma nor ba'o /
anumānaṃ pratyakṣaśiṣṭasaṃpratyayaḥ
# rjes su dpag pa ni mngon sum gyi lhag ma la yid ches pa'o /
āptāgamaḥ taduviruddhopadeśaḥ
# yid ches pa'i lung ni de gnyi ga dang mi 'gal bar ston pa'o /
caturtho vādālaṃkāraḥ vādādhiṣṭhāne samyagyuktibhiḥ vādasabhāyāṃ gambhīro nipuṇaśca bhavatīti vādālaṃkāra ityucyate / sa punaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ
# smra ba'i rgyan ni bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung lugs shes pa dang tshig zur phyin pa phun sum tshogs pa dang mi 'jigs pa dang brtan pa dang mthun par byed pa'o /
svaparasamayajñatā vākkaraṇasaṃpad vaiśaradyaṃ pratibhānaṃ sthairyaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ ca / pañcamo vādanigrahaḥ kathātyāgaḥ kathāsādaḥ kathādoṣaśca / kathātyāgaḥ svāvādadoṣābhyupagamaḥ paravāaguṇābhyupagamaśca
# smra ba chad pas gcad pa ni gtam rjes gcad pa dang gtam 'phro lus dang gtam gyi nyes pa'o / / gtam rjes gcad pa ni rang gi smra ba'i skyon khas blang ba dang gzhan gyi smra ba'i yon tan khas blang ba'o / / gtam 'phro lus pa ni 'di lta ste /
kathāsādaḥ anyavastupratisaraṇena vyāvṛttiḥ bāhyavastuvacanena mūlaparatijñāparityāgaḥ krodhamadamānamrākṣādi pradarśanaṃ ca / yathoktaṃ sūtre / kathādoṣaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa navavidhaḥ / ākulaṃ saṃrabdham agamakam amitam anarthakam akālam asthiram apradīptam apravaddhaṃ ca
# gzhan nas gzhan du brgyud pa'am / / gtam gzhan smra ba ste / / mdo sde las ji skad 'byung ba lta bu'o / / gtam gyi nyes pa ni cal col dang 'khrugs pa dang brda phrad du mi rung ba dang ran pa ma yin pa dang don dang ldan pa ma yin pa dang dus tshigs ma yin par smra ba dang mi brtan pa dang mi bsal ba dang tshig rgyun chags pa ma yin pa'o /
ṣaṣṭhaṃ vādaniḥsaraṇaṃ guṇadoṣau vicārya vādānniḥsaratyakaraṇena vā prativādityabhājanatāṃ parṣado vaiguṇyamātmano 'kauśalyaṃ ca jñātvā vādaṃ na karoti
# smra ba las 'byung ba ni phyir rgol ba snod ma yin pa dang 'khor yon tan med pa dang bdag kyang mi mkhas par rig nas smra bar mi bya ba dang phyir rgol ba snod du gyur ba zhig gam /
prativādini bhājanatāṃ parṣado guṇavattvamātmanaḥ kauśalyaṃ ca jñātvā vādaṃ karoti / vāde bahukarā dharmāḥ samāsatastrayaḥ
# 'khor yon tan dang ldan nam / / bdag kyang mkhas par rig nas smra bar bya'o / / smra ba la gces spras byed pa'i chos rnams ni bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung lugs la mkhas pa ste /
svaparasamayajñatā yayā sarvatra nipuṇo vādaṃ karoti / vaiśāradyaṃ yena nipuṇaḥ samagraparṣadi vādaṃ karoti / pratimānaṃ yena nipuṇaḥ sarvāṃn kaṭhinān praśnān vyākaroti / api khalu svahitasukha kāmena vādeṣu abhijñātuṃ pravarttitavyaṃ na paraiḥ vivādaṃ kartum / taduktaṃ bhagavatā mahāyānā bhidharmasutre
# des thams cad du smra bar byed do / / mi 'jigs pa ni gang gis 'khor thams cad du smra bar byed pa'o / / spobs pa ni gang gis thams cad du lan gdab pa shes pa'o / / yang dag legs su 'dod pas smra ba'i tshul shes par bya'i brtsad cing smra bar ni mi bya ste / / bcom ldan 'das kyis chos mngon pa'i mdo las ji skad du gsungs pa lta bu ste /
bodhisattvena vīryamārabhamāṇena kuśalapakṣaprayuktena pratipattisārakeṇa dharmānudharmacāriṇā sarvasattvasaṃgrāhakeṇa kṣipramanuttarāṃ samyak saṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyatā dvādaśasthānadharmān samanupaśyatā na paraiḥ saha vivādaḥ kāryaḥ / katame dvādaśa / anuttarārthaparamadharmadeśanāyāṃ saṃpratyayo durlabhaḥ / prāśnikānāmavavādagrāhakaṃ cittaṃ durlabham / sabhyā guṇadoṣavicārakāśca durlabhā / vāde prayuktānāṃ ṣaḍdoṣaviraho durlabhaḥ / katame ṣaṭ / asatpakṣabhiniveśadoṣaḥ kusṛtivacanadoṣaḥ akālikavākkaraṇadoṣaḥ kathāsādadoṣaḥ pārupyavacatadoṣaḥ cittāghātadoṣaśca / vāde saṃrambhābhāvo durlabhaḥ / vāde paracittānurakṣaṇaṃ durlabham / vāde anurakṣaṇe 'pi cittasamādhidurlabhaḥ / vāde cittasya nikārsaparotkarṣakāmatā durlabhā
# gnas bcu gnyis mthong ba'i byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i phyogs la brtson pa nan tan snying por byed pa sems can sdud pa myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas / / gzhan dag dang rtsod pas smra bar mi bya'o / / bcu gnyis gang zhe na / / dam pa'i chos kyi don gyi mchog dang ldan pa bshad pa kun shes pa dkon pa dang kun shes par bya ba'i bsam pas smra ba dkon pa dang tshogs pa mkhas pa dang rtogs pa dang ldan pa rnams dkon pa dang phyogs ngan pa yongs su 'dzin cing mngon par zhen pa'i nyes pa dang ngan g yo smra ba'i nyes pa dang dus ma yin par gtam la sbyor ba'i nyes pa dang gtam khyad du gsod pa'i nyes pa dang tshig brlang po'i nyes pa dang yid 'khrugs pa'i nyes pa dang gang nyes pa rnam pa drug spangs te smra ba dkon pa dang 'khrugs pa med par smra ba dkon pa dang gzhan gyi sems bsrung zhing smra ba dkon pa dang ting nge 'dzin rjes su bsrung zhing smra ba dkon pa dang rgyal ba'am pham pa'i sems med par smra ba dkon pa dang rgyal ba'am pham yang kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dkon pa dang kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa reg par gnas pa dkon pa dang reg par mi gnas pa dge ba'i chos rnams la rgyun du bsgom pa dkon pa dang dge ba'i chos rgyun du mi bsgom pa sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa la mnyam par gzhag pa dang sems mnyam par gzhag pa la rnam par grol ba dkon pa'o zhe'o / / ldem por dgongs pa rnam par nges pa gang zhe na / / ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams kyi don gzhan du brjod la don gzhan du yongs su bsgyur ba ste / / ji skad du pha dang ma ni bsad byas shing / / rgyal po gtsang sbra can gnyis dang / / yul 'khor 'khor dang bcas bcom nas /
nikarṣaparotkarṣayorapi cittasyāsaṃkleśo durlabhaḥ / saṃkliṣṭe tu citte sparśavihāro durlabhaḥ / asparśavihāre tu kuśaladharmabhāvanā durlabhā / nirantaraṃ kuśaladharme 'bhāvite tu asamāhicittasya kṣipraṃ samādhilābhaḥ samāhitacittasya vā kṣipraṃ vimokṣalābho durlabhaḥ / abhisandhiviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / uktādanyo 'rthaḥ / nāmapadavyañjanakāyānāṃ channasyābhisandheḥ anyārthābhivyañjane vipariṇāmaḥ / yathoktaṃ sūtre / mātaraṃ pitaraṃ hatvā rājānaṃ dvau bahuśrutau / rāṣṭraṃ sānucaraṃ hatvā naro viśuddha ucyate / apicoktaṃ sūtre / aśraddho 'kṛtajñaśca sandhicchedī ca yo naraḥ / hatāvakāśo vāntāśaḥ sa vai uttamapuruṣaḥ / punaścoktaṃ sūtre / asāre sāramatayo viparyāse ca susthitāḥ / kleśena ca susaṃkliṣṭā labhante bodhimuttamām / api coktaṃ sūtre bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ pañcabhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgato dānapāra mitāyāṃ kṣipraṃ paripūriṃ labhate / katame pañca / mātsaryadharmatāmanuvṛṃhayati / dānena ca parikhidyate / yācanakaṃ ca dveṣṭi / na kiṃcit kadācid dadāti / dūre ca bhavati dānasya / punaścoktaṃ sūtre / bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ pañcadharmasamanvāgato brahmacārī bhavati parameṇa viśuddhena brahmacaryeṇa samanvāgataḥ
# mi de dag par 'gyur zhes bya / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / yang ji skad du / / yid mi ches dang byas mi gzo / / mi gang khyim 'bigs byed pa dang / / go skabs bcom dang skyugs pa za / / de ni skyes bu mchog yin no / / snying po med pa la snying por shes / / phyin ci log la shin tu gnas / / nyon mongs kun nas rab snyon mongs; / / byang chub dam pa thob par 'gyur / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / yang ji skad du / / byang chub sems dpa' chos lnga dang ldan na / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed de / / lnga gang zhe na; ser sna'i chos nyid 'phel bar byed pa dang sbyin pas yongs su skyo ba dang slong ba la tshig pa za ba dang res 'ga' ci yang sbyin par mi byed pa dang sbyin pa las ring du gyur pa'o / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / yang ji skad du; byang chub sems dpa' chos lnga dang ldan na tshangs par spyod pa yin zhing / / tshangs par spyod pa mchog dang ldan pa ste / / 'khrig pa las gzhan du 'khrig pa las nges par 'byung ba mi tshol ba dang 'khrig pa spang ba la g yel ba dang 'khrig pa'i 'dod chags skyes pa dang du len pa dang 'khrig pa'i gnyen po'i chos kyis skrag pa dang rgyun mi 'chad par gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
katame pañca / nānyatra maithunyānmaithunasya niḥsaraṇaṃ paryeṣate
# chos mngon pa kun las btus pa las / / 'brel ba'i gtam rnam par nges pa kun las btus pa zhes bya ba ste /
maithunaprahāṇenopekṣako bhavati / utpannaṃ ca maithunarogamadhivāsayati
# kun las btus pa lnga pa'o / / bstan bcos 'di ci'i phyir chos mngon pa kun las btus pa zhes bya zhe na /
maithunapratipakṣeṇa ca dharmeṇottrasyati / abhīkṣṇaṃ ca dvayadvayaṃ samāpadyate / kimupādāyedaṃ śāstramabhidharmasamuccaya iti nāma labhate
# rtogs nas bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / kun nas bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / yang dag par mtho ba'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / chos mngon pa kun las btus pa /
saṃkṣepatastribhirarthaiḥ
# slob dpon thogs med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so /
sametyoccayatāmupādāya samantāduccayatāmupādāya samyaguccayatāṃ copādāya
# rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang sh'i lendra bo dhi dang zhu chen gyi lo ts'a ba ban de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o /
